Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yunke Ao, Le Chen, Bruce D. Lee, Assefa S. Wahd, Aline Czarnobai, Philipp Fürnstahl, Bernhard Schölkopf, Andreas Krause
First: 2026-04-20T17:59:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:59:01+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 9 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) has become the predominant algorithm for on-policy reinforcement learning due to its scalability and empirical robustness across domains. However, there is a significant disconnect between the underlying foundations of trust region methods and the heuristic clipped objective used in PPO. In this paper, we bridge this gap by introducing the Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning (BRRL) framework. We formulate a novel regularized and constrained policy optimization problem and derive its analytical optimal solution. We prove that this solution ensures monotonic performance improvement. To handle parameterized policy classes, we develop a policy optimization algorithm called Bounded Policy Optimization (BPO) that minimizes an advantage-weighted divergence between the policy and the analytic optimal solution from BRRL. We further establish a lower bound on the expected performance of the resulting policy in terms of the BPO loss function. Notably, our framework also provides a new theoretical lens to interpret the success of the PPO loss, and connects trust region policy optimization and the Cross-Entropy Method (CEM). We additionally extend BPO to Group-relative BPO (GBPO) for LLM fine-tuning. Empirical evaluations of BPO across MuJoCo, Atari, and complex IsaacLab environments (e.g., Humanoid locomotion), and of GBPO for LLM fine-tuning tasks, demonstrate that BPO and GBPO generally match or outperform PPO and GRPO in stability and final performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有界比率强化学习
近端策略优化（PPO）因其可扩展性和跨领域的经验鲁棒性，已成为同策略强化学习的主导算法。然而，信任域方法的基础理论与PPO中使用的启发式截断目标之间存在显著脱节。本文通过引入有界比率强化学习（BRRL）框架来弥合这一差距。我们构建了一个新颖的正则化约束策略优化问题，并推导出其解析最优解。我们证明该解能确保性能的单调改进。为处理参数化策略类，我们开发了一种名为有界策略优化（BPO）的策略优化算法，该算法最小化策略与BRRL解析最优解之间的优势加权散度。我们进一步基于BPO损失函数建立了所得策略期望性能的下界。值得注意的是，本框架还为解释PPO损失的成功提供了新的理论视角，并连接了信任域策略优化与交叉熵方法（CEM）。我们还将BPO扩展至适用于大语言模型微调的组相对BPO（GBPO）。在MuJoCo、Atari和复杂IsaacLab环境（如人形机器人运动）中对BPO的实证评估，以及在大语言模型微调任务中对GBPO的评估表明，BPO和GBPO在稳定性和最终性能上通常匹配或优于PPO和GRPO。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning (BRRL) to address the theoretical disconnect between trust region methods and the heuristic clipped objective used in Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO). The method formulates a regularized and constrained policy optimization problem, derives its analytical optimal solution that guarantees monotonic improvement, and develops the Bounded Policy Optimization (BPO) algorithm to minimize an advantage-weighted divergence between the policy and this optimal solution. Experimental results show that BPO matches or outperforms PPO in stability and final performance across MuJoCo, Atari, and IsaacLab environments, and its extension, Group-relative BPO (GBPO), achieves similar success in LLM fine-tuning tasks.
本文提出有界比率强化学习（BRRL），以解决近端策略优化（PPO）中信任域方法与其启发式裁剪目标之间的理论脱节问题。该方法构建了一个正则化和约束的策略优化问题，推导出保证单调性能改进的解析最优解，并开发了有界策略优化（BPO）算法，以最小化策略与该最优解之间的优势加权散度。实验结果表明，BPO在MuJoCo、Atari和IsaacLab环境中，在稳定性和最终性能上均匹配或优于PPO，其扩展方法——组相对BPO（GBPO）在大语言模型微调任务中也取得了类似成功。
When Can LLMs Learn to Reason with Weak Supervision?
Authors: Salman Rahman, Jingyan Shen, Anna Mordvina, Hamid Palangi, Saadia Gabriel, Pavel Izmailov
First: 2026-04-20T17:57:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:57:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models have achieved significant reasoning improvements through reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). Yet as model capabilities grow, constructing high-quality reward signals becomes increasingly difficult, making it essential to understand when RLVR can succeed under weaker forms of supervision. We conduct a systematic empirical study across diverse model families and reasoning domains under three weak supervision settings: scarce data, noisy rewards, and self-supervised proxy rewards. We find that generalization is governed by training reward saturation dynamics: models that generalize exhibit a prolonged pre-saturation phase during which training reward and downstream performance climb together, while models that saturate rapidly memorize rather than learn. We identify reasoning faithfulness, defined as the extent to which intermediate steps logically support the final answer, as the pre-RL property that predicts which regime a model falls into, while output diversity alone is uninformative. Motivated by these findings, we disentangle the contributions of continual pre-training and supervised fine-tuning, finding that SFT on explicit reasoning traces is necessary for generalization under weak supervision, while continual pre-training on domain data amplifies the effect. Applied together to Llama3.2-3B-Base, these interventions enable generalization across all three settings where the base model previously failed.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型何时能在弱监督下学会推理？
大语言模型通过可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在推理能力上取得了显著提升。然而，随着模型能力的增强，构建高质量奖励信号变得日益困难，因此理解RLVR在何种弱监督条件下仍能成功至关重要。我们在三种弱监督设置（稀缺数据、噪声奖励、自监督代理奖励）下，对不同模型系列和推理领域进行了系统性实证研究。研究发现，泛化能力受训练奖励饱和动态的支配：能够泛化的模型在训练奖励与下游性能同步提升的预饱和阶段持续时间较长，而快速饱和的模型则倾向于记忆而非学习。我们将推理忠实性（定义为中间步骤对最终答案的逻辑支持程度）确定为预测模型所处机制的关键预强化学习属性，而仅凭输出多样性无法提供有效信息。基于这些发现，我们分离了持续预训练与监督微调的贡献：发现对显式推理轨迹进行监督微调是弱监督下实现泛化的必要条件，而对领域数据的持续预训练则能放大这一效果。将这些干预措施共同应用于Llama3.2-3B-Base模型后，使其在基础模型原本失败的三种设置中均实现了泛化。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates when large language models can learn reasoning under weak supervision, motivated by the difficulty of obtaining high-quality reward signals as models scale. The method involves a systematic empirical study across model families and reasoning domains under three weak supervision settings: scarce data, noisy rewards, and self-supervised proxy rewards. The main experimental results reveal that generalization is governed by training reward saturation dynamics, with models that generalize showing a prolonged pre-saturation phase where training reward and downstream performance improve together, while those that saturate rapidly memorize instead. Reasoning faithfulness, defined as the logical support of intermediate steps for the final answer, is identified as a key pre-RL property predicting this regime, whereas output diversity alone is uninformative. Further analysis shows that supervised fine-tuning on explicit reasoning traces is necessary for generalization under weak supervision, and continual pre-training on domain data amplifies this effect, enabling successful generalization in a Llama3.2-3B-Base model where it previously failed.
本文研究大型语言模型在何种条件下能够通过弱监督学习推理能力，其动机在于随着模型规模扩大，获取高质量奖励信号变得日益困难。方法上，通过对不同模型系列和推理领域在三种弱监督设置（数据稀缺、奖励噪声和自监督代理奖励）下进行系统性实证研究。主要实验结果表明，泛化能力受训练奖励饱和动态的支配：能够泛化的模型表现出较长的预饱和阶段，其中训练奖励和下游性能同步提升，而快速饱和的模型则倾向于记忆而非学习。研究发现，推理忠实性（即中间步骤对最终答案的逻辑支持程度）是预测模型所处机制的关键预强化学习属性，而输出多样性单独则无信息量。基于这些发现，研究进一步解耦了持续预训练和监督微调的贡献，发现对显式推理轨迹进行监督微调是弱监督下泛化的必要条件，而领域数据的持续预训练则能放大此效果。将这些干预措施应用于Llama3.2-3B-Base模型后，使其在原本失败的三种设置中均实现了泛化。
Empowering Multi-Turn Tool-Integrated Agentic Reasoning with Group Turn Policy Optimization
Authors: Yifeng Ding, Hung Le, Songyang Han, Kangrui Ruan, Zhenghui Jin, Varun Kumar, Zijian Wang, Anoop Deoras
First: 2025-11-18T19:01:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:40:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training Large Language Models (LLMs) for multi-turn Tool-Integrated Reasoning (TIR) - where models iteratively reason, generate code, and verify through execution - remains challenging for existing reinforcement learning (RL) approaches. Current RL methods, exemplified by Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), suffer from coarse-grained, trajectory-level rewards that provide insufficient learning signals for complex multi-turn interactions, leading to training stagnation. To address this issue, we propose Group Turn Policy Optimization (GTPO), a novel RL algorithm specifically designed for training LLMs on multi-turn TIR tasks. GTPO introduces three key innovations: (1) turn-level reward assignment that provides fine-grained feedback for individual turns, (2) return-based advantage estimation where normalized discounted returns are calculated as advantages, and (3) self-supervised reward shaping that exploits self-supervision signals from generated code to densify sparse binary outcome-based rewards. Our comprehensive evaluation demonstrates that GTPO outperforms GRPO by 3.0% across diverse math reasoning benchmarks, establishing its effectiveness. GTPO also improves GRPO by 3.9% on commonsense reasoning and program synthesis tasks, demonstrating its generalizability to non-math domains. Importantly, GTPO incurs negligible overhead, ensuring its practicality for real-world scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过组轮次策略优化赋能多轮工具集成智能体推理
为多轮工具集成推理（TIR）训练大型语言模型（LLMs）——即模型通过迭代推理、生成代码并执行验证——对现有强化学习（RL）方法仍具挑战。当前以组相对策略优化（GRPO）为代表的RL方法存在奖励粒度粗、仅基于轨迹级别的问题，无法为复杂的多轮交互提供充分学习信号，导致训练停滞。为解决此问题，我们提出组轮次策略优化（GTPO），一种专为多轮TIR任务训练LLMs设计的新型RL算法。GTPO引入三项关键创新：（1）轮次级奖励分配，为单轮提供细粒度反馈；（2）基于回报的优势估计，以归一化折现回报计算优势；（3）自监督奖励塑形，利用生成代码中的自监督信号来稠化稀疏的基于二元结果的奖励。全面评估表明，GTPO在多样化数学推理基准上超越GRPO达3.0%，验证了其有效性；在常识推理和程序合成任务上亦提升GRPO达3.9%，证明了其向非数学领域的泛化能力。重要的是，GTPO引入的开销可忽略不计，确保了实际应用的可行性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitations of existing reinforcement learning methods, such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), which use coarse-grained rewards that hinder effective training of Large Language Models for complex multi-turn Tool-Integrated Reasoning tasks. The proposed method, Group Turn Policy Optimization (GTPO), introduces three innovations: turn-level reward assignment for fine-grained feedback, return-based advantage estimation using normalized discounted returns, and self-supervised reward shaping to densify sparse binary rewards. Experimental results show that GTPO outperforms GRPO by 3.0% on math reasoning benchmarks and by 3.9% on commonsense reasoning and program synthesis tasks, demonstrating both effectiveness and generalizability with negligible computational overhead.
本研究的动机在于解决现有强化学习方法（如组相对策略优化GRPO）的局限性，这些方法使用粗粒度的奖励信号，难以有效训练大语言模型进行复杂的多轮工具集成推理任务。提出的方法——组轮次策略优化（GTPO）引入了三项创新：为单个轮次提供细粒度反馈的轮次级奖励分配、使用归一化折扣回报计算优势的基于回报的优势估计，以及利用生成代码的自监督信号来稠密化稀疏二元奖励的自监督奖励塑造。实验结果表明，GTPO在数学推理基准上比GRPO性能提升3.0%，在常识推理和程序合成任务上提升3.9%，证明了其有效性和泛化能力，且计算开销可忽略不计。
OGER: A Robust Offline-Guided Exploration Reward for Hybrid Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xinyu Ma, Mingzhou Xu, Xuebo Liu, Chang Jin, Qiang Wang, Derek F. Wong, Min Zhang
First: 2026-04-20T17:26:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:26:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent advancements in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) have significantly improved Large Language Model (LLM) reasoning, yet models often struggle to explore novel trajectories beyond their initial latent space. While offline teacher guidance and entropy-driven strategies have been proposed to address this, they often lack deep integration or are constrained by the model's inherent capacity. In this paper, we propose OGER, a novel framework that unifies offline teacher guidance and online reinforcement learning through a specialized reward modeling lens. OGER employs multi-teacher collaborative training and constructs an auxiliary exploration reward that leverages both offline trajectories and the model's own entropy to incentivize autonomous exploration. Extensive experiments across mathematical and general reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that OGER significantly outperforms competitive baselines, achieving substantial gains in mathematical reasoning while maintaining robust generalization to out-of-domain tasks. We provide a comprehensive analysis of training dynamics and conduct detailed ablation studies to validate the effectiveness of our entropy-aware reward modulation. Our code is available at https://github.com/ecoli-hit/OGER.git.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OGER：一种用于混合强化学习的鲁棒离线引导探索奖励机制
近期，可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）的进展显著提升了大型语言模型（LLM）的推理能力，但模型往往难以探索其初始潜在空间之外的新轨迹。尽管已有离线教师引导和熵驱动策略被提出以解决此问题，但它们通常缺乏深度整合或受限于模型固有容量。本文提出OGER，一种通过专用奖励建模视角统一离线教师引导与在线强化学习的新框架。OGER采用多教师协同训练，并构建一种辅助探索奖励，该奖励同时利用离线轨迹和模型自身的熵来激励自主探索。在数学与通用推理基准上的大量实验表明，OGER显著优于现有基线方法，在数学推理任务中取得大幅提升，同时保持对领域外任务的鲁棒泛化能力。我们提供了训练动态的全面分析，并进行了详细的消融研究以验证熵感知奖励调节机制的有效性。代码已开源：https://github.com/ecoli-hit/OGER.git。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the limitations of existing Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods, where models often fail to explore novel trajectories beyond their initial latent space, despite advancements in LLM reasoning. To address this, the authors propose OGER, a novel framework that unifies offline teacher guidance and online reinforcement learning by constructing an auxiliary exploration reward; this reward leverages multi-teacher collaborative training and the model's own entropy to incentivize autonomous exploration. Experimental results on mathematical and general reasoning benchmarks show that OGER significantly outperforms baselines, achieving substantial gains in mathematical reasoning while maintaining robust generalization to out-of-domain tasks, with ablation studies validating the effectiveness of the entropy-aware reward modulation.
本研究的动机源于现有可验证奖励强化学习方法的局限性，即模型难以探索其初始潜在空间之外的新轨迹。为解决此问题，作者提出了OGER框架，该框架通过构建辅助探索奖励，将离线教师指导与在线强化学习相统一；该奖励利用多教师协同训练和模型自身的熵来激励自主探索。在数学和通用推理基准上的实验结果表明，OGER显著优于现有基线方法，在数学推理上取得了实质性提升，同时保持了对外领域任务的鲁棒泛化能力，消融研究验证了熵感知奖励调节的有效性。
UDM-GRPO: Stable and Efficient Group Relative Policy Optimization for Uniform Discrete Diffusion Models
Authors: Jiaqi Wang, Haoge Deng, Ting Pan, Yang Liu, Chengyuan Wang, Fan Zhang, Yonggang Qi, Xinlong Wang
First: 2026-04-20T17:16:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:16:50+00:00
Comments: Code:\href{https://github.com/Yovecent/UDM-GRPO}{this https URL}
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Uniform Discrete Diffusion Model (UDM) has recently emerged as a promising paradigm for discrete generative modeling; however, its integration with reinforcement learning remains largely unexplored. We observe that naively applying GRPO to UDM leads to training instability and marginal performance gains. To address this, we propose \Ours, the first framework to integrate UDM with RL. Our method is guided by two key insights: (i) treating the final clean sample as the action provides more accurate and stable optimization signals; and (ii) reconstructing trajectories via the diffusion forward process better aligns probability paths with the pretraining distribution. Additionally, we introduce two strategies, Reduced-Step and CFG-Free, to further improve training efficiency. \Ours significantly improves base model performance across multiple T2I tasks. Notably, GenEval accuracy improves from $69\%$ to $96\%$ and PickScore increases from $20.46$ to $23.81$, achieving state-of-the-art performance in both continuous and discrete settings. On the OCR benchmark, accuracy rises from $8\%$ to $57\%$, further validating the generalization ability of our method. Code is available at \href{https://github.com/Yovecent/UDM-GRPO}{https://github.com/Yovecent/UDM-GRPO}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UDM-GRPO：面向均匀离散扩散模型的稳定高效群体相对策略优化
均匀离散扩散模型（UDM）近期成为离散生成建模的重要范式，但其与强化学习的结合尚未得到充分探索。研究发现，直接将GRPO应用于UDM会导致训练不稳定且性能提升有限。为此，我们提出首个将UDM与强化学习融合的框架。该方法基于两个关键洞见：（1）将最终纯净样本作为动作可提供更精确稳定的优化信号；（2）通过扩散前向过程重构轨迹能使概率路径与预训练分布更好对齐。我们还引入“降阶采样”和“免分类器引导”策略以提升训练效率。本方法在多项文生图任务中显著提升基础模型性能：GenEval准确率从69%提升至96%，PickScore从20.46提升至23.81，在连续与离散设定下均达到最优性能。在OCR基准测试中，准确率从8%提升至57%，进一步验证了方法的泛化能力。代码已开源。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of integrating Uniform Discrete Diffusion Models (UDM) with reinforcement learning, as naive application of Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) leads to instability and limited gains. The proposed UDM-GRPO framework introduces two key methodological insights: using the final clean sample as the action for stable optimization signals and reconstructing trajectories via the diffusion forward process to align with pretraining distributions, supplemented by Reduced-Step and CFG-Free strategies for efficiency. Experimental results demonstrate significant performance improvements, with GenEval accuracy rising from 69% to 96%, PickScore from 20.46 to 23.81, and OCR benchmark accuracy from 8% to 57%, achieving state-of-the-art outcomes in both continuous and discrete settings.
本文针对均匀离散扩散模型与强化学习结合时，直接应用组相对策略优化会导致训练不稳定和性能提升有限的问题，提出了UDM-GRPO框架。该方法基于两个核心思路：将最终干净样本作为动作以提供更准确的优化信号，以及通过扩散前向过程重构轨迹以更好地对齐预训练分布，并辅以减少步数和免分类器引导策略来提升效率。实验结果表明，该方法显著提升了基础模型性能，在多个文本到图像任务中，GenEval准确率从69%提高到96%，PickScore从20.46提升至23.81，在OCR基准测试中准确率从8%增至57%，在连续和离散设置下均达到了最先进的性能水平。
SEARL: Joint Optimization of Policy and Tool Graph Memory for Self-Evolving Agents
Authors: Xinshun Feng, Xinhao Song, Lijun Li, Gongshen Liu, Jing Shao
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-09T04:38:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:11:17+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) have demonstrated significant potential in single-turn reasoning tasks. With the paradigm shift toward self-evolving agentic learning, models are increasingly expected to learn from trajectories by synthesizing tools or accumulating explicit experiences. However, prevailing methods typically rely on large-scale LLMs or multi-agent frameworks, which hinder their deployment in resource-constrained environments. The inherent sparsity of outcome-based rewards also poses a substantial challenge, as agents typically receive feedback only upon completion of tasks. To address these limitations, we introduce a Tool-Memory based self-evolving agentic framework SEARL. Unlike approaches that directly utilize interaction experiences, our method constructs a structured experience memory that integrates planning with execution. This provides a novel state abstraction that facilitates generalization across analogous contexts, such as tool reuse. Consequently, agents extract explicit knowledge from historical data while leveraging inter-trajectory correlations to densify reward signals. We evaluate our framework on knowledge reasoning and mathematics tasks, demonstrating its effectiveness in achieving more practical and efficient learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SEARL：面向自进化智能体的策略与工具图记忆联合优化框架
近期基于可验证奖励的强化学习在单轮推理任务中展现出显著潜力。随着范式向自进化智能体学习转变，模型日益需要通过合成工具或积累显式经验从轨迹中学习。然而，主流方法通常依赖大规模语言模型或多智能体框架，限制了其在资源受限环境中的部署。基于结果的奖励本身具有稀疏性，因智能体通常仅在任务完成后获得反馈，这构成了重大挑战。为应对这些局限，我们提出了基于工具记忆的自进化智能体框架SEARL。与直接利用交互经验的方法不同，本方法构建了融合规划与执行的结构化经验记忆，提供了一种新颖的状态抽象机制，可促进跨相似场景（如工具复用）的泛化能力。由此，智能体既能从历史数据中提取显式知识，又能利用轨迹间关联性来稠密化奖励信号。我们在知识推理与数学任务上评估了该框架，验证了其在实现更实用高效学习方面的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of large-scale LLMs and sparse rewards in self-evolving agents, this paper introduces SEARL, a framework that jointly optimizes policy and a structured tool graph memory. The method constructs a memory integrating planning and execution to provide state abstraction, enabling generalization and denser reward signals by leveraging inter-trajectory correlations. Experimental results on knowledge reasoning and mathematics tasks demonstrate that SEARL achieves more practical and efficient learning compared to prevailing approaches.
针对自进化智能体中大规模语言模型依赖和奖励稀疏性的问题，本文提出了SEARL框架，联合优化策略与结构化工具图记忆。该方法构建了融合规划与执行的记忆系统，通过状态抽象促进泛化，并利用轨迹间关联来稠密化奖励信号。在知识推理和数学任务上的实验结果表明，SEARL相比主流方法实现了更实用高效的学习。
Different Paths to Harmful Compliance: Behavioral Side Effects and Mechanistic Divergence Across LLM Jailbreaks
Authors: Md Rysul Kabir, Zoran Tiganj
First: 2026-04-20T17:01:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T17:01:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Open-weight language models can be rendered unsafe through several distinct interventions, but the resulting models may differ substantially in capabilities, behavioral profile, and internal failure mode. We study behavioral and mechanistic properties of jailbroken models across three unsafe routes: harmful supervised fine-tuning (SFT), harmful reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), and refusal-suppressing abliteration. All three routes achieve near-ceiling harmful compliance, but they diverge once we move beyond direct harmfulness. RLVR-jailbroken models show minimal degradation and preserve explicit harm recognition in a structured self-audit: they are able to identify harmful prompts and describe how a safe LLM should respond, yet they comply with the harmful request. With RLVR, harmful behavior is strongly suppressed by a reflective safety scaffold: when a harmful prompt is prepended with an instruction to reflect on safety standards, harmful behavior drops close to the baseline. Category-specific RLVR jailbreaks generalize broadly across harmfulness domains. Models jailbroken with SFT show the largest collapse in explicit safety judgments, the highest behavioral drift, and a substantial capability loss on standard benchmarks. Abliteration is family-dependent in both self-audit and response to a reflective safety scaffold. Mechanistic and repair analyses further separate the routes: abliteration is consistent with localized refusal-feature deletion, RLVR with preserved safety geometry but retargeted policy behavior, and SFT with broader distributed drift. Targeted repair partially recovers RLVR-jailbroken models, but has little effect on SFT-jailbroken models. Together, these results show that jailbreaks can produce vastly different properties despite similar harmfulness, with models jailbroken via RLVR showing remarkable similarity to the base model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通往有害合规的不同路径：大语言模型越狱的行为副作用与机制差异
开源语言模型可通过多种干预手段变得不安全，但由此产生的模型在能力、行为特征和内部故障模式上可能存在显著差异。本研究通过三种不安全路径——有害监督微调（SFT）、基于可验证奖励的有害强化学习（RLVR）以及拒绝抑制消融——系统考察了越狱模型的行为与机制特性。三种路径均能实现接近上限的有害合规率，但在直接有害性之外的维度呈现明显分化：RLVR越狱模型在结构化自审中表现出最小性能退化，且能保持明确的有害识别能力——它们能识别有害提示并描述安全模型应如何回应，却仍遵从有害指令。当有害提示前置安全反思指令时，RLVR模型的有害行为会被反思性安全框架强烈抑制至接近基线水平。类别特定的RLVR越狱在多个有害领域具有广泛泛化性。SFT越狱模型在显式安全判断上崩溃最严重，行为漂移最大，且在标准基准测试中出现显著能力损失。消融越狱在自审与安全框架响应中均呈现家族依赖性。机制分析与修复实验进一步区分了这些路径：消融符合局部拒绝特征删除机制，RLVR保持安全几何结构但重定向策略行为，SFT则引发更广泛的分布式漂移。针对性修复能部分恢复RLVR越狱模型，但对SFT越狱模型效果甚微。这些结果表明，尽管危害程度相似，不同越狱方式产生的模型特性差异巨大，其中RLVR越狱模型与原始模型展现出惊人的相似性。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates how different jailbreaking methods affect large language models (LLMs), motivated by the need to understand the distinct behavioral and internal changes that arise from various interventions aimed at inducing harmful compliance. The authors compare three unsafe routes—harmful supervised fine-tuning (SFT), harmful reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), and refusal-suppressing abliteration—finding that while all achieve high harmful compliance, they diverge significantly in other aspects. Experimental results show that RLVR-jailbroken models maintain explicit harm recognition and general capabilities, with harmful behavior strongly suppressed by safety reflections, whereas SFT leads to major safety judgment collapse, behavioral drift, and capability loss, and abliteration exhibits family-dependent effects; mechanistic analyses reveal distinct internal failure modes, with targeted repair partially effective only for RLVR models.
本研究探讨不同越狱方法对大型语言模型的影响，动机在于理解旨在诱导有害服从的各种干预措施所产生的不同行为与内部变化。作者比较了三种不安全路径——有害监督微调、有害可验证奖励强化学习和拒绝抑制消除术，发现尽管三者都实现了高有害服从率，但在其他方面差异显著。实验结果表明，通过强化学习越狱的模型保持了明确的有害识别能力和通用性能，其有害行为可被安全反思强烈抑制，而监督微调则导致安全判断严重崩溃、行为漂移和能力下降，消除术则表现出家族依赖性效应；机理分析揭示了不同的内部故障模式，针对性修复仅对强化学习模型部分有效。
Too Correct to Learn: Reinforcement Learning on Saturated Reasoning Data
Authors: Zhenwen Liang, Yujun Zhou, Sidi Lu, Xiangliang Zhang, Haitao Mi, Dong Yu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-20T16:43:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T16:43:28+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Main Paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) enhances LLM reasoning, yet a paradox emerges as models scale: strong base models saturate standard benchmarks (e.g., MATH), yielding correct but homogeneous solutions. In such environments, the lack of failure cases causes the advantage signal in group-relative algorithms (e.g., GRPO) to vanish, driving policies into mode collapse. To address this, we propose Constrained Uniform Top-K Sampling (CUTS), a parameter-free decoding strategy enforcing structure-preserving exploration. Unlike standard sampling that follows model biases, CUTS flattens the local optimization landscape by sampling uniformly from constrained high-confidence candidates. We integrate this into Mixed-CUTS, a training framework synergizing exploitative and exploratory rollouts to amplify intra-group advantage variance. Experiments on Qwen3 models demonstrate that our approach prevents policy degeneration and significantly boosts out-of-domain generalization. Notably, Mixed-CUTS improves Pass@1 accuracy on the challenging AIME25 benchmark by up to 15.1% over standard GRPO, validating that maintaining diversity within the semantic manifold is critical for rigorous reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：过于正确以致难学：饱和推理数据上的强化学习
强化学习（RL）能提升大语言模型的推理能力，但随着模型规模扩大，出现一个悖论：强大的基础模型会使标准基准（如MATH）趋于饱和，产生正确但同质化的解决方案。在此类环境中，失败案例的缺失导致群体相对算法（如GRPO）中的优势信号消失，使策略陷入模式崩溃。为解决此问题，我们提出约束均匀Top-K采样（CUTS），这是一种无需参数的解码策略，强制进行结构保持式探索。与遵循模型偏见的标准采样不同，CUTS通过从受限高置信候选中均匀采样来平坦化局部优化空间。我们将其整合为Mixed-CUTS训练框架，协同利用开发性与探索性推演以放大组内优势方差。基于Qwen3模型的实验表明，该方法能防止策略退化并显著提升跨领域泛化能力。值得注意的是，在挑战性基准AIME25上，Mixed-CUTS的Pass@1准确率较标准GRPO最高提升15.1%，验证了在语义流形中保持多样性对严谨推理至关重要。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses a paradox in reinforcement learning for large language models, where strong base models saturate reasoning benchmarks, leading to homogeneous correct solutions and vanishing advantage signals that cause policy mode collapse. The authors propose Constrained Uniform Top-K Sampling (CUTS), a parameter-free decoding method that enforces structure-preserving exploration by uniformly sampling from high-confidence candidates to flatten the local optimization landscape, and integrate it into Mixed-CUTS, a training framework combining exploitative and exploratory rollouts to increase intra-group advantage variance. Experimental results on Qwen3 models show the approach prevents policy degeneration and enhances out-of-domain generalization, improving Pass@1 accuracy on the AIME25 benchmark by up to 15.1% over standard GRPO, underscoring the importance of maintaining diversity for rigorous reasoning.
本文针对大语言模型强化学习中的一个悖论展开研究，即强大的基础模型会使推理基准饱和，导致解决方案同质化且优势信号消失，从而引发策略模式崩溃。作者提出了约束均匀Top-K采样方法，这是一种无参数的解码策略，通过从高置信度候选中均匀采样以保持结构探索，从而平坦化局部优化景观，并将其整合到Mixed-CUTS训练框架中，该框架结合了利用性和探索性轨迹以增强组内优势方差。在Qwen3模型上的实验结果表明，该方法能有效防止策略退化并提升领域外泛化能力，在AIME25基准测试中将Pass@1准确率较标准GRPO提高了15.1%，验证了保持语义流形多样性对严格推理的重要性。
TOOLCAD: Exploring Tool-Using Large Language Models in Text-to-CAD Generation with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yifei Gong, Xing Wu, Wenda Liu, Kang Tu
First: 2026-04-09T08:22:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T16:37:31+00:00
Comments: ACL2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Computer-Aided Design (CAD) is an expert-level task that relies on long-horizon reasoning and coherent modeling actions. Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown remarkable advancements in enabling language agents to tackle real-world tasks. Notably, there has been no investigation into how tool-using LLMs optimally interact with CAD engines, hindering the emergence of LLM-based agentic text-to-CAD modeling systems. We propose ToolCAD, a novel agentic CAD framework deploying LLMs as tool-using agents for text-to-CAD generation. Furthermore, we introduce an interactive CAD modeling gym to rollout reasoning and tool-augmented interaction trajectories with the CAD engine, incorporating hybrid feedback and human supervision. Meanwhile, an end-to-end post-training strategy is presented to enable the LLM agent to elicit refined CAD Modeling Chain of Thought (CAD-CoT) and evolve into proficient CAD tool-using agents via online curriculum reinforcement learning. Our findings demonstrate ToolCAD fills the gap in adopting and training open-source LLMs for CAD tool-using agents, enabling them to perform comparably to proprietary models, paving the way for more accessible and robust autonomous text-to-CAD modeling systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TOOLCAD：基于强化学习的工具化大语言模型在文本到CAD生成中的探索
计算机辅助设计（CAD）是一项依赖长程推理与连贯建模操作的专家级任务。大语言模型（LLM）在赋能语言智能体处理现实任务方面已取得显著进展。然而，目前尚未有研究探讨工具化LLM如何与CAD引擎实现最优交互，这阻碍了基于LLM的自主文本到CAD建模系统的发展。我们提出ToolCAD——一种新颖的自主CAD框架，将LLM部署为工具化智能体以实现文本到CAD生成。此外，我们构建了交互式CAD建模训练场，用于展开与CAD引擎的推理及工具增强交互轨迹，并融合混合反馈与人工监督。同时，提出端到端的后训练策略，使LLM智能体能通过在线课程强化学习生成精细化的CAD建模思维链（CAD-CoT），并进化为熟练的CAD工具使用智能体。实验表明，ToolCAD填补了开源LLM在CAD工具化智能体适配与训练方面的空白，使其性能可比肩专有模型，为构建更易用、更鲁棒的自主文本到CAD建模系统开辟了道路。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the lack of research on how tool-using large language models (LLMs) can optimally interact with CAD engines for text-to-CAD generation, this paper introduces ToolCAD, a novel agentic framework that deploys LLMs as tool-using agents. The method involves an interactive CAD modeling gym to generate interaction trajectories with hybrid feedback and human supervision, coupled with an end-to-end post-training strategy using online curriculum reinforcement learning to refine the model's CAD modeling chain of thought. Experimental results demonstrate that ToolCAD successfully bridges the gap in training open-source LLMs for CAD tasks, enabling them to achieve performance comparable to proprietary models and advancing accessible autonomous text-to-CAD systems.
本文的动机在于，目前缺乏关于工具使用型大语言模型如何与CAD引擎最优交互以实现文本到CAD生成的研究。为此，论文提出了ToolCAD这一新颖的智能体框架，将大语言模型部署为工具使用型智能体。方法上，通过一个交互式CAD建模环境来生成与CAD引擎的交互轨迹，并结合混合反馈与人工监督，同时采用端到端的后训练策略，利用在线课程强化学习来优化CAD建模思维链。主要实验结果表明，ToolCAD填补了在训练开源大语言模型作为CAD工具使用智能体方面的空白，使其性能可与专有模型相媲美，为开发更易用、更稳健的自主文本到CAD建模系统铺平了道路。
Train Separately, Merge Together: Modular Post-Training with Mixture-of-Experts
Authors: Jacob Morrison, Sanjay Adhikesaven, Akshita Bhagia, Matei Zaharia, Noah A. Smith, Sewon Min
First: 2026-04-20T16:24:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T16:24:41+00:00
Comments: 9 content pages, 23 pages overall, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Extending a fully post-trained language model with new domain capabilities is fundamentally limited by monolithic training paradigms: retraining from scratch is expensive and scales poorly, while continued training often degrades existing capabilities. We present BAR (Branch-Adapt-Route), which trains independent domain experts, each through its own mid-training, supervised finetuning, and reinforcement learning pipeline, and composes them via a Mixture-of-Experts architecture with lightweight router training. Unlike retraining approaches that mix all domains and require full reprocessing for any update (with cost scaling quadratically), BAR enables updating individual experts independently with linear cost scaling and no degradation to existing domains. At the 7B scale, with experts for math, code, tool use, and safety, BAR achieves an overall score of 49.1 (averaged across 7 evaluation categories), matching or exceeding re-training baselines (47.8 without mid-training, 50.5 with). We further show that modular training provides a structural advantage: by isolating each domain, it avoids the catastrophic forgetting that occurs when late-stage RL degrades capabilities from earlier training stages, while significantly reducing the cost and complexity of updating or adding a domain. Together, these results suggest that decoupled, expert-based training is a scalable alternative to monolithic retraining for extending language models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分训合构：基于专家混合的模块化后训练方法
扩展已完全后训练的语言模型以获取新领域能力，受限于传统整体训练范式：从头再训练成本高昂且扩展性差，而持续训练常导致原有能力退化。本文提出BAR（分支-适配-路由）方法，通过独立训练各领域专家（各自包含中期训练、监督微调和强化学习流程），并借助轻量级路由训练的专家混合架构进行组合。与需混合所有领域且每次更新均需全量重处理（成本呈二次增长）的再训练方法不同，BAR支持独立更新单个专家，成本呈线性增长且不影响现有领域。在70亿参数规模下，针对数学、代码、工具使用和安全领域的专家模型，BAR在7个评估类别上的综合得分为49.1，达到或超越再训练基线（无中期训练为47.8，含中期训练为50.5）。研究进一步表明模块化训练具有结构优势：通过隔离各领域，可避免后期强化学习对早期训练能力的灾难性遗忘，同时显著降低领域更新或新增的成本与复杂度。这些结果共同表明，解耦的专家化训练是扩展语言模型时替代整体再训练的可扩展方案。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitations of monolithic training paradigms for extending language models, which are either expensive to retrain from scratch or suffer from catastrophic forgetting during continued training. The method, called BAR (Branch-Adapt-Route), involves training independent domain experts separately through mid-training, supervised finetuning, and reinforcement learning pipelines, and then composing them via a Mixture-of-Experts architecture with lightweight router training. Main experimental results at the 7B scale, with experts for math, code, tool use, and safety, show that BAR achieves an overall score of 49.1 across seven evaluation categories, matching or exceeding retraining baselines, while enabling independent expert updates with linear cost scaling and no degradation to existing domains.
本研究的动机是克服整体式训练范式在扩展语言模型时的局限性，即从头开始重新训练成本高昂，而持续训练又常导致灾难性遗忘。该方法名为BAR（分支-适应-路由），通过独立的中间训练、监督微调和强化学习流程分别训练各领域专家，然后通过轻量级路由器训练的混合专家架构将它们组合起来。在70亿参数规模下，针对数学、代码、工具使用和安全等领域的专家实验结果表明，BAR在七个评估类别中取得了49.1的综合得分，达到或超过了重新训练的基线水平，同时支持独立更新专家，实现线性成本扩展且不损害现有领域能力。
Scalable Physics-Informed Neural Differential Equations and Data-Driven Algorithms for HVAC Systems
Authors: Hanfeng Zhai, Hongtao Qiao, Hassan Mansour, Christopher Laughman
First: 2026-04-20T15:56:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T15:56:00+00:00
Comments: 50 pages, 26 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a scalable, data-driven simulation framework for large-scale heating, ventilation, and air conditioning (HVAC) systems that couples physics-informed neural ordinary differential equations (PINODEs) with differential-algebraic equation (DAE) solvers. At the component level, we learn heat-exchanger dynamics using an implicit PINODE formulation that predicts conserved quantities (refrigerant mass $M_r$ and internal energy $E_\text{hx}$) as outputs, enabling physics-informed training via automatic differentiation of mass/energy balances. Stable long-horizon prediction is achieved through gradient-stabilized latent evolution with gated architectures and layer normalization. At the system level, we integrate learned components with DAE solvers (IDA and DASSL) that explicitly enforce junction constraints (pressure equilibrium and mass-flow consistency), and we use Bayesian optimization to tune solver parameters for accuracy--efficiency trade-offs. To reduce residual system-level bias, we introduce a lightweight corrector network trained on short trajectory segments. Across dual-compressor and scaled network studies, the proposed approach attains multi-fold speedups over high-fidelity simulation while keeping errors low (MAPE below a few percent) and scales to systems with up to 32 compressor--condenser pairs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向暖通空调系统的可扩展物理信息神经微分方程与数据驱动算法
我们提出了一种面向大规模暖通空调系统的可扩展数据驱动仿真框架，该框架将物理信息神经常微分方程与微分代数方程求解器相结合。在组件层面，我们采用隐式PINODE公式学习换热器动力学，以守恒量（制冷剂质量$M_r$和内能$E_\text{hx}$）作为输出，通过质量/能量平衡的自动微分实现物理信息训练。通过门控架构与层归一化的梯度稳定潜变量演化，实现了稳定的长时程预测。在系统层面，我们将学习到的组件与显式强制节点约束（压力平衡与质量流量一致性）的DAE求解器（IDA和DASSL）集成，并采用贝叶斯优化调整求解器参数以权衡精度与效率。为降低系统级残差偏差，我们引入基于短轨迹段训练的轻量级校正网络。在双压缩机和扩展网络的研究中，所提方法在保持较低误差（平均绝对百分比误差低于百分之几）的同时，相比高保真仿真实现数倍加速，并可扩展至最多32组压缩机-冷凝器对的系统。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the need for efficient and accurate simulation of large-scale HVAC systems by developing a scalable, data-driven framework that integrates physics-informed neural ordinary differential equations (PINODEs) with differential-algebraic equation (DAE) solvers. The method involves learning component-level dynamics, such as heat exchangers, using implicit PINODEs that output conserved quantities and enable physics-informed training via automatic differentiation, while employing gradient-stabilized latent evolution for stable long-horizon predictions. At the system level, learned components are coupled with DAE solvers to enforce junction constraints, with Bayesian optimization tuning solver parameters and a lightweight corrector network reducing residual bias. Experimental results on dual-compressor and scaled networks demonstrate multi-fold speedups over high-fidelity simulations while maintaining low errors (MAPE below a few percent) and scaling to systems with up to 32 compressor-condenser pairs.
本文针对大规模HVAC系统高效精确仿真的需求，提出了一种可扩展的数据驱动框架，将物理信息神经常微分方程（PINODEs）与微分代数方程（DAE）求解器相结合。该方法在组件层面使用隐式PINODEs学习热交换器等动力学，输出守恒量并通过自动微分实现物理信息训练，同时采用梯度稳定潜变量演化确保长期预测稳定性；在系统层面，将学习到的组件与DAE求解器耦合以强制执行节点约束，利用贝叶斯优化调整求解器参数，并引入轻量级校正网络减少残余偏差。在双压缩机和扩展网络上的实验结果表明，该方法相比高保真仿真实现了数倍加速，同时保持较低误差（平均绝对百分比误差低于几个百分点），并可扩展至多达32个压缩机-冷凝器对的系统。
Knowing When to Quit: A Principled Framework for Dynamic Abstention in LLM Reasoning
Authors: Hen Davidov, Nachshon Cohen, Oren Kalinsky, Yaron Fairstein, Guy Kushilevitz, Ram Yazdi, Patrick Rebeschini
First: 2026-04-20T15:38:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T15:38:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) using chain-of-thought reasoning often waste substantial compute by producing long, incorrect responses. Abstention can mitigate this by withholding outputs unlikely to be correct. While most abstention methods decide to withhold outputs before or after generation, dynamic mid-generation abstention considers early termination of unpromising reasoning traces at each token position. Prior work has explored empirical variants of this idea, but principled guidance for the abstention rule remains lacking. We present a formal analysis of dynamic abstention for LLMs, modeling abstention as an explicit action within a regularized reinforcement learning framework. An abstention reward parameter controls the trade-off between compute and information. We show that abstaining when the value function falls below this reward strictly outperforms natural baselines under general conditions. We further derive a principled and efficient method to approximate the value function. Empirical results on mathematical reasoning and toxicity avoidance tasks support our theory and demonstrate improved selective accuracy over existing methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：适时终止：大语言模型推理中动态弃权的原则性框架
采用思维链推理的大语言模型常因生成冗长错误回答而浪费大量算力。弃权机制可通过抑制可能错误的输出来缓解此问题。现有弃权方法多在生成前后决定是否抑制输出，而动态中途弃权则考虑在每个词元位置提前终止无潜力的推理轨迹。先前研究虽探索了该思想的实证变体，但弃权规则仍缺乏原则性指导。本文对大语言模型的动态弃权进行形式化分析，将弃权建模为正则化强化学习框架中的显式动作。通过弃权奖励参数控制算力与信息间的权衡，证明当价值函数低于该奖励时执行弃权，在一般条件下严格优于自然基线方法。进一步推导出近似价值函数的原则性高效方法。数学推理与毒性规避任务的实证结果支持理论分析，并展现出优于现有方法的选择性准确率。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of large language models (LLMs) expending compute on lengthy, incorrect chain-of-thought reasoning, this paper introduces a principled framework for dynamic mid-generation abstention, which terminates unpromising reasoning traces early. The method formulates abstention as an action within a regularized reinforcement learning framework, where an abstention reward parameter balances compute and information, and demonstrates that abstaining when a derived value function falls below this reward is theoretically optimal. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning and toxicity avoidance tasks show that this approach improves selective accuracy over existing baselines.
针对大语言模型在思维链推理中因生成冗长错误回答而浪费计算资源的问题，本文提出了一个动态中途弃权的原则性框架，旨在早期终止无望的推理轨迹。该方法将弃权建模为强化学习框架中的一个显式动作，通过一个弃权奖励参数权衡计算与信息，并证明当价值函数低于该奖励时弃权在理论上是最优的。在数学推理和毒性规避任务上的实验结果表明，该方法相比现有基线提高了选择性准确率。
ReflexiCoder: Teaching Large Language Models to Self-Reflect on Generated Code and Self-Correct It via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Juyong Jiang, Jiasi Shen, Sunghun Kim, Kang Min Yoo, Jeonghoon Kim, Sungju Kim
First: 2026-03-06T03:38:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T15:16:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While Large Language Models (LLMs) have revolutionized code generation, standard ``System 1'' approaches that generate solutions in a single forward pass often hit a performance ceiling on complex algorithmic tasks. Existing iterative refinement strategies attempt to bridge this gap at inference time, yet they predominantly rely on external oracles, execution feedback, or computationally expensive prompt-response cycles. In this work, we propose ReflexiCoder, a novel reinforcement learning (RL) framework that internalizes the structured reasoning trajectory, encompassing initial generation, bug and optimization aware reflection, and self-correction, directly into the model's weights. Unlike prior methods, ReflexiCoder shifts the paradigm from external-dependent refinement to an intrinsic, fully autonomous self-reflection and self-correction capabilities at inference time. We utilize an RL-only training paradigm with granular reward functions to optimize the entire reflection-correction trajectory, teaching the model how to debug without reliance on ground-truth feedback or execution engines at inference time. Extensive experiments across seven benchmarks demonstrate that our ReflexiCoder-8B establishes a new state-of-the-art (SOTA) among leading open-source models in the 1.5B to 14B range, achieving 94.51% (87.20%) on HumanEval (Plus), 81.80% (78.57%) on MBPP (Plus), 35.00% on BigCodeBench, 52.21% on LiveCodeBench, and 37.34% on CodeForces in a single-attempt setting, rivaling or surpassing proprietary models like GPT-5.1. Notably, our framework is significantly more token-efficient than base models, reducing inference-time compute overhead by approximately 40% through disciplined, efficient reasoning and reflection patterns. The source code and data are available at https://github.com/juyongjiang/ReflexiCoder.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReflexiCoder：通过强化学习教导大语言模型对生成代码进行自我反思与自我修正
尽管大语言模型（LLMs）已彻底改变了代码生成领域，但依赖单次前向生成的标准“系统1”方法在处理复杂算法任务时往往触及性能瓶颈。现有的迭代优化策略试图在推理阶段弥补这一差距，但它们主要依赖外部验证器、执行反馈或计算成本高昂的提示-响应循环。本研究提出ReflexiCoder——一种新颖的强化学习框架，它将结构化推理轨迹（包括初始生成、缺陷与优化感知的反思、自我修正）直接内化至模型权重中。与先前方法不同，ReflexiCoder将范式从外部依赖的优化转变为推理阶段内在的、完全自主的自我反思与自我修正能力。我们采用纯强化学习训练范式，配合细粒度奖励函数来优化整个反思-修正轨迹，使模型学会在不依赖真实反馈或执行引擎的情况下进行调试。在七个基准测试上的广泛实验表明，ReflexiCoder-8B在1.5B至14B参数规模的主流开源模型中确立了新的最优性能：在HumanEval（Plus）达到94.51%（87.20%），MBPP（Plus）达到81.80%（78.57%），BigCodeBench为35.00%，LiveCodeBench为52.21%，CodeForces为37.34%（单次尝试设置），其表现可与GPT-5.1等专有模型媲美甚至超越。值得注意的是，该框架的令牌效率显著优于基础模型，通过规范高效的推理与反思模式，将推理阶段计算开销降低约40%。源代码与数据已发布于https://github.com/juyongjiang/ReflexiCoder。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the performance limitations of single-pass code generation in large language models (LLMs) and the external dependencies of existing iterative refinement methods, this paper introduces ReflexiCoder, a reinforcement learning framework that teaches models to internalize self-reflection and self-correction for code generation. Learning from Less: Measuring the Effectiveness of RLVR in Low Data and Compute Regimes
Authors: Justin Bauer, Thomas Walshe, Derek Pham, Harit Vishwakarma, Armin Parchami, Frederic Sala, Paroma Varma
First: 2026-04-20T15:04:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T15:04:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Fine-tuning Large Language Models (LLMs) typically relies on large quantities of high-quality annotated data, or questions with well-defined ground truth answers in the case of Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR). While previous work has explored the benefits to model reasoning capabilities by scaling both data and compute used for RLVR, these results lack applicability in many real-world settings where annotated data and accessible compute may be scarce. In this work, we present a comprehensive empirical study of open-source Small Language Model (SLM) performance after RLVR in low data regimes. Across three novel datasets covering number counting problems, graph reasoning, and spatial reasoning, we characterize how model performance scales with dataset size, diversity, and complexity. We demonstrate that (1) procedural datasets allow for fine-grained evaluation and training dataset development with controllable properties (size, diversity, and complexity), (2) under RLVR, models trained on lower complexity tasks can generalize to higher complexity tasks, and (3) training on mixed complexity datasets is associated with the greatest benefits in low data regimes, providing up to 5x sample efficiency versus training on easy tasks. These findings inspire future work on the development of data scaling laws for RLVR and the use of procedural data generators to further understand effective data development for efficient LLM fine-tuning.

微调大型语言模型通常依赖于大量高质量标注数据，或在可验证奖励强化学习情境下需要具备明确标准答案的问题。尽管先前研究已探索通过扩展RLVR所用数据与算力来提升模型推理能力的益处，但这些成果在许多现实场景中适用性有限，因为标注数据和可用算力可能匮乏。本研究对开源小型语言模型在低数据条件下进行RLVR后的性能进行了全面实证分析。通过涵盖数字计数问题、图推理和空间推理的三个新颖数据集，我们刻画了模型性能如何随数据集规模、多样性和复杂性而变化。结果表明：（1）程序化数据集支持具有可控属性（规模、多样性和复杂性）的细粒度评估与训练数据集开发；（2）在RLVR框架下，基于低复杂性任务训练的模型能够泛化至高复杂性任务；（3）在低数据条件下，混合复杂性数据集的训练能带来最大效益，相较于简单任务训练可实现高达5倍的样本效率提升。这些发现为未来RLVR数据缩放定律的建立，以及利用程序化数据生成器进一步理解高效LLM微调的有效数据开发提供了启示。

Training and Agentic Inference Strategies for LLM-based Manim Animation Generation
Authors: Ravidu Suien Rammuni Silva, Ahmad Lotfi, Isibor Kennedy Ihianle, Golnaz Shahtahmassebi, Jordan J. Bird
First: 2026-04-20T14:54:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T14:54:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generating programmatic animation using libraries such as Manim presents unique challenges for Large Language Models (LLMs), requiring spatial reasoning, temporal sequencing, and familiarity with domain-specific APIs that are underrepresented in general pre-training data. A systematic study of how training and inference strategies interact in this setting is lacking in current research. This study introduces ManimTrainer, a training pipeline that combines Supervised Fine-tuning (SFT) with Reinforcement Learning (RL) based Group Relative Policy Optimisation (GRPO) using a unified reward signal that fuses code and visual assessment signals, and ManimAgent, an inference pipeline featuring Renderer-in-the-loop (RITL) and API documentation-augmented RITL (RITL-DOC) strategies. Using these techniques, this study presents the first unified training and inference study for text-to-code-to-video transformation with Manim. It evaluates 17 open-source sub-30B LLMs across nine combinations of training and inference strategies using ManimBench. Results show that SFT generally improves code quality, while GRPO enhances visual outputs and increases the models' responsiveness to extrinsic signals during self-correction at inference time. The Qwen 3 Coder 30B model with GRPO and RITL-DOC achieved the highest overall performance, with a 94% Render Success Rate (RSR) and 85.7% Visual Similarity (VS) to reference videos, surpassing the baseline GPT-4.1 model by +3 percentage points in VS. Additionally, the analysis shows that the correlation between code and visual metrics strengthens with SFT and GRPO but weakens with inference-time enhancements, highlighting the complementary roles of training and agentic inference strategies in Manim animation generation.

Enhancing LLM-based Search Agents via Contribution Weighted Group Relative Policy Optimization
Authors: Junzhe Wang, Zhiheng Xi, Yajie Yang, Hao Luo, Shihan Dou, Tao Gui, Qi Zhang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-15T17:37:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T14:14:42+00:00
Comments: Accepted to the 64th Annual Meeting of the Association for Computational Linguistics (ACL 2026), Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Search agents extend Large Language Models (LLMs) beyond static parametric knowledge by enabling access to up-to-date and long-tail information unavailable during pretraining. While reinforcement learning has been widely adopted for training such agents, existing approaches face key limitations: process supervision often suffers from unstable value estimation, whereas outcome supervision struggles with credit assignment due to sparse, trajectory-level rewards. To bridge this gap, we propose Contribution-Weighted GRPO (CW-GRPO), a framework that integrates process supervision into group relative policy optimization. Instead of directly optimizing process rewards, CW-GRPO employs an LLM judge to assess the retrieval utility and reasoning correctness at each search round, producing per-round contribution scores. These scores are used to rescale outcome-based advantages along the trajectory, enabling fine-grained credit assignment without sacrificing optimization stability. Experiments on multiple knowledge-intensive benchmarks show that CW-GRPO outperforms standard GRPO by 5.0% on Qwen3-8B and 6.3% on Qwen3-1.7B, leading to more effective search behaviors. Additional analysis reveals that successful trajectories exhibit concentrated contributions in specific rounds, providing empirical insight into search agent tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于贡献加权组相对策略优化的LLM搜索智能体增强方法
搜索智能体通过获取预训练阶段无法获得的实时信息与长尾知识，拓展了大语言模型（LLMs）的静态参数化知识边界。尽管强化学习已被广泛用于训练此类智能体，现有方法仍面临关键局限：过程监督常受价值估计不稳定影响，而结果监督则因稀疏的轨迹级奖励难以实现精确的信用分配。为弥合这一差距，我们提出贡献加权GRPO（CW-GRPO）框架，将过程监督融入组相对策略优化。该方法不直接优化过程奖励，而是通过LLM评判器评估每轮检索的效用与推理正确性，生成逐轮贡献分数。这些分数用于重新标定基于结果的轨迹优势度，在保持优化稳定性的同时实现细粒度信用分配。在多个知识密集型基准测试中，CW-GRPO在Qwen3-8B和Qwen3-1.7B模型上分别超越标准GRPO 5.0%和6.3%，展现出更高效的搜索行为。进一步分析表明，成功轨迹的贡献度集中于特定轮次，为搜索智能体任务提供了实证依据。

The paper addresses limitations in training LLM-based search agents, where process supervision suffers from unstable value estimation and outcome supervision struggles with sparse rewards. To bridge this gap, the authors propose Contribution-Weighted GRPO (CW-GRPO), a framework that integrates process supervision into group relative policy optimization by using an LLM judge to assess retrieval utility and reasoning correctness per round, producing contribution scores that rescale outcome-based advantages for fine-grained credit assignment. Experimental results on knowledge-intensive benchmarks show that CW-GRPO outperforms standard GRPO by 5.0% on Qwen3-8B and 6.3% on Qwen3-1.7B, leading to more effective search behaviors, with analysis revealing that successful trajectories exhibit concentrated contributions in specific rounds.
该论文针对基于大语言模型的搜索智能体训练中的局限性提出改进，其中过程监督存在价值估计不稳定的问题，而结果监督则因稀疏的轨迹级奖励难以进行信用分配。为弥补这一差距，作者提出了贡献加权组相对策略优化框架，通过集成过程监督到组相对策略优化中，利用大语言模型作为评判器评估每轮检索效用和推理正确性，生成贡献分数以重新调整基于结果的优势，实现细粒度信用分配而不牺牲优化稳定性。在多个知识密集型基准测试上的实验表明，CW-GRPO在Qwen3-8B和Qwen3-1.7B模型上分别比标准GRPO性能提升5.0%和6.3%，产生了更有效的搜索行为，分析还显示成功轨迹在特定轮次中贡献集中，为搜索智能体任务提供了实证见解。
Agent-World: Scaling Real-World Environment Synthesis for Evolving General Agent Intelligence
Authors: Guanting Dong, Junting Lu, Junjie Huang, Wanjun Zhong, Longxiang Liu, Shijue Huang, Zhenyu Li, Yang Zhao, Xiaoshuai Song, Xiaoxi Li, Jiajie Jin, Yutao Zhu, Hanbin Wang, Fangyu Lei, Qinyu Luo, Mingyang Chen, Zehui Chen, Jiazhan Feng, Ji-Rong Wen, Zhicheng Dou
First: 2026-04-20T14:01:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T14:01:10+00:00
Comments: Working in progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models are increasingly expected to serve as general-purpose agents that interact with external, stateful tool environments. The Model Context Protocol (MCP) and broader agent skills offer a unified interface for connecting agents with scalable real-world services, but training robust agents remains limited by the lack of realistic environments and principled mechanisms for life-long learning. In this paper, we present \textbf{Agent-World}, a self-evolving training arena for advancing general agent intelligence through scalable environments. Agent-World has two main components: (1) Agentic Environment-Task Discovery, which autonomously explores topic-aligned databases and executable tool ecosystems from thousands of real-world environment themes and synthesizes verifiable tasks with controllable difficulty; and (2) Continuous Self-Evolving Agent Training, which combines multi-environment reinforcement learning with a self-evolving agent arena that automatically identifies capability gaps through dynamic task synthesis and drives targeted learning, enabling the co-evolution of agent policies and environments. Across 23 challenging agent benchmarks, Agent-World-8B and 14B consistently outperforms strong proprietary models and environment scaling baselines. Further analyses reveal scaling trends in relation to environment diversity and self-evolution rounds, offering insights for building general agent intelligence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Agent-World：为进化通用智能体而扩展的真实世界环境合成
大型语言模型日益被期望成为与外部有状态工具环境交互的通用智能体。模型上下文协议（MCP）及更广泛的智能体技能为连接智能体与可扩展的真实世界服务提供了统一接口，但缺乏真实环境和终身学习的机制化方法，限制了鲁棒智能体的训练。本文提出\textbf{Agent-World}，一个通过可扩展环境推进通用智能体智能的自进化训练场。Agent-World包含两个核心组件：（1）智能体化环境-任务发现：从数千个真实世界环境主题中自主探索主题对齐的数据库与可执行工具生态系统，合成具有可控难度的可验证任务；（2）持续自进化智能体训练：结合多环境强化学习与自进化智能体竞技场，通过动态任务合成自动识别能力缺口并驱动针对性学习，实现智能体策略与环境的协同进化。在23个具有挑战性的智能体基准测试中，Agent-World-8B和14B模型持续超越强大的专有模型与环境扩展基线。进一步分析揭示了环境多样性与自进化轮次相关的扩展趋势，为构建通用智能体智能提供了洞见。

FireScope: Wildfire Risk Prediction with a Chain-of-Thought Oracle
Authors: Mario Markov, Stefan Maria Ailuro, Luc Van Gool, Konrad Schindler, Danda Pani Paudel
First: 2025-11-21T11:45:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T13:49:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Predicting wildfire risk is a reasoning-intensive spatial problem that requires the integration of visual, climatic, and geographic factors to infer continuous risk maps. Existing methods lack the causal reasoning and multimodal understanding required for reliable generalization. We introduce $\textbf{FireScope-Bench}$, a large-scale dataset and benchmark that couples Sentinel-2 imagery and climate data with expert-defined risk rasters across the USA, and real wildfire events in Europe for cross-continental evaluation. Building on this dataset, we propose $\textbf{FireScope}$, a VLM-based reasoning-to-generation framework that learns from both reinforcement learning and visual supervision to predict risk rasters with complementary reasoning traces. When trained in the USA and tested in Europe, $\textbf{FireScope}$ achieves substantial performance gains, while expert feedback and automated analysis confirm that its reasoning traces are faithful and semantically meaningful. Our findings demonstrate that reasoning can ground raster prediction models, improving both generalization and interpretability. To our knowledge, this is the first framework to (1) demonstrate that language-based reasoning can improve generalization in visual generation, (2) propose a high-resolution wildfire risk model that can be applied across continents, and (3) enable systematic studies of robust cross-continental generalization for multimodal fire risk models. We believe that $\textbf{FireScope-Bench}$ has the potential to serve as a foundation for advancing reasoning-driven, interpretable and generalizable spatial modeling. Data and source code will be made publicly available.

Style-Based Neural Architectures for Real-Time Weather Classification
Authors: Hamed Ouattara, Pascal Houssam Salmane, Pierre Duthon, Frédéric Bernardin, Omar Ait Aider
Venue: International Conference on Image Analysis (ICIAR 2025) and Recognition
First: 2026-04-20T13:28:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T13:28:24+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 21 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we present three neural network architectures designed for real-time classification of weather conditions (sunny, rain, snow, fog) from images. These models, inspired by recent advances in style transfer, aim to capture the stylistic elements present in images. One model, called "Multi-PatchGAN", is based on PatchGANs used in well-known architectures such as Pix2Pix and CycleGAN, but here adapted with multiple patch sizes for detection tasks. The second model, "Truncated ResNet50", is a simplified version of ResNet50 retaining only its first nine layers. This truncation, determined by an evolutionary algorithm, facilitates the extraction of high-frequency features essential for capturing subtle stylistic details. Finally, we propose "Truncated ResNet50 with Gram Matrix and Attention", which computes Gram matrices for each layer during training and automatically weights them via an attention mechanism, thus optimizing the extraction of the most relevant stylistic expressions for classification. These last two models outperform the state of the art and demonstrate remarkable generalization capability on several public databases. Although developed for weather detection, these architectures are also suitable for other appearance-based classification tasks, such as animal species recognition, texture classification, disease detection in medical imaging, or industrial defect identification.
中文标题/摘要

本文提出三种用于图像天气条件（晴天、雨、雪、雾）实时分类的神经网络架构。这些模型受风格迁移最新进展启发，旨在捕捉图像中的风格化元素。首个模型“多尺度PatchGAN”基于PatchGAN架构（如Pix2Pix和CycleGAN），但采用多尺度图像块以适应检测任务。第二个模型“截断ResNet50”是ResNet50的简化版本，仅保留前九层——该截断方案通过进化算法确定，有助于提取捕获细微风格细节所需的高频特征。最后，我们提出“带Gram矩阵与注意力机制的截断ResNet50”，该模型在训练时计算每层Gram矩阵，并通过注意力机制自动加权，从而优化对分类最相关风格特征的提取。后两种模型在多个公开数据集上超越现有技术，展现出卓越的泛化能力。虽然专为天气检测开发，这些架构也适用于其他基于外观的分类任务，如动物物种识别、纹理分类、医学影像疾病检测或工业缺陷识别。

Experimental results show that the latter two models outperform state-of-the-art approaches and generalize well across public datasets, with potential applications extending to other appearance-based tasks like species recognition and medical imaging.

AJ-Bench: Benchmarking Agent-as-a-Judge for Environment-Aware Evaluation
Authors: Wentao Shi, Yu Wang, Yuyang Zhao, Yuxin Chen, Fuli Feng, Xueyuan Hao, Xi Su, Qi Gu, Hui Su, Xunliang Cai, Xiangnan He
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-20T13:23:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T13:23:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 Findings. 43 pages total, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
As reinforcement learning continues to scale the training of large language model-based agents, reliably verifying agent behaviors in complex environments has become increasingly challenging. Existing approaches rely on rule-based verifiers or LLM-as-a-Judge models, which struggle to generalize beyond narrow domains. Agent-as-a-Judge addresses this limitation by actively interacting with environments and tools to acquire verifiable evidence, yet its capabilities remain underexplored. We introduce a benchmark AJ-Bench to systematically evaluate Agent-as-a-Judge across three domains-search, data systems, and graphical user interfaces-comprising 155 tasks and 516 annotated trajectories. The benchmark comprehensively assesses judge agents' abilities in information acquisition, state verification, and process verification. Experiments demonstrate consistent performance gains over LLM-as-a-Judge baselines, while also revealing substantial open challenges in agent-based verification. Our data and code are available at https://aj-bench.github.io/.

Similarity-based Portfolio Construction for Black-box Optimization
Authors: Catalin-Viorel Dinu, Diederick Vermetten, Carola Doerr
First: 2026-04-20T12:48:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T12:48:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In black-box optimization, a central question is which algorithm to use to solve a given, previously unseen, problem. Selecting a single algorithm, however, entails inherent risks: inaccuracies in the selector may lead to poor choices, and even well-performing algorithms with high variance can yield unsatisfactory results in a single run. A natural remedy is to split the evaluation budget across multiple runs of potentially different algorithms. Such sequential algorithm portfolios benefit from variance reduction and complementarities between algorithms, often outperforming approaches that allocate the entire budget to a single solver. While effective portfolios can be constructed post-hoc, transferring this idea to the algorithm selection setting is non-trivial. We show that a naive portfolio constructed over the full training set already outperforms the strongest traditional baseline, the virtual best solver. We then propose a simple yet effective k-nearest-neighbor-based finetuning approach to construct portfolios tailored to unseen instances, yielding further improvements and highlighting the effectiveness of portfolio selection in fixed-budget black-box optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于相似性的黑盒优化投资组合构建
在黑盒优化中，核心问题是如何选择算法来解决先前未见过的给定问题。然而，选择单一算法存在固有风险：选择器的误差可能导致不良选择，且即使性能良好但方差高的算法在单次运行中也可能产生不理想的结果。一种自然的解决方案是将评估预算分配给多个可能不同算法的运行。这种序列算法投资组合受益于方差减少和算法间的互补性，通常优于将全部预算分配给单一求解器的方法。虽然有效的投资组合可以事后构建，但将此思路迁移到算法选择场景并非易事。我们证明，基于完整训练集构建的朴素投资组合已优于最强的传统基线——虚拟最佳求解器。随后，我们提出一种简单而有效的基于k近邻的微调方法，为未见实例构建定制化投资组合，从而获得进一步改进，并突显了固定预算黑盒优化中投资组合选择的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of selecting a single algorithm for black-box optimization, where such choices risk poor performance due to selector inaccuracies or high variance in algorithm outcomes. To mitigate this, the authors propose constructing sequential algorithm portfolios that allocate the evaluation budget across multiple runs of different algorithms, leveraging variance reduction and complementary strengths. Their method involves a naive portfolio over the full training set, which outperforms the virtual best solver baseline, and a k-nearest-neighbor-based finetuning approach to tailor portfolios to unseen instances, yielding further improvements in fixed-budget optimization.
本文针对黑盒优化中单一算法选择可能因选择器不准确或算法高方差导致性能不佳的问题，提出构建顺序算法组合，将评估预算分配给不同算法的多次运行，以利用方差减少和算法间的互补性。方法包括在完整训练集上构建朴素组合，其表现优于虚拟最佳求解器基线，以及采用基于k近邻的微调方法为未见实例定制组合，从而在固定预算优化中取得进一步性能提升。
ImpRIF: Stronger Implicit Reasoning Leads to Better Complex Instruction Following
Authors: Yuancheng Yang, Lin Yang, Xu Wang, Chao Tong, Haihua Yang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-02-04T07:50:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T12:48:23+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As applications of large language models (LLMs) become increasingly complex, the demand for robust complex instruction following capabilities is growing accordingly. We argue that a thorough understanding of the instruction itself, especially the latent reasoning structure embedded between the lines, is crucial for improving instruction following. Therefore we target complex instructions that involve implicit reasoning, intricate logical relations, and multi-constraint dependencies. We propose ImpRIF, a method to enhance LLMs' understanding of implicit reasoning instructions, thereby improving its ability to follow complex instructions. We formalize such instructions as verifiable reasoning graphs, enabling programmatic verification and graph-driven chain-of-thought reasoning. Based on this formulation, we synthesize large-scale single- and multi-turn data, propose fine-tuning with graph reasoning, and apply reinforcement learning to explicitly train models to reason along the graph. On five complex instruction following benchmarks, our models substantially outperform their base models. These results demonstrate that enhancing implicit reasoning capabilities can significantly improve complex instruction following.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ImpRIF：更强的隐式推理能力提升复杂指令跟随性能
随着大语言模型（LLMs）的应用日益复杂，对鲁棒的复杂指令跟随能力的需求也相应增长。我们认为，深入理解指令本身，尤其是隐藏在字里行间的潜在推理结构，对于提升指令跟随能力至关重要。因此，我们聚焦于涉及隐式推理、复杂逻辑关系和多约束依赖的复杂指令。我们提出ImpRIF方法，旨在增强LLMs对隐式推理指令的理解，从而提升其遵循复杂指令的能力。我们将此类指令形式化为可验证的推理图，支持程序化验证和图驱动的思维链推理。基于此形式化框架，我们合成了大规模的单轮与多轮数据，提出结合图推理的微调方法，并应用强化学习显式训练模型沿图进行推理。在五个复杂指令跟随基准测试中，我们的模型显著超越了其基础模型。这些结果表明，增强隐式推理能力能有效提升复杂指令跟随性能。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is the growing need for large language models (LLMs) to robustly follow complex instructions, which often contain implicit reasoning, intricate logic, and multiple constraints. The proposed method, ImpRIF, formalizes such instructions as verifiable reasoning graphs to enable programmatic verification and graph-driven chain-of-thought reasoning; it then synthesizes large-scale data and employs fine-tuning with graph reasoning combined with reinforcement learning to explicitly train models to reason along these graphs. The main experimental results show that models trained with ImpRIF substantially outperform their base models across five complex instruction following benchmarks, demonstrating that enhancing implicit reasoning capabilities significantly improves performance on this task.
本研究的动机是，随着应用日益复杂，大型语言模型需要更稳健地遵循包含隐式推理、复杂逻辑关系和多重约束的复杂指令。为此提出的方法ImpRIF将此类指令形式化为可验证的推理图，以实现程序化验证和图驱动的思维链推理；基于此形式化，该方法合成了大规模单轮和多轮数据，提出了结合图推理的微调，并应用强化学习来显式训练模型沿图进行推理。主要实验结果表明，在五个复杂指令遵循基准测试中，经ImpRIF训练的模型显著优于其基础模型，这证明增强隐式推理能力能有效提升复杂指令遵循性能。
QuantumQA: Enhancing Scientific Reasoning via Physics-Consistent Dataset and Verification-Aware Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Songxin Qu, Tai-Ping Sun, Yun-Jie Wang, Huan-Yu Liu, Cheng Xue, Xiao-Fan Xu, Han Fang, Yang Yang, Yu-Chun Wu, Guo-Ping Guo, Zhao-Yun Chen
First: 2026-04-20T12:33:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T12:33:50+00:00
Comments: 25 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) show strong capabilities in general reasoning but typically lack reliability in scientific domains like quantum mechanics, which demand strict adherence to physical constraints. This limitation arises from the scarcity of verifiable training resources and the inadequacy of coarse feedback signals in standard alignment paradigms. To address the data challenge, we introduce QuantumQA, a large-scale dataset constructed via a task-adaptive strategy and a hybrid verification protocol that combines deterministic solvers with semantic auditing to guarantee scientific rigor. Building on this foundation, we propose the verification-aware reward model (VRM) tailored for Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), which employs an adaptive reward fusion (ARF) mechanism to dynamically integrate deterministic signals from a scientific execution suite (SES) with multidimensional semantic evaluations for precise supervision. Experimental results demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms baselines and general-purpose preference models. Notably, our optimized 8B model achieves performance competitive with proprietary models, validating that incorporating verifiable, rule-based feedback into the reinforcement learning loop offers a parameter-efficient alternative to pure scaling.

标题：QuantumQA：通过物理一致性数据集与验证感知强化学习增强科学推理能力
大语言模型在通用推理方面展现出强大能力，但在量子力学等科学领域通常缺乏可靠性，这些领域要求严格遵守物理约束。这一局限性源于可验证训练资源的稀缺性，以及标准对齐范式中粗粒度反馈信号的不足。为解决数据挑战，我们提出了QuantumQA——一个通过任务自适应策略构建的大规模数据集，采用结合确定性求解器与语义审计的混合验证协议，确保科学严谨性。在此基础上，我们提出专为可验证奖励强化学习设计的验证感知奖励模型，该模型采用自适应奖励融合机制，动态整合来自科学执行套件的确定性信号与多维度语义评估，实现精准监督。实验结果表明，我们的方法持续优于基线模型和通用偏好模型。值得注意的是，我们优化的80亿参数模型达到了与专有模型相竞争的性能，验证了将可验证的、基于规则的反馈纳入强化学习循环，为纯扩展提供了参数高效的替代方案。

Reinforced Efficient Reasoning via Semantically Diverse Exploration
Authors: Ziqi Zhao, Zhaochun Ren, Jiahong Zou, Liu Yang, Zhiwei Xu, Xuri Ge, Zhumin Chen, Xinyu Ma, Daiting Shi, Shuaiqiang Wang, Dawei Yin, Xin Xin
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-08T15:56:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T12:27:51+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ACL 2026 Main
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has proven effective in enhancing the reasoning of large language models (LLMs). Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS)-based extensions improve upon vanilla RLVR (e.g., GRPO) by providing tree-based reasoning rollouts that enable fine-grained and segment-level credit assignment. However, existing methods still suffer from limited exploration diversity and inefficient reasoning. To address the above challenges, we propose reinforced efficient reasoning via semantically diverse explorations, i.e., ROSE, for LLMs. To encourage more diverse reasoning exploration, our method incorporates a semantic-entropy-based branching strategy and an $\varepsilon$-exploration mechanism. The former operates on already sampled reasoning rollouts to capture semantic uncertainty and select branching points with high semantic divergence to generate new successive reasoning paths, whereas the latter stochastically initiates reasoning rollouts from the root, preventing the search process from becoming overly local. To improve efficiency, we design a length-aware segment-level advantage estimator that rewards concise and correct reasoning while penalizing unnecessarily long reasoning chains. Extensive experiments on various mathematical reasoning benchmarks with Qwen and Llama models validate the effectiveness and efficiency of ROSE. Codes are available at https://github.com/ZiqiZhao1/ROSE-rl.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于语义多样性探索的强化高效推理
可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已被证明能有效提升大语言模型（LLM）的推理能力。基于蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）的扩展方法（如GRPO）通过提供树状推理推演，实现了细粒度和片段级的信用分配，改进了基础RLVR。然而，现有方法仍存在探索多样性有限和推理效率低下的问题。为解决这些挑战，我们提出了面向LLM的基于语义多样性探索的强化高效推理方法——ROSE。为促进更多样化的推理探索，本方法融合了基于语义熵的分支策略和ε-探索机制：前者基于已采样的推理推演捕获语义不确定性，选择语义分歧度高的分支点生成新的连续推理路径；后者随机从根节点启动推理推演，避免搜索过程过度局部化。为提升效率，我们设计了长度感知的片段级优势估计器，对简洁正确的推理给予奖励，同时对冗余的推理链进行惩罚。基于Qwen和Llama模型在多项数学推理基准上的大量实验验证了ROSE的有效性与高效性。代码发布于https://github.com/ZiqiZhao1/ROSE-rl。

The paper addresses the limitations of existing reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) methods, such as limited exploration diversity and inefficient reasoning in large language models (LLMs). It proposes ROSE, a method that enhances exploration through a semantic-entropy-based branching strategy and an ε-exploration mechanism to generate diverse reasoning paths, while improving efficiency with a length-aware segment-level advantage estimator that rewards concise correct reasoning. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks with Qwen and Llama models demonstrate the effectiveness and efficiency of ROSE in improving reasoning performance.
本文针对现有基于可验证奖励的强化学习方法在大语言模型中存在的探索多样性不足和推理效率低下的问题，提出了ROSE方法。该方法通过基于语义熵的分支策略和ε探索机制来增强探索，生成多样化的推理路径，同时利用长度感知的片段级优势估计器奖励简洁正确的推理以提高效率。在Qwen和Llama模型上的多个数学推理基准测试实验验证了ROSE的有效性和高效性。
Does "Do Differentiable Simulators Give Better Policy Gradients?'' Give Better Policy Gradients?
Authors: Ku Onoda, Paavo Parmas, Manato Yaguchi, Yutaka Matsuo
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-04-20T12:23:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T12:23:48+00:00
Comments: ICLR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In policy gradient reinforcement learning, access to a differentiable model enables 1st-order gradient estimation that accelerates learning compared to relying solely on derivative-free 0th-order estimators. However, discontinuous dynamics cause bias and undermine the effectiveness of 1st-order estimators. Prior work addressed this bias by constructing a confidence interval around the REINFORCE 0th-order gradient estimator and using these bounds to detect discontinuities. However, the REINFORCE estimator is notoriously noisy, and we find that this method requires task-specific hyperparameter tuning and has low sample efficiency. This paper asks whether such bias is the primary obstacle and what minimal fixes suffice. First, we re-examine standard discontinuous settings from prior work and introduce DDCG, a lightweight test that switches estimators in nonsmooth regions; with a single hyperparameter, DDCG achieves robust performance and remains reliable with small samples. Second, on differentiable robotics control tasks, we present IVW-H, a per-step inverse-variance implementation that stabilizes variance without explicit discontinuity detection and yields strong results. Together, these findings indicate that while estimator switching improves robustness in controlled studies, careful variance control often dominates in practical deployments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：“可微分模拟器能否提供更优的策略梯度？”真的能提供更优策略梯度吗？
在策略梯度强化学习中，相比仅依赖无导数的零阶估计器，可微分模型能通过一阶梯度估计加速学习。然而，动力学的不连续性会导致偏差，削弱一阶估计器的有效性。先前研究通过围绕REINFORCE零阶梯度估计器构建置信区间，并利用这些边界检测不连续性来解决偏差问题。但REINFORCE估计器噪声显著，且该方法需要任务特定的超参数调优，样本效率较低。本文探讨此类偏差是否为主要障碍，以及何种最小化修正方案足够有效。首先，我们重新检验先前研究中的标准不连续场景，并提出DDCG——一种在非平滑区域切换估计器的轻量级测试方法；仅需单一超参数，DDCG即能实现鲁棒性能，并在小样本下保持可靠性。其次，在可微分机器人控制任务中，我们提出IVW-H——一种逐步逆方差加权实现方法，无需显式不连续性检测即可稳定方差，并获得优异结果。综合表明：在受控研究中，估计器切换能提升鲁棒性；而在实际部署中，精细的方差控制往往更具决定性作用。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether the primary challenge in using differentiable simulators for policy gradients is bias from discontinuous dynamics, as previously suggested, and explores minimal solutions. The authors first re-examine standard discontinuous settings and propose DDCG, a lightweight method that switches between gradient estimators in nonsmooth regions; DDCG requires only one hyperparameter, demonstrates robust performance, and maintains reliability with small sample sizes. Second, on differentiable robotics control tasks, they introduce IVW-H, a per-step inverse-variance weighting implementation that stabilizes variance without explicit discontinuity detection and yields strong results. Overall, the findings indicate that while estimator switching enhances robustness in controlled studies, careful variance control is often more critical in practical deployments.
本文探讨了在使用可微分模拟器进行策略梯度优化时，不连续动态引起的偏差是否是主要障碍，并研究了最小化解决方案。作者首先重新审视了先前工作中的标准不连续设置，提出了DDCG方法，该方法在非平滑区域切换梯度估计器，仅需一个超参数，即表现出鲁棒性能并在小样本下保持可靠。其次，在可微分机器人控制任务中，他们引入了IVW-H，一种基于每步逆方差加权的实现，无需显式检测不连续性即可稳定方差并获得优异结果。总体而言，研究结果表明，在受控研究中估计器切换能提升鲁棒性，但在实际部署中，精细的方差控制往往更为关键。
Distributional Off-Policy Evaluation with Deep Quantile Process Regression
Authors: Qi Kuang, Chao Wang, Yuling Jiao, Fan Zhou
First: 2026-04-20T12:07:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T12:07:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper investigates the off-policy evaluation (OPE) problem from a distributional perspective. Rather than focusing solely on the expectation of the total return, as in most existing OPE methods, we aim to estimate the entire return distribution. To this end, we introduce a quantile-based approach for OPE using deep quantile process regression, presenting a novel algorithm called Deep Quantile Process regression-based Off-Policy Evaluation (DQPOPE). We provide new theoretical insights into the deep quantile process regression technique, extending existing approaches that estimate discrete quantiles to estimate a continuous quantile function. A key contribution of our work is the rigorous sample complexity analysis for distributional OPE with deep neural networks, bridging theoretical analysis with practical algorithmic implementations. We show that DQPOPE achieves statistical advantages by estimating the full return distribution using the same sample size required to estimate a single policy value using conventional methods. Empirical studies further show that DQPOPE provides significantly more precise and robust policy value estimates than standard methods, thereby enhancing the practical applicability and effectiveness of distributional reinforcement learning approaches.

标题：基于深度分位数过程回归的分布式离策略评估
本文从分布视角研究离策略评估问题。与现有多数仅关注总回报期望的方法不同，我们旨在估计完整的回报分布。为此，我们提出一种基于分位数的深度分位数过程回归方法，并设计了名为DQPOPE的新算法。我们为深度分位数过程回归技术提供了新的理论见解，将离散分位数估计扩展为连续分位数函数估计。本工作的核心贡献在于对深度神经网络分布式离策略评估进行了严格的样本复杂度分析，搭建了理论分析与算法实践的桥梁。研究表明，DQPOPE仅需传统方法估计单一策略值所需的样本量，即可获得完整回报分布的统计优势。实证分析进一步表明，DQPOPE能提供比标准方法更精确、更稳健的策略值估计，从而提升分布强化学习方法在实际应用中的有效性与适用性。

The proposed method, Deep Quantile Process regression-based Off-Policy Evaluation (DQPOPE), leverages deep quantile process regression to estimate a continuous quantile function, extending prior discrete quantile approaches and supported by novel theoretical insights and a rigorous sample complexity analysis for deep networks.
