本文的动机是超越传统离策略评估（OPE）中对回报期望的点估计，转而捕捉回报的完整分布不确定性。方法上，提出了基于深度分位数过程回归的离策略评估算法（DQPOPE），利用深度分位数过程回归来估计连续的分位数函数，扩展了现有离散分位数方法，并提供了新的理论分析和针对深度网络的严格样本复杂度论证。主要实验结果表明，DQPOPE相比标准方法能提供更精确、更稳健的策略价值估计，在仅需传统方法估计单个期望值所需的样本量下，即可实现对整个回报分布的估计，从而提升了分布强化学习方法的实际适用性和有效性。
Evidence-Augmented Policy Optimization with Reward Co-Evolution for Long-Context Reasoning
Authors: Xin Guan, Zijian Li, Shen Huang, Pengjun Xie, Jingren Zhou, Jiuxin Cao
First: 2026-01-15T11:40:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T12:01:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While Reinforcement Learning (RL) has advanced LLM reasoning, applying it to long-context scenarios is hindered by sparsity of outcome rewards. This limitation fails to penalize ungrounded "lucky guesses," leaving the critical process of needle-in-a-haystack evidence retrieval largely unsupervised. To address this, we propose EAPO (Evidence-Augmented Policy Optimization). We first establish the Evidence-Augmented Reasoning paradigm, validating via Tree-Structured Evidence Sampling that precise evidence extraction is the decisive bottleneck for long-context reasoning. Guided by this insight, EAPO introduces a specialized RL algorithm where a reward model computes a Group-Relative Evidence Reward, providing dense process supervision to explicitly improve evidence quality. To sustain accurate supervision throughout training, we further incorporate an Adaptive Reward-Policy Co-Evolution mechanism. This mechanism iteratively refines the reward model using outcome-consistent rollouts, sharpening its discriminative capability to ensure precise process guidance. Comprehensive evaluations across eight benchmarks demonstrate that EAPO significantly enhances long-context reasoning performance compared to SOTA baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于证据增强策略优化与奖励协同进化的长上下文推理方法
尽管强化学习（RL）推动了大型语言模型（LLM）的推理能力，但其在长上下文场景中的应用受限于结果奖励的稀疏性。这一局限无法有效惩罚缺乏依据的'侥幸猜测'，导致关键的'大海捞针'式证据检索过程缺乏监督。为此，我们提出EAPO（证据增强策略优化）方法。首先建立证据增强推理范式，通过树状结构证据抽样验证精确证据提取是长上下文推理的关键瓶颈。基于此发现，EAPO设计了一种专用RL算法：通过奖励模型计算群体相对证据奖励，提供密集的过程监督以显式提升证据质量。为维持训练全程的精准监督，我们进一步引入自适应奖励-策略协同进化机制，该机制利用结果一致的推演轨迹迭代优化奖励模型，增强其判别能力以确保精确的过程指导。在八个基准测试上的综合评估表明，相较于最先进基线方法，EAPO显著提升了长上下文推理性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of sparse outcome rewards in Reinforcement Learning for long-context reasoning with large language models, which fails to supervise the critical evidence retrieval process and may reward ungrounded guesses. The proposed method, Evidence-Augmented Policy Optimization (EAPO), first establishes an Evidence-Augmented Reasoning paradigm, identifying precise evidence extraction as the key bottleneck. It then introduces a specialized RL algorithm using a reward model to compute a dense Group-Relative Evidence Reward for process supervision, coupled with an Adaptive Reward-Policy Co-Evolution mechanism that iteratively refines the reward model using outcome-consistent rollouts to maintain accurate guidance. Experimental results across eight benchmarks show that EAPO significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in long-context reasoning performance.
本文针对大语言模型长上下文推理中强化学习结果奖励稀疏的问题，该问题无法监督关键的证据检索过程并可能奖励无根据的猜测。提出的方法，即证据增强策略优化（EAPO），首先建立了证据增强推理范式，确定精确证据提取是关键瓶颈。随后引入一种专门的强化学习算法，使用奖励模型计算密集的组相对证据奖励以进行过程监督，并结合自适应奖励-策略协同进化机制，该机制利用结果一致的轨迹迭代优化奖励模型以保持精确指导。在八个基准测试上的综合评估表明，EAPO在长上下文推理性能上显著优于现有最先进的基线方法。
Semantic-Space Exploration and Exploitation in RLVR for LLM Reasoning
Authors: Fanding Huang, Guanbo Huang, Xiao Fan, Yi He, Xiao Liang, Xiao Chen, Qinting Jiang, Faisal Nadeem Khan, Jingyan Jiang, Zhi Wang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-09-28T11:14:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T11:06:36+00:00
Comments: Accepted as an ACL 2026 Findings paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for LLM reasoning is often framed as balancing exploration and exploitation in action space, typically operationalized with token-level proxies (e.g., output entropy or confidence). We argue that this apparent trade-off is largely a measurement artifact: token-level statistics reflect next-token uncertainty rather than how reasoning progresses over multi-token semantic structures. We therefore study exploration and exploitation in the hidden-state space of response trajectories. We use Effective Rank (ER) to quantify representational exploration and introduce its temporal derivatives, Effective Rank Velocity (ERV) and Effective Rank Acceleration (ERA), to characterize exploitative refinement dynamics. Empirically and theoretically, ER and ERV exhibit near-zero correlation in semantic space, suggesting the two capacities can be improved simultaneously. Motivated by this, we propose Velocity-Exploiting Rank Learning (VERL), which shapes the RLVR advantage with an auxiliary signal derived from ER/ERV and uses the more stable ERA as a meta-control variable to adaptively balance the incentives. Across multiple base models, RLVR algorithms, and reasoning benchmarks, VERL yields consistent improvements, including large gains on challenging tasks (e.g., 21.4\% in Gaokao 2024). The code is available at https://github.com/hf618/VERL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大语言模型推理的RLVR语义空间探索与利用研究
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在大语言模型推理中常被视作动作空间中探索与利用的权衡问题，通常通过词元级代理指标（如输出熵或置信度）实现。我们认为这种表面权衡主要是测量假象：词元级统计量反映的是下一词元的不确定性，而非推理在多词元语义结构中的演进过程。为此，我们研究响应轨迹隐状态空间中的探索与利用机制。采用有效秩量化表征探索，并引入其时间导数——有效秩速度与有效秩加速度——刻画利用性精炼动态。实证与理论分析表明，语义空间中有效秩与有效秩速度呈现近零相关性，揭示两种能力可同步提升。基于此，我们提出速度利用秩学习算法，通过有效秩/有效秩速度衍生的辅助信号塑造RLVR优势函数，并采用更稳定的有效秩加速度作为元控制变量自适应平衡激励权重。在多种基模型、RLVR算法与推理基准测试中，该算法均取得稳定提升，尤其在挑战性任务上表现显著（如2024年高考题提升21.4%）。代码已开源：https://github.com/hf618/VERL。
Summary / 总结
This paper challenges the conventional framing of exploration-exploitation in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for LLMs, arguing that token-level proxies are measurement artifacts that fail to capture reasoning progress over semantic structures. The authors propose analyzing these dynamics in the hidden-state space of response trajectories, quantifying exploration via Effective Rank (ER) and exploitative refinement via its temporal derivatives, ERV and ERA. Their key finding is that ER and ERV are nearly uncorrelated in semantic space, indicating these capacities can be improved simultaneously, which motivates their method, Velocity-Exploiting Rank Learning (VERL). VERL shapes the RLVR advantage with an auxiliary signal from ER/ERV and uses ERA for adaptive balancing, leading to consistent performance gains across models and benchmarks, including a 21.4% improvement on the challenging Gaokao 2024 task.
本文对大型语言模型推理中可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）的探索-利用权衡的传统框架提出挑战，认为词元级代理指标是测量伪影，无法捕捉语义结构上的推理进展。作者提出在响应轨迹的隐藏状态空间中分析这些动态，使用有效秩（ER）量化探索，并使用其时间导数ERV和ERA量化利用性精炼动态。关键发现是，在语义空间中ER和ERV几乎不相关，表明这两种能力可以同时提升，这启发了他们提出的方法——速度利用秩学习（VERL）。VERL利用来自ER/ERV的辅助信号塑造RLVR优势函数，并使用ERA进行自适应平衡，从而在多个基础模型、RLVR算法和推理基准上取得了一致的性能提升，包括在具有挑战性的2024年高考任务上实现了21.4%的显著增益。
SCALER:Synthetic Scalable Adaptive Learning Environment for Reasoning
Authors: Caijun Xu, Changyi Xiao, Zhongyuan Peng, Xinrun Wang, Yixin Cao
First: 2026-01-08T10:42:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T09:53:19+00:00
Comments: 22 pages,5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) offers a principled way to enhance the reasoning capabilities of large language models, yet its effectiveness hinges on training signals that remain informative as models evolve. In practice, RL progress often slows when task difficulty becomes poorly aligned with model capability, or when training is dominated by a narrow set of recurring problem patterns. To jointly address these issues, we propose SCALER (Synthetic sCalable Adaptive Learning Environment for Reasoning), a framework that sustains effective learning signals through adaptive environment design. SCALER introduces a scalable synthesis pipeline that converts real-world programming problems into verifiable reasoning environments with controllable difficulty and unbounded instance generation, enabling RL training beyond finite datasets while preserving strong correctness guarantees. Building on this, SCALER further employs an adaptive multi-environment RL strategy that dynamically adjusts instance difficulty and curates the active set of environments to track the model's capability frontier and maintain distributional diversity. This co-adaptation prevents reward sparsity, mitigates overfitting to narrow task patterns, and supports sustained improvement throughout training. Extensive experiments show that SCALER consistently outperforms dataset-based RL baselines across diverse reasoning benchmarks and exhibits more stable, long-horizon training dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SCALER：面向推理的合成可扩展自适应学习环境
强化学习为提升大语言模型的推理能力提供了原则性方法，但其有效性依赖于随模型演化保持信息量的训练信号。实践中，当任务难度与模型能力不匹配，或训练被少数重复问题模式主导时，强化学习进展常会放缓。为协同解决这些问题，我们提出SCALER（面向推理的合成可扩展自适应学习环境），该框架通过自适应环境设计维持有效的学习信号。SCALER引入可扩展的合成流程，将真实编程问题转化为具有可控难度和无限实例生成能力的可验证推理环境，使强化学习训练突破有限数据集限制，同时保持强正确性保证。在此基础上，SCALER进一步采用自适应多环境强化学习策略，动态调整实例难度并精选活跃环境集合，以追踪模型能力边界并维持分布多样性。这种协同适应机制避免了奖励稀疏性，缓解了对狭窄任务模式的过拟合，支持训练过程中的持续改进。大量实验表明，SCALER在多样化推理基准测试中持续优于基于数据集的强化学习基线，并展现出更稳定、长周期的训练动态。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge that reinforcement learning (RL) for improving large language models often suffers from diminishing training signals when task difficulty mismatches model capability or when training data lacks diversity. To address this, the authors propose SCALER, a framework that creates a synthetic, scalable learning environment by converting real-world programming problems into verifiable reasoning tasks with controllable difficulty and unlimited instance generation, ensuring correctness. The method further employs an adaptive multi-environment RL strategy that dynamically adjusts difficulty and curates environments to match the model's evolving capability and maintain diversity. Experimental results demonstrate that SCALER consistently outperforms dataset-based RL baselines across various reasoning benchmarks, showing more stable and sustained training progress.
本文的动机在于，用于提升大语言模型推理能力的强化学习常因任务难度与模型能力不匹配或训练数据缺乏多样性而导致训练信号减弱。为解决此问题，作者提出了SCALER框架，该框架通过将现实编程问题转化为可验证的推理任务，构建了一个可扩展的合成学习环境，其中难度可控且能无限生成实例，确保了正确性。方法进一步采用自适应多环境强化学习策略，动态调整难度并筛选环境，以匹配模型能力前沿并保持分布多样性。实验结果表明，SCALER在多种推理基准测试中持续优于基于数据集的强化学习基线，展现出更稳定、持久的训练动态。
RASP-Tuner: Retrieval-Augmented Soft Prompts for Context-Aware Black-Box Optimization in Non-Stationary Environments
Authors: Enze Pan
Venue: ICML
First: 2026-04-20T09:52:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T09:52:36+00:00
Comments: Withdraw by ICML and prepare for NeurIPS or ICLR
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many deployed systems expose black-box objectives whose minimizing configuration shifts with an externally observed context. When contexts revisit a small set of latent regimes, an optimizer that discards history pays repeated adaptation cost; when each step must remain inexpensive, full Gaussian-process (GP) refits at high observation counts are difficult to sustain. We cast online tuning as context-conditioned regret minimization and present RASP-Tuner, which instantiates a decomposition motivated by first principles: (i) identify a regime proxy by retrieving similar past contexts; (ii) predict short-horizon loss with a mixture-of-experts surrogate whose input concatenates parameters, context, and a retrieved soft prompt; (iii) adapt chiefly in a low-dimensional prompt subspace, invoking full surrogate updates only when scalarized error or disagreement spikes. A RealErrorComposer maps heterogeneous streaming metrics to [0,1] via EMA-stabilized logistic scores, supplying a single differentiable training target. On nine synthetic non-stationary benchmarks, an adversarial-context sanity check, and three tabular real-world streams (Section on real-world experiments), RASP-Tuner improves or matches cumulative regret relative to our GP-UCB and CMA-ES implementations on seven of nine synthetic tasks under paired tests at horizon T=100, while recording 8-12 times lower wall-clock per step than sliding-window GP-UCB on identical hardware. Idealized analysis in a cluster-separated, strongly convex regime model (RA-GD) supplies sufficient conditions for bounded dynamic regret; the deployed pipeline violates several of these premises, and we articulate which gaps remain open.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RASP-Tuner：面向非平稳环境中上下文感知黑盒优化的检索增强软提示
许多已部署系统存在黑盒目标函数，其最小化配置会随外部观测到的上下文发生偏移。当上下文重复访问少量潜在状态时，丢弃历史记录的优化器需反复支付适应成本；当每一步必须保持低成本时，在高观测次数下进行完整高斯过程（GP）重拟合难以持续。我们将在线调优建模为上下文条件遗憾最小化问题，提出RASP-Tuner方法。该方法基于第一性原理实现分解：（1）通过检索相似历史上下文识别状态代理；（2）使用专家混合代理模型预测短期损失，其输入为参数、上下文及检索到的软提示的拼接；（3）主要在低维提示子空间进行适应，仅在标量化误差或分歧激增时触发完整代理更新。RealErrorComposer通过EMA稳定逻辑分数将异构流式指标映射至[0,1]区间，提供单一可微训练目标。在九个合成非平稳基准测试、对抗上下文完整性检验及三个真实世界表格数据流实验中，RASP-Tuner在T=100时间跨度的配对测试中，于七项合成任务上实现优于或匹配GP-UCB与CMA-ES实现的累积遗憾，同时在相同硬件上单步耗时较滑动窗口GP-UCB降低8-12倍。基于聚类分离强凸状态模型（RA-GD）的理想化分析为有界动态遗憾提供了充分条件；实际部署流程违反其中若干前提，我们明确了尚未解决的理论缺口。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of optimizing black-box systems with objectives that shift based on external contexts, particularly in non-stationary environments where reusing past data can reduce adaptation costs. The method, RASP-Tuner, decomposes the problem by retrieving similar past contexts to identify regimes, predicting loss with a mixture-of-experts surrogate that incorporates parameters, context, and a retrieved soft prompt, and adapting primarily in a low-dimensional prompt subspace to maintain efficiency. Experimental results on synthetic benchmarks and real-world data streams show that RASP-Tuner matches or improves cumulative regret compared to GP-UCB and CMA-ES in most tasks, while achieving 8-12 times faster per-step computation than sliding-window GP-UCB, with theoretical analysis providing conditions for bounded dynamic regret.
该论文针对非平稳环境中目标随外部上下文变化而漂移的黑箱系统优化问题，旨在通过复用历史数据降低重复适应成本。方法RASP-Tuner将问题分解为：检索相似历史上下文以识别状态，使用结合参数、上下文和检索软提示的专家混合代理预测损失，并在低维提示子空间中进行主要适应以保持效率。在合成基准和真实世界数据流上的实验表明，RASP-Tuner在多数任务中匹配或优于GP-UCB和CMA-ES的累积遗憾，同时每步计算速度比滑动窗口GP-UCB快8-12倍，理论分析为有界动态遗憾提供了条件。
SELF-EMO: Emotional Self-Evolution from Recognition to Consistent Expression
Authors: Shaowei Zhang, Faqiang Qian, Yan Chen, Ziliang Wang, Kang An, Yong Dai, Mengya Gao, Yichao Wu
First: 2026-04-20T09:27:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T09:27:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Emotion Recognition in Conversation (ERC) has become a fundamental capability for large language models (LLMs) in human-centric interaction. Beyond accurate recognition, coherent emotional expression is also crucial, yet both are limited by the scarcity and static nature of high-quality annotated data. In this work, we propose SELF-EMO, a self-evolution framework grounded in the hypothesis that better emotion prediction leads to more consistent emotional responses. We introduce two auxiliary tasks, emotional understanding and emotional expression, and design a role-based self-play paradigm where the model acts as both an emotion recognizer and a dialogue responder. Through iterative interactions, the model generates diverse conversational trajectories, enabling scalable data generation. To ensure quality, we adopt a data flywheel mechanism that filters candidate predictions and responses using a smoothed IoU-based reward and feeds selected samples back for continuous self-improvement without external supervision. We further develop SELF-GRPO, a reinforcement learning algorithm that stabilizes optimization with multi-label alignment rewards and group-level consistency signals. Experiments on IEMOCAP, MELD, and EmoryNLP show that SELF-EMO achieves state-of-the-art performance, improving accuracy by +6.33% on Qwen3-4B and +8.54% on Qwen3-8B, demonstrating strong effectiveness and generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SELF-EMO：从情感到表达一致性的自我演进
对话情感识别已成为大语言模型在人本交互中的基础能力。除准确识别外，连贯的情感表达同样关键，但两者均受限于高质量标注数据的稀缺性与静态性。本研究提出SELF-EMO，该自我演进框架基于“更优情感预测可催生更一致情感响应”的假设。我们引入情感理解与情感表达两项辅助任务，设计基于角色的自我博弈范式，使模型同时担任情感识别器与对话响应者。通过迭代交互，模型生成多样化对话轨迹，实现可扩展的数据生成。为确保质量，采用数据飞轮机制：基于平滑IoU奖励筛选候选预测与响应，并将优选样本反馈至系统以达成无外部监督的持续自优化。进一步提出SELF-GRPO强化学习算法，通过多标签对齐奖励与组级一致性信号稳定优化过程。在IEMOCAP、MELD及EmoryNLP数据集上的实验表明，SELF-EMO取得最先进性能，在Qwen3-4B与Qwen3-8B模型上分别提升准确率6.33%与8.54%，展现出强效性与泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of static, scarce annotated data for both emotion recognition and coherent emotional expression in conversational AI, this paper introduces SELF-EMO, a self-evolution framework. The method is based on the hypothesis that improved emotion prediction enables more consistent emotional responses; it employs a role-based self-play paradigm where the model acts as both an emotion recognizer and a dialogue responder to generate diverse conversational data. A data flywheel mechanism filters outputs using a smoothed IoU-based reward for quality, and a reinforcement learning algorithm, SELF-GRPO, is developed for stable optimization. Experimental results on IEMOCAP, MELD, and EmoryNLP datasets demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, with accuracy improvements of +6.33% on Qwen3-4B and +8.54% on Qwen3-8B, showcasing strong effectiveness and generalization.
本文的动机是解决对话AI中情感识别和连贯情感表达所面临的静态、高质量标注数据稀缺的局限。为此，提出了SELF-EMO自进化框架，其核心假设是更好的情感预测能带来更一致的情感响应；方法上采用基于角色的自博弈范式，让模型同时扮演情感识别器和对话响应者，以生成多样化的对话数据，并通过基于平滑IoU奖励的数据飞轮机制筛选高质量样本，同时开发了SELF-GRPO强化学习算法进行稳定优化。在IEMOCAP、MELD和EmoryNLP数据集上的主要实验结果表明，该方法达到了最先进的性能，在Qwen3-4B和Qwen3-8B模型上分别提升了+6.33%和+8.54%的准确率，证明了其有效性和良好的泛化能力。
Neural Garbage Collection: Learning to Forget while Learning to Reason
Authors: Michael Y. Li, Jubayer Ibn Hamid, Emily B. Fox, Noah D. Goodman
First: 2026-04-20T09:26:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T09:26:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Chain-of-thought reasoning has driven striking advances in language model capability, yet every reasoning step grows the KV cache, creating a bottleneck to scaling this paradigm further. Current approaches manage these constraints on the model's behalf using hand-designed criteria. A more scalable approach would let end-to-end learning subsume this design choice entirely, following a broader pattern in deep learning. After all, if a model can learn to reason, why can't it learn to forget? We introduce Neural Garbage Collection (NGC), in which a language model learns to forget while learning to reason, trained end-to-end from outcome-based task reward alone. As the model reasons, it periodically pauses, decides which KV cache entries to evict, and continues to reason conditioned on the remaining cache. By treating tokens in a chain-of-thought and cache-eviction decisions as discrete actions sampled from the language model, we can use reinforcement learning to jointly optimize how the model reasons and how it manages its own memory: what the model evicts shapes what it remembers, what it remembers shapes its reasoning, and the correctness of that reasoning determines its reward. Crucially, the model learns this behavior entirely from a single learning signal - the outcome-based task reward - without supervised fine-tuning or proxy objectives. On Countdown, AMC, and AIME tasks, NGC maintains strong accuracy relative to the full-cache upper bound at 2-3x peak KV cache size compression and substantially outperforms eviction baselines. Our results are a first step towards a broader vision where end-to-end optimization drives both capability and efficiency in language models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：神经垃圾回收：在学习推理中学会遗忘
思维链推理推动了语言模型能力的显著进步，但每个推理步骤都会增加键值缓存，成为进一步扩展该范式的瓶颈。现有方法通过人工设计的标准代表模型管理这些约束。更具扩展性的方法是让端到端学习完全涵盖这一设计选择，遵循深度学习的更广泛模式。毕竟，如果模型能学会推理，为何不能学会遗忘？我们提出神经垃圾回收（NGC），使语言模型在学习推理的同时学会遗忘，仅基于结果导向的任务奖励进行端到端训练。模型在推理过程中定期暂停，决定驱逐哪些键值缓存条目，并基于剩余缓存继续推理。通过将思维链中的标记和缓存驱逐决策视为语言模型采样的离散动作，我们可以使用强化学习联合优化模型的推理方式和内存管理策略：模型的驱逐行为决定其记忆内容，记忆内容塑造其推理过程，而推理的正确性决定其奖励。关键在于，模型完全从单一学习信号——结果导向的任务奖励——中习得此行为，无需监督微调或代理目标。在Countdown、AMC和AIME任务中，NGC在实现2-3倍峰值键值缓存压缩的同时，仍保持接近全缓存上限的较高准确率，显著优于基线驱逐方法。我们的成果是迈向更广阔愿景的第一步：通过端到端优化共同驱动语言模型的能力与效率。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the scaling bottleneck caused by the growing KV cache in chain-of-thought reasoning for language models, where current hand-designed cache management methods lack scalability. The method, Neural Garbage Collection (NGC), enables a language model to learn both reasoning and cache eviction decisions end-to-end through reinforcement learning, using only outcome-based task reward without supervised fine-tuning. Experimental results on Countdown, AMC, and AIME tasks show that NGC maintains strong accuracy relative to a full-cache upper bound while achieving 2-3x peak KV cache compression, substantially outperforming baseline eviction methods.
本文的动机在于，思维链推理中不断增长的KV缓存造成了语言模型扩展的瓶颈，而当前基于人工设计的缓存管理方法缺乏可扩展性。该方法名为神经垃圾回收（NGC），通过强化学习使语言模型端到端地学习推理和缓存驱逐决策，仅使用基于结果的任务奖励，无需监督微调。在Countdown、AMC和AIME任务上的实验结果表明，NGC在实现2-3倍峰值KV缓存压缩的同时，相对于全缓存上限保持了较强的准确性，显著优于基线驱逐方法。
Tape: A Cellular Automata Benchmark for Evaluating Rule-Shift Generalization in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Enze Pan
Venue: ICML
First: 2026-01-08T08:05:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T09:26:00+00:00
Comments: ICML reject and seeking for NeurIPS
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Out-of-distribution generalization in reinforcement learning is hard to diagnose when benchmark shifts mix dynamics, observations, goals, and rewards. We address this with Tape, a controlled benchmark that isolates latent rule-shift in dynamics while keeping the observation-action interface fixed. The protocol combines deterministic splits, 20-seed replication, bootstrap uncertainty reporting, and continuous metrics for sparse-success regimes. Across baseline families, we find a consistent ID-to-OOD drop and strong heterogeneity across stable/periodic/chaotic rules. Importantly, this fragility appears even in an intentionally simple 1D deterministic setting, suggesting that many current RL algorithms remain brittle to latent-law changes under minimal confounds. To calibrate strict success, we report a protocol-matched true-dynamics random-shooting reference (p_oracle is almost 0.187) and oracle-normalized scores ON(p) = 100 p / p_oracle; this is a budgeted operational reference, not a global-optimality bound. A smaller feasibility regime (L = H = 16) with 100% rule-wise solvability helps separate reachability limits from policy failure. These results position Tape as a mechanism-oriented diagnostic for robust adaptation and latent-mechanism inference, and as a controlled benchmark relevant to broader AGI-oriented evaluation without making strong AGI sufficiency claims.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Tape：用于评估强化学习中规则迁移泛化能力的细胞自动机基准
当基准迁移混合了动态、观测、目标与奖励时，强化学习的分布外泛化问题难以诊断。为此我们提出Tape——一个通过固定观测-动作接口来隔离动态中潜在规则迁移的受控基准。该协议结合了确定性划分、20次种子复现、自助法不确定性报告以及稀疏成功机制下的连续度量。在多个基线族中，我们观察到一致的域内到域外性能下降，以及稳定/周期/混沌规则间的显著异质性。重要的是，这种脆弱性甚至出现在刻意简化的单维确定性环境中，表明当前多数强化学习算法在最小混杂因素下对潜在规律变化仍显脆弱。为校准严格成功率，我们报告了协议匹配的真实动态随机采样参考值（p_oracle约0.187）及归一化分数ON(p)=100p/p_oracle；此为预算化操作参考，非全局最优界。通过可完全规则求解的小规模可行域（L=H=16），有效区分了可达性极限与策略失效。这些成果使Tape成为面向机制诊断的鲁棒适应与潜在机制推断工具，并作为与更广泛AGI导向评估相关的受控基准，且不作强AGI充分性声明。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Tape, a benchmark designed to isolate and evaluate out-of-distribution generalization in reinforcement learning, specifically focusing on latent rule-shifts in dynamics while keeping observations and actions fixed, to address the challenge of diagnosing generalization when benchmark shifts involve multiple confounding factors. The method employs a controlled protocol with deterministic splits, 20-seed replication, bootstrap uncertainty reporting, and continuous metrics for sparse-success regimes, testing baseline algorithms in a simple 1D deterministic cellular automata environment. Experimental results reveal a consistent performance drop from in-distribution to out-of-distribution settings, with significant heterogeneity across stable, periodic, and chaotic rules, indicating that current RL algorithms remain brittle to latent-law changes even in minimal-confound scenarios; the study also provides an oracle-normalized score for calibration, using a random-shooting reference to separate reachability limits from policy failure, positioning Tape as a diagnostic tool for robust adaptation and latent-mechanism inference in AGI-oriented evaluation.
本文介绍了Tape这一基准测试，旨在隔离和评估强化学习中的分布外泛化能力，特别关注动态中的潜在规则变化，同时保持观察和行动接口固定，以解决在基准偏移涉及多个混杂因素时难以诊断泛化的问题。方法采用受控协议，包括确定性分割、20次种子重复、自助法不确定性报告以及稀疏成功区域的连续度量，在一个简单的1D确定性元胞自动机环境中测试基线算法。实验结果显示，从分布内到分布外设置存在一致的性能下降，且在稳定、周期和混沌规则间表现出显著异质性，表明即使在没有混杂因素的最小化场景中，当前RL算法对潜在规律变化仍显脆弱；研究还通过随机射击参考提供了归一化分数进行校准，以区分可达性限制与策略失败，将Tape定位为面向AGI评估中鲁棒适应和潜在机制推断的诊断工具。
Eluder dimension: localise it!
Authors: Alireza Bakhtiari, Alex Ayoub, Samuel Robertson, David Janz, Csaba Szepesvári
Venue: NeurIPS
First: 2026-01-14T19:35:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T09:06:48+00:00
Comments: This version corrects a significant error in the published NeurIPS proceedings version. We thank Marc Abeille for bringing the error to our attention
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We establish a lower bound on the eluder dimension of generalised linear model classes, showing that standard eluder dimension-based analysis cannot lead to first-order regret bounds. To address this, we introduce a localisation method for the eluder dimension; our analysis immediately recovers and improves on classic results for Bernoulli bandits, and allows for the first genuine first-order bounds for finite-horizon reinforcement learning tasks with bounded cumulative returns.
中文标题/摘要
标题：迷惑者维度：局部化方法
本文建立了广义线性模型类迷惑者维度的下界，证明基于标准迷惑者维度的分析无法获得一阶遗憾界。为此，我们提出了迷惑者维度的局部化方法：该分析不仅立即恢复并改进了伯努利多臂老虎机问题的经典结果，还首次为具有累积回报有界的有限时域强化学习任务提供了真正的一阶遗憾界。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of standard eluder dimension analysis in achieving first-order regret bounds for generalized linear models, this paper introduces a localized approach to the eluder dimension. The method involves refining the eluder dimension concept to better capture model complexity in localized settings, enabling more precise regret analysis. Experimentally, this approach recovers and improves upon classic results for Bernoulli bandits and, for the first time, yields genuine first-order regret bounds for finite-horizon reinforcement learning tasks with bounded cumulative returns, as demonstrated in NeurIPS.
针对广义线性模型标准eluder维度分析无法实现一阶遗憾界限的局限性，本文提出了一种eluder维度的局部化方法。该方法通过细化eluder维度概念，以更好地捕捉局部设置中的模型复杂性，从而实现更精确的遗憾分析。实验结果表明，该方法恢复并改进了伯努利多臂老虎机问题的经典结果，并首次为具有有界累积回报的有限时域强化学习任务提供了真正的一阶遗憾界限，相关成果已在NeurIPS发表。
EvoCoT: Overcoming the Exploration Bottleneck in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Huanyu Liu, Jia Li, Yihong Dong, Chang Yu, Taozhi Chen, Lecheng Wang, Yongding Tao, Bin Gu, Ge Li
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-08-11T09:49:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T09:03:51+00:00
Comments: Camera-ready version for ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable reward (RLVR) has become a promising paradigm for post-training large language models (LLMs) to improve their reasoning capability. However, when the rollout accuracy is low on hard problems, the reward becomes sparse, limiting learning efficiency and causing exploration bottlenecks. Existing approaches either rely on teacher models for distillation or filter out difficult problems, which limits scalability or restricts reasoning improvement through exploration. We propose EvoCoT, a self-evolving curriculum learning framework based on two-stage chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning optimization. EvoCoT constrains the exploration space by self-generating and verifying CoT trajectories, then gradually shortens CoT steps to expand the space in a controlled way. The framework enables LLMs to stably learn from initially unsolved hard problems under sparse rewards. We apply EvoCoT to multiple LLM families, including Qwen, DeepSeek, and Llama. Experiments show that EvoCoT enables LLMs to solve previously unsolved problems, improves reasoning capability without external CoT supervision, and is compatible with various RL fine-tuning methods. We release the source code to support future research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EvoCoT：克服强化学习中的探索瓶颈
具有可验证奖励的强化学习已成为后训练大型语言模型以提升其推理能力的重要范式。然而，当在复杂问题上展开准确率较低时，奖励信号变得稀疏，导致学习效率受限并引发探索瓶颈。现有方法要么依赖教师模型进行知识蒸馏，要么过滤困难问题，这限制了可扩展性或阻碍了通过探索提升推理能力。 我们提出EvoCoT，一种基于两阶段思维链推理优化的自演进课程学习框架。该框架通过自主生成并验证思维链轨迹来约束探索空间，随后逐步缩短思维链步骤以可控方式扩展探索范围。该框架使大型语言模型能够在稀疏奖励下稳定地从初始未解决的难题中学习。我们将EvoCoT应用于包括Qwen、DeepSeek和Llama在内的多个大模型系列。实验表明，EvoCoT能使大模型解决先前无法处理的问题，在无需外部思维链监督的情况下提升推理能力，且兼容多种强化学习微调方法。我们已开源代码以支持后续研究。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the exploration bottleneck in reinforcement learning with verifiable reward (RLVR) for large language models, where sparse rewards on hard problems hinder learning efficiency. The proposed method, EvoCoT, is a self-evolving curriculum learning framework that uses two-stage chain-of-thought reasoning optimization to constrain and gradually expand the exploration space by self-generating and verifying CoT trajectories. Experimental results on LLMs like Qwen, DeepSeek, and Llama demonstrate that EvoCoT enables solving previously unsolved problems, improves reasoning capability without external supervision, and is compatible with various RL fine-tuning methods.
本文针对大型语言模型在可验证奖励强化学习中面临的探索瓶颈问题，即困难任务上稀疏奖励会限制学习效率。提出的方法EvoCoT是一种自演进的课程学习框架，基于两阶段思维链推理优化，通过自生成和验证思维链轨迹来约束并逐步扩展探索空间。在Qwen、DeepSeek和Llama等模型上的实验表明，EvoCoT能够解决先前未解决的问题，无需外部监督即可提升推理能力，并且兼容多种强化学习微调方法。
Erase to Improve: Erasable Reinforcement Learning for Search-Augmented LLMs
Authors: Ziliang Wang, Kang An, Xuhui Zheng, Faqiang Qian, Weikun Zhang, Cijun Ouyang, Jialu Cai, Yuhang Wang, Yichao Wu
First: 2025-10-01T13:10:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T08:17:44+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While search-augmented large language models (LLMs) exhibit impressive capabilities, their reliability in complex multi-hop reasoning remains limited. This limitation arises from three fundamental challenges: decomposition errors, where tasks are incorrectly broken down; retrieval missing, where key evidence fails to be retrieved; and reasoning errors, where flawed logic propagates through the reasoning chain. A single failure in any of these stages can derail the final answer. We propose Erasable Reinforcement Learning (ERL), a novel framework that transforms fragile reasoning into a robust process. ERL explicitly identifies faulty steps, erases them, and regenerates reasoning in place, preventing defective logic from propagating through the reasoning chain. This targeted correction mechanism turns brittle reasoning into a more resilient process. Models trained with ERL, termed ESearch, achieve substantial improvements on HotpotQA, MuSiQue, 2Wiki, and Bamboogle, with the 3B model achieving +8.48% EM and +11.56% F1, and the 7B model achieving +5.38% EM and +7.22% F1 over previous state-of-the-art(SOTA) results. These findings suggest that erasable reinforcement learning provides a powerful paradigm shift for robust multi-step reasoning in LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：擦除以改进：面向检索增强大语言模型的可擦除强化学习
尽管检索增强大语言模型展现出卓越能力，但其在复杂多跳推理中的可靠性仍存在局限。这一局限源于三个根本性挑战：分解错误（任务被错误拆解）、检索缺失（关键证据未能被检索）以及推理错误（错误逻辑在推理链中传播）。任一阶段的单点故障都可能导致最终答案失效。我们提出可擦除强化学习这一新颖框架，将脆弱的推理过程转化为鲁棒流程。该框架能明确识别错误步骤，将其擦除并就地重新生成推理，防止缺陷逻辑在推理链中传播。这种定向修正机制将脆性推理转化为更具韧性的过程。经可擦除强化学习训练的模型（称为ESearch）在HotpotQA、MuSiQue、2Wiki和Bamboogle数据集上取得显著提升：3B模型相较先前最优结果提升8.48%精确匹配率和11.56%F1值，7B模型提升5.38%精确匹配率和7.22%F1值。这些发现表明，可擦除强化学习为大语言模型的鲁棒多步推理提供了强大的范式转变。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the reliability limitations of search-augmented large language models (LLMs) in complex multi-hop reasoning, which stem from decomposition errors, retrieval missing, and reasoning errors that can derail final answers. To overcome these issues, the authors propose Erasable Reinforcement Learning (ERL), a framework that identifies faulty reasoning steps, erases them, and regenerates correct reasoning in place to prevent error propagation. Experimental results show that models trained with ERL, called ESearch, achieve significant improvements over previous state-of-the-art methods on benchmarks like HotpotQA, MuSiQue, 2Wiki, and Bamboogle, with a 3B model gaining +8.48% EM and +11.56% F1, and a 7B model gaining +5.38% EM and +7.22% F1, demonstrating ERL's effectiveness in enhancing robust multi-step reasoning.
本文针对搜索增强大语言模型在复杂多跳推理中可靠性不足的问题，该问题源于分解错误、检索缺失和推理错误，这些错误可能导致最终答案失效。为解决此问题，作者提出了可擦除强化学习框架，通过识别错误推理步骤、擦除并重新生成正确推理，以防止错误在推理链中传播。实验结果表明，使用该框架训练的ESearch模型在HotpotQA、MuSiQue、2Wiki和Bamboogle等基准测试上显著优于先前最优方法，其中3B模型在EM和F1分数上分别提升8.48%和11.56%，7B模型分别提升5.38%和7.22%，证明了该框架在增强稳健多步推理方面的有效性。
ContraPrompt: Contrastive Prompt Optimization via Dyadic Reasoning Trace Analysis
Authors: Rishav Rishav, Pushpak Pujari, Pushpendre Rastogi
First: 2026-04-20T08:17:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T08:17:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Prompt optimization methods either analyze individual failures in isolation or compare prompt variants across examples, operating on single execution traces with no access to the reasoning process distinguishing success from failure on the same input. We introduce ContraPrompt, built on the observation that when a model fails but succeeds on a retry with feedback, the difference between its two chain-of-thought traces constitutes an optimization signal not captured by prior methods. Unlike prior contrastive methods, we compare complete intermediate reasoning processes: the two traces share model, input, and base prompt, so remaining differences reflect reasoning strategy and appended error feedback -- we call this dyadic reasoning trace analysis. The multi-attempt solving phase is an instrumented agentic retry loop that generates contrastive data automatically without human annotation. Extracted rules are organized into an input-aware decision tree routing instructions by observable input characteristics. On four reasoning and compliance benchmarks, ContraPrompt outperforms GEPA (Agrawal et al., 2026) on all four, with absolute gains of +8.29 pp on HotPotQA (+20.8% rel.), +2.21 pp on GDPR-Bench (+18.2% rel.), +7.14 pp on GPQA Diamond (+10.6% rel.), and +0.74 pp on BBH (+0.85% rel.). Ablations confirm dyadic trace contrastivity is the critical component, with a -16% relative average drop upon its removal. On 53 EvalSet black-box optimization problems, ContraPrompt beats GEPA on 11, ties on 41, and loses on 1 at equal budget. On FiNER-139 financial named entity recognition (Loukas et al., 2022), ContraPrompt achieves +7.77 pp over the unoptimized baseline (+11.6% rel.) and +1.94 pp over GEPA (+2.66% rel.), with branch conditions aligning with standard US GAAP financial-instrument categories.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ContraPrompt：基于二元推理轨迹分析的对比提示优化方法
现有提示优化方法通常孤立分析单次失败案例，或跨样本比较提示变体，仅依赖单次执行轨迹且无法捕捉同一输入下成败差异的推理过程。本文提出ContraPrompt，其核心洞见在于：当模型首次失败但通过反馈重试成功时，两次思维链轨迹的差异构成先前方法未能捕获的优化信号。与现有对比方法不同，我们比较完整的中间推理过程：两次轨迹共享模型、输入和基础提示，因此剩余差异反映推理策略与附加错误反馈——我们称之为二元推理轨迹分析。多轮求解阶段采用可监测的智能重试循环，无需人工标注即可自动生成对比数据。提取的规则按可观测输入特征组织为输入感知型决策树指令路由机制。在四个推理与合规基准测试中，ContraPrompt全面超越GEPA（Agrawal等，2026）：HotPotQA绝对提升8.29个百分点（相对提升20.8%）、GDPR-Bench提升2.21个百分点（18.2%）、GPQA Diamond提升7.14个百分点（10.6%）、BBH提升0.74个百分点（0.85%）。消融实验证实二元轨迹对比性是关键组件，移除后平均相对性能下降16%。在53个EvalSet黑盒优化问题上，等预算条件下ContraPrompt在11项超越GEPA、41项持平、仅1项落后。在FiNER-139金融命名实体识别任务（Loukas等，2022）中，ContraPrompt较未优化基线提升7.77个百分点（相对提升11.6%），较GEPA提升1.94个百分点（2.66%），其分支条件与美国通用会计准则金融工具分类标准高度吻合。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for ContraPrompt is to improve prompt optimization by analyzing the reasoning process differences when a model fails and then succeeds on the same input with feedback, a signal missed by prior methods that examine single traces or compare variants across examples. The method employs dyadic reasoning trace analysis, comparing complete intermediate reasoning traces from an instrumented agentic retry loop to automatically extract optimization rules without human annotation, which are then organized into an input-aware decision tree for routing instructions. Experimental results show that ContraPrompt outperforms the baseline GEPA across four reasoning and compliance benchmarks, with significant relative gains such as +20.8% on HotPotQA and +18.2% on GDPR-Bench, and it also achieves superior performance on financial named entity recognition, with ablations confirming the critical role of dyadic trace contrastivity.
ContraPrompt的动机是通过分析模型在同一输入上失败后通过反馈成功时推理过程的差异来改进提示优化，这一信号被先前仅检查单次执行轨迹或跨示例比较变体的方法所忽略。该方法采用二元推理轨迹分析，通过一个自动化的代理重试循环比较完整的中间推理轨迹，无需人工标注即可提取优化规则，并将其组织成基于输入感知的决策树以路由指令。实验结果表明，ContraPrompt在四个推理和合规基准测试中均优于基线GEPA，取得了显著的相对提升，如在HotPotQA上相对增益达+20.8%，在GDPR-Bench上为+18.2%，并在金融命名实体识别任务中表现更优，消融实验证实了二元轨迹对比性的关键作用。
LiteResearcher: A Scalable Agentic RL Training Framework for Deep Research Agent
Authors: Wanli Li, Bince Qu, Bo Pan, Jianyu Zhang, Zheng Liu, Pan Zhang, Wei Chen, Bo Zhang
First: 2026-04-20T08:11:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T08:11:09+00:00
Comments: Preprint. Under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has emerged as a powerful training paradigm for LLM-based agents. However, scaling agentic RL for deep research remains constrained by two coupled challenges: hand-crafted synthetic data fails to elicit genuine real-world search capabilities, and real-world search dependency during RL training introduces instability and prohibitive cost, which limits the scalability of Agentic RL. LiteResearcher is a training framework that makes Agentic RL scalable: by constructing a lite virtual world that mirrors real-world search dynamics, we enable a continuously improving training recipe that empowers a tiny search agent to outperform large-scale open-source and commercial models (e.g., Tongyi DeepResearch and Claude-4.5 Sonnet). Specifically, on common benchmarks such as GAIA and Xbench, our LiteResearcher-4B achieves open-source state-of-the-art results of 71.3% and 78.0% respectively, demonstrating that scalable RL training is a key enabler for Deep Research Agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LiteResearcher：面向深度研究智能体的可扩展智能强化学习训练框架
强化学习已成为基于大语言模型的智能体的一种强大训练范式。然而，针对深度研究的智能强化学习规模化仍受限于两个相互关联的挑战：手工合成的数据无法激发真实的现实世界搜索能力，而强化学习训练中对现实世界搜索的依赖则引入了不稳定性和高昂成本，制约了智能强化学习的可扩展性。LiteResearcher 是一个使智能强化学习可扩展的训练框架：通过构建一个映射现实世界搜索动态的轻量虚拟环境，我们实现了一种持续改进的训练方案，使小型搜索智能体能够超越大规模开源及商业模型（如通义深度研究、Claude-4.5 Sonnet）。具体而言，在 GAIA 和 Xbench 等常见基准测试中，我们的 LiteResearcher-4B 分别取得了 71.3% 和 78.0% 的开源最优结果，证明了可扩展的强化学习训练是深度研究智能体的关键赋能技术。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces LiteResearcher, a scalable agentic reinforcement learning (RL) framework designed to overcome limitations in training deep research agents, where synthetic data inadequately simulates real search capabilities and real-world search during RL proves costly and unstable. The method constructs a lightweight virtual world that replicates real search dynamics, enabling continuous training that allows a compact search agent to surpass larger models. Experimental results show that LiteResearcher-4B achieves state-of-the-art open-source performance on GAIA and Xbench benchmarks with scores of 71.3% and 78.0%, respectively, outperforming commercial models like Tongyi DeepResearch and Claude-4.5 Sonnet, thus demonstrating scalable RL as a key enabler for advanced research agents.
本文提出了LiteResearcher，一个可扩展的智能体强化学习框架，旨在解决训练深度研究智能体时的两大耦合挑战：手工合成的数据无法激发真实的现实世界搜索能力，而RL训练中对现实搜索的依赖会导致不稳定和高成本。该方法通过构建一个模拟真实搜索动态的轻量级虚拟世界，实现了持续改进的训练方案，使一个小型搜索智能体能够超越大规模开源和商业模型。实验结果表明，LiteResearcher-4B在GAIA和Xbench等常见基准测试中分别取得了71.3%和78.0%的开源最优性能，优于如通义深度研究和Claude-4.5 Sonnet等模型，证明了可扩展RL训练是深度研究智能体的关键推动因素。
HEALing Entropy Collapse: Enhancing Exploration in Few-Shot RLVR via Hybrid-Domain Entropy Dynamics Alignment
Authors: Zhanyu Liu, Qingguo Hu, Ante Wang, Chenqing Liu, Zhishang Xiang, Hui Li, Delai Qiu, Jinsong Su
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-20T08:09:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T08:09:01+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) has proven effective for training reasoning-oriented large language models, but existing methods largely assume high-resource settings with abundant training data. In low-resource scenarios, RLVR is prone to more severe entropy collapse, which substantially limits exploration and degrades reasoning performance. To address this issue, we propose Hybrid-domain Entropy dynamics ALignment (HEAL), a framework tailored for few-shot RLVR. HEAL first selectively incorporates high-value general-domain data to promote more diverse exploration. Then, we introduce Entropy Dynamics Alignment (EDA), a reward mechanism that aligns trajectory-level entropy dynamics between the target and general domains, capturing both entropy magnitude and fine-grained variation. Through this alignment, EDA not only further mitigates entropy collapse but also encourages the policy to acquire more diverse exploration behaviors from the general domain. Experiments across multiple domains show that HEAL consistently improves few-shot RLVR performance. Notably, using only 32 target-domain samples, HEAL matches or even surpasses full-shot RLVR trained with 1K target-domain samples.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HEALing熵崩塌：通过混合域熵动态对齐增强小样本RLVR中的探索能力
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）已被证明能有效训练面向推理的大语言模型，但现有方法大多假设训练数据充足的高资源场景。在低资源场景中，RLVR易出现更严重的熵崩塌，极大限制探索并降低推理性能。为解决此问题，我们提出混合域熵动态对齐（HEAL），一个专为小样本RLVR设计的框架。HEAL首先选择性引入高价值通用领域数据以促进多样化探索；随后提出熵动态对齐（EDA）奖励机制，通过对齐目标域与通用域的轨迹级熵动态（涵盖熵值大小与细粒度变化），不仅进一步缓解熵崩塌，还鼓励策略从通用域学习更多样化的探索行为。跨多领域实验表明，HEAL能持续提升小样本RLVR性能。值得注意的是，仅使用32个目标域样本时，HEAL即可达到甚至超越使用1K目标域样本训练的全样本RLVR水平。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the severe entropy collapse that limits exploration and degrades reasoning performance in few-shot Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) settings. The proposed method, Hybrid-domain Entropy dynamics ALignment (HEAL), selectively incorporates high-value general-domain data and introduces an Entropy Dynamics Alignment (EDA) reward mechanism to align trajectory-level entropy dynamics between target and general domains, capturing both magnitude and fine-grained variation to mitigate collapse and encourage diverse exploration. Main experimental results demonstrate that HEAL consistently improves few-shot RLVR performance across multiple domains, notably matching or surpassing full-shot RLVR trained with 1K target-domain samples using only 32 target-domain samples.
本研究的动机是解决在少样本可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）中，严重的熵崩溃限制探索并降低推理性能的问题。所提出的方法——混合域熵动态对齐（HEAL），选择性地整合高价值的通用域数据，并引入熵动态对齐（EDA）奖励机制，以对齐目标域和通用域之间的轨迹级熵动态，捕捉熵的大小和细粒度变化，从而缓解熵崩溃并鼓励多样化的探索行为。主要实验结果表明，HEAL在多个领域持续提升了少样本RLVR的性能，特别是在仅使用32个目标域样本的情况下，其表现匹配甚至超越了使用1K个目标域样本训练的全样本RLVR。
Fisher Decorator: Refining Flow Policy via A Local Transport Map
Authors: Xiaoyuan Cheng, Haoyu Wang, Wenxuan Yuan, Ziyan Wang, Zonghao Chen, Li Zeng, Zhuo Sun
First: 2026-04-20T07:54:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T07:54:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent advances in flow-based offline reinforcement learning (RL) have achieved strong performance by parameterizing policies via flow matching. However, they still face critical trade-offs among expressiveness, optimality, and efficiency. In particular, existing flow policies interpret the $L_2$ regularization as an upper bound of the 2-Wasserstein distance ($W_2$), which can be problematic in offline settings. This issue stems from a fundamental geometric mismatch: the behavioral policy manifold is inherently anisotropic, whereas the $L_2$ (or upper bound of $W_2$) regularization is isotropic and density-insensitive, leading to systematically misaligned optimization directions. To address this, we revisit offline RL from a geometric perspective and show that policy refinement can be formulated as a local transport map: an initial flow policy augmented by a residual displacement. By analyzing the induced density transformation, we derive a local quadratic approximation of the KL-constrained objective governed by the Fisher information matrix, enabling a tractable anisotropic optimization formulation. By leveraging the score function embedded in the flow velocity, we obtain a corresponding quadratic constraint for efficient optimization. Our results reveal that the optimality gap in prior methods arises from their isotropic approximation. In contrast, our framework achieves a controllable approximation error within a provable neighborhood of the optimal solution. Extensive experiments demonstrate state-of-the-art performance across diverse offline RL benchmarks. See project page: https://github.com/ARC0127/Fisher-Decorator.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Fisher装饰器：通过局部传输映射精化流策略
基于流的离线强化学习近期通过流匹配参数化策略取得了优异性能，但仍面临表达能力、最优性与效率之间的权衡。现有流策略将$L_2$正则化视为2-Wasserstein距离($W_2$)的上界，这在离线场景中可能存在问题。该问题源于几何失配：行为策略流形本质上是各向异性的，而$L_2$正则化（或$W_2$上界）是各向同性且对密度不敏感的，导致优化方向系统性错位。为此，我们从几何视角重新审视离线强化学习，证明策略精化可表述为局部传输映射：即通过残差位移增强的初始流策略。通过分析诱导的密度变换，我们推导出由费舍尔信息矩阵控制的KL约束目标的局部二次近似，从而建立可处理的各向异性优化框架。利用流速度中嵌入的得分函数，我们获得了对应的高效优化二次约束。结果表明，现有方法的最优性差距源于其各向同性近似。相比之下，我们的框架在可证明的最优解邻域内实现了可控近似误差。大量实验在多样化离线强化学习基准上展示了最先进的性能。项目页面：https://github.com/ARC0127/Fisher-Decorator。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a geometric mismatch in flow-based offline reinforcement learning, where isotropic L2 regularization misaligns with the anisotropic nature of behavioral policy manifolds, leading to suboptimal policies. The method refines flow policies by formulating policy refinement as a local transport map, using a residual displacement and deriving a tractable anisotropic optimization via a local quadratic approximation of the KL-constrained objective governed by the Fisher information matrix. Experimental results show that this approach achieves state-of-the-art performance across diverse offline RL benchmarks by reducing the optimality gap present in prior isotropic methods.
该论文针对基于流的离线强化学习中存在的几何不匹配问题，即各向同性的L2正则化与行为策略流形的各向异性本质不符，导致策略次优。方法通过将策略精炼表述为局部传输映射来改进流策略，利用残差位移，并通过费舍尔信息矩阵控制的KL约束目标的局部二次近似，推导出可处理的各向异性优化公式。实验结果表明，该方法通过减少先前各向同性方法中的最优性差距，在多样化的离线强化学习基准测试中实现了最先进的性能。
Learning to Correct: Calibrated Reinforcement Learning for Multi-Attempt Chain-of-Thought
Authors: Muhammed Emrullah Ildiz, Halil Alperen Gozeten, Ege Onur Taga, Samet Oymak
First: 2026-04-20T07:42:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T07:42:22+00:00
Comments: 24 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
State-of-the-art reasoning models utilize long chain-of-thought (CoT) to solve increasingly complex problems using more test-time computation. In this work, we explore a long CoT setting where the model makes up to K successive attempts at solving a problem, in which each attempt is allowed to build on earlier ones after the model receives a hard verifier feedback. This motivates RL methods that can harness per-attempt rewards by carefully weighting individual attempts. We study optimizing the Verification@K reward (the model succeeds by the K-th attempt) and show that naively weighing the attempts by their pass/fail results in biased gradients. We introduce Calibrated Attempt-Level (CAL) GRPO by devising a weighing strategy to obtain unbiased gradients while maintaining small variance. Our theory reveals how incorporating per-attempt rewards influence the training and the eventual Verification@K performance. Experiments, baselines, and ablations on synthetic and real data corroborate our theory and the benefits of CAL-GRPO over vanilla GRPO as well as naive weighting.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习修正：面向多轮尝试思维链的校准强化学习
当前最先进的推理模型通过长思维链（CoT）利用更多测试时计算解决日益复杂的问题。本研究探索了一种长思维链场景：模型最多可进行K次连续尝试以解决问题，每次尝试在接收到严格验证器反馈后均可基于先前尝试进行改进。这促使强化学习方法能通过精细加权单次尝试来利用每次尝试的奖励。我们研究了优化Verification@K奖励（模型在第K次尝试前成功）的问题，并证明简单按通过/失败结果加权尝试会导致梯度偏差。我们通过设计加权策略提出校准尝试级（CAL）GRPO方法，在保持低方差的同时获得无偏梯度。理论分析揭示了融入每次尝试奖励如何影响训练及最终Verification@K性能。在合成与真实数据上的实验、基线测试及消融研究均验证了理论结论，并证明CAL-GRPO相较于原始GRPO及简单加权方法的优势。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to improve reasoning models that use multi-step chain-of-thought (CoT) processes, where models can make up to K successive attempts with verifier feedback after each try, aiming to optimize the Verification@K reward which measures success within K attempts. The method introduces Calibrated Attempt-Level (CAL) GRPO, a reinforcement learning approach that addresses biased gradients from naive weighting of per-attempt rewards by devising an unbiased, low-variance weighting strategy for individual attempts. Experimental results on synthetic and real data show that CAL-GRPO outperforms vanilla GRPO and naive weighting baselines, validating the theoretical insights into how per-attempt rewards affect training and final performance.
本文的动机在于改进使用多步思维链（CoT）的推理模型，这些模型可进行最多K次连续尝试，并在每次尝试后接收验证器反馈，以优化在K次尝试内成功的Verification@K奖励。方法上提出了校准尝试级别（CAL）GRPO，这是一种强化学习方法，通过设计无偏且低方差的权重策略来处理基于每次尝试奖励的朴素加权导致的梯度偏差问题。在合成和真实数据上的实验结果表明，CAL-GRPO优于原始GRPO和朴素加权基线，验证了关于每次尝试奖励如何影响训练和最终性能的理论见解。
VIDEOP2R: Video Understanding from Perception to Reasoning
Authors: Yifan Jiang, Yueying Wang, Rui Zhao, Toufiq Parag, Zhimin Chen, Zhenyu Liao, Jayakrishnan Unnikrishnan
Venue: CVPR
First: 2025-11-14T09:42:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T07:37:36+00:00
Comments: CVPR Findings 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Reinforcement fine-tuning (RFT), a two-stage framework consisting of supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL) has shown promising results on improving reasoning ability of large language models (LLMs). Yet extending RFT to large video language models (LVLMs) remains challenging. We propose VideoP2R, a novel process-aware video RFT framework that enhances video reasoning by modeling perception and reasoning as distinct processes. In the SFT stage, we develop a three-step pipeline to generate VideoP2R-CoT-162K, a high-quality, process-aware chain-of-thought (CoT) dataset for perception and reasoning. In the RL stage, we introduce a novel process-aware group relative policy optimization (PA-GRPO) algorithm that supplies separate rewards for perception and reasoning. Extensive experiments show that VideoP2R achieves state-of-the-art (SotA) performance on six out of seven video reasoning and understanding benchmarks. Ablation studies further confirm the effectiveness of our process-aware modeling and PA-GRPO and demonstrate that model's perception output is information-sufficient for downstream reasoning. Our project page is available at https://videop2r.github.io/videop2r/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VIDEOP2R：从感知到推理的视频理解
强化微调（RFT）是一种包含监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）的两阶段框架，在提升大语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力方面已展现出良好效果。然而，将RFT扩展至大型视频语言模型（LVLMs）仍具挑战性。我们提出VideoP2R，一种新颖的流程感知视频RFT框架，通过将感知与推理建模为独立过程来增强视频推理能力。在SFT阶段，我们开发了一个三步流程，生成VideoP2R-CoT-162K——一个高质量、流程感知的感知与推理思维链（CoT）数据集。在RL阶段，我们引入了一种新颖的流程感知分组相对策略优化（PA-GRPO）算法，为感知和推理分别提供奖励。大量实验表明，VideoP2R在七项视频推理与理解基准测试中的六项上取得了最先进（SotA）性能。消融研究进一步证实了我们流程感知建模和PA-GRPO的有效性，并证明模型的感知输出足以支持下游推理。项目页面详见：https://videop2r.github.io/videop2r/。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for VideoP2R is to extend the successful reinforcement fine-tuning (RFT) framework, which improves reasoning in large language models, to the challenging domain of large video-language models (LVLMs) for enhanced video understanding. The method introduces a novel process-aware framework that explicitly separates video perception from reasoning: first, it creates a high-quality chain-of-thought dataset (VideoP2R-CoT-162K) via a three-step pipeline during supervised fine-tuning; second, it develops a process-aware group relative policy optimization (PA-GRPO) algorithm that provides distinct rewards for perception and reasoning during reinforcement learning. The main experimental results demonstrate state-of-the-art performance on six out of seven video reasoning benchmarks, with ablation studies confirming the effectiveness of the process-aware modeling and showing that the model's perception output contains sufficient information for downstream reasoning tasks.
VideoP2R的研究动机是将已在大型语言模型中成功提升推理能力的强化微调框架，扩展到具有挑战性的视频-语言模型领域，以增强视频理解能力。该方法提出了一种新颖的流程感知框架，明确将视频感知与推理分离：首先，在监督微调阶段通过三步流程生成了高质量的思维链数据集；其次，在强化学习阶段开发了流程感知分组相对策略优化算法，为感知和推理过程提供独立的奖励。主要实验结果表明，该方法在七个视频推理基准中的六个上取得了最先进的性能，消融研究进一步证实了流程感知建模的有效性，并证明模型的感知输出为下游推理任务提供了充分的信息。
Less Noise, More Voice: Reinforcement Learning for Reasoning via Instruction Purification
Authors: Yiju Guo, Tianyi Hu, Zexu Sun, Yankai Lin
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-29T04:08:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T07:32:10+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ACL 2026, camera-ready version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has advanced LLM reasoning, but remains constrained by inefficient exploration under limited rollout budgets, leading to low sampling success and unstable training in complex tasks. We find that many exploration failures arise not from problem difficulty, but from a small number of prompt tokens that introduce interference. Building on this insight, we propose the Less Noise Sampling Framework (LENS), which first prompts by identifying and removing interference tokens. then transfers successful rollouts from the purification process to supervise policy optimization on the original noisy prompts, enabling the model to learn to ignore interference in the real-world, noisy prompting settings. Experimental results show that LENS significantly outperforms GRPO, delivering higher performance and faster convergence, with a 3.88% average gain and over 1.6$\times$ speedup on math reasoning, and a 1.83% gain on scientific and general reasoning. Our work highlights the critical role of pruning interference tokens in improving rollout efficiency, offering a new perspective for RLVR research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：降噪增声：基于指令净化的强化学习推理方法
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）虽推动了大型语言模型的推理能力，但在有限计算预算下仍受低效探索的制约，导致复杂任务中采样成功率低且训练不稳定。研究发现，许多探索失败并非源于问题难度，而是由少数引发干扰的提示词所致。基于此，我们提出降噪采样框架（LENS）：首先通过识别并移除干扰词实现提示净化，随后将净化过程中成功的轨迹迁移至原始含噪提示的策略优化监督中，使模型学会在实际含噪提示场景中忽略干扰。实验表明，LENS显著优于GRPO，在数学推理任务上实现3.88%的平均性能提升与超1.6倍的加速，在科学及通用推理任务上获得1.83%提升。本研究揭示了剪枝干扰词对提升轨迹效率的关键作用，为RLVR研究提供了新视角。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) in complex reasoning tasks due to limited rollout budgets and unstable training, this paper identifies that many exploration failures stem from a small number of interfering tokens in prompts rather than inherent problem difficulty. The proposed method, Less Noise Sampling Framework (LENS), addresses this by first purifying prompts through identifying and removing interference tokens, then transferring successful rollouts from this purified setting to supervise policy optimization on the original noisy prompts, enabling the model to learn to ignore interference in real-world scenarios. Experimental results demonstrate that LENS significantly outperforms GRPO, achieving an average 3.88% performance gain and over 1.6× speedup on math reasoning tasks, along with a 1.83% gain on scientific and general reasoning, highlighting the importance of pruning interference tokens for improved rollout efficiency and offering a new direction for RLVR research.
本文针对基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在复杂推理任务中因有限的探索预算和训练不稳定而效率低下的问题，发现许多探索失败源于提示中少量干扰令牌而非问题本身难度。为此，提出了低噪声采样框架（LENS），该方法首先通过识别并移除干扰令牌来净化提示，然后将净化后成功的探索样本迁移到原始噪声提示上监督策略优化，使模型学会在真实噪声提示设置中忽略干扰。实验结果表明，LENS显著优于GRPO，在数学推理任务上平均性能提升3.88%且加速超过1.6倍，在科学和通用推理上提升1.83%，强调了修剪干扰令牌对提高探索效率的关键作用，为RLVR研究提供了新视角。
LEPO: \underline{L}atent R\underline{e}asoning \underline{P}olicy \underline{O}ptimization for Large Language~Models
Authors: Yuyan Zhou, Jiarui Yu, Hande Dong, Zhezheng Hao, Hong Wang, Jianqing Zhang, Qiang Lin
First: 2026-04-20T07:05:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T07:05:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recently, latent reasoning has been introduced into large language models (LLMs) to leverage rich information within a continuous space. However, without stochastic sampling, these methods inevitably collapse to deterministic inference, failing to discover diverse reasoning paths. To bridge the gap, we inject controllable stochasticity into latent reasoning via Gumbel-Softmax, restoring LLMs' exploratory capacity and enhancing their compatibility with Reinforcement Learning (RL). Building on this, we propose \textbf{\underline{L}}atent R\textbf{\underline{e}}asoning \textbf{\underline{P}}olicy \textbf{\underline{O}}ptimization~(\textbf{LEPO}), a novel framework that applies RL directly to continuous latent representations. Specifically, in rollout stage, LEPO maintains stochasticity to enable diverse trajectory sampling, while in optimization stage, LEPO constructs a unified gradient estimation for both latent representations and discrete tokens. Extensive experiments show that LEPO significantly outperforms existing RL methods for discrete and latent reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LEPO：面向大语言模型的潜在推理策略优化
近期，潜在推理被引入大语言模型以利用连续空间中的丰富信息。然而，由于缺乏随机采样，这些方法不可避免地退化为确定性推理，难以发现多样化的推理路径。为弥补这一缺陷，我们通过Gumbel-Softmax向潜在推理注入可控随机性，恢复大语言模型的探索能力并增强其与强化学习的兼容性。在此基础上，我们提出潜在推理策略优化（LEPO）这一创新框架，将强化学习直接应用于连续潜在表示。具体而言，在推演阶段，LEPO保持随机性以实现多样化轨迹采样；在优化阶段，LEPO构建针对潜在表示和离散标记的统一梯度估计。大量实验表明，LEPO在离散与潜在推理任务上显著优于现有强化学习方法。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for LEPO is to address the deterministic collapse and lack of diversity in existing latent reasoning methods for large language models (LLMs), which limits their exploratory capacity and compatibility with reinforcement learning (RL). The method introduces controllable stochasticity into latent reasoning via Gumbel-Softmax, enabling diverse reasoning path sampling during rollout, and proposes a novel RL framework that optimizes both continuous latent representations and discrete tokens through unified gradient estimation. Experimental results demonstrate that LEPO significantly outperforms existing RL methods in tasks involving discrete and latent reasoning.
LEPO的动机是解决现有大语言模型潜在推理方法中存在的确定性崩溃和多样性不足问题，这些问题限制了模型的探索能力以及与强化学习的兼容性。该方法通过Gumbel-Softmax将可控随机性注入潜在推理，在推演阶段实现多样化推理路径采样，并提出一种新颖的强化学习框架，通过统一梯度估计同时优化连续潜在表示和离散标记。实验结果表明，LEPO在离散和潜在推理任务上显著优于现有的强化学习方法。
On Scalability of Multi-Objective Evolutionary Algorithms on Combinatorial Optimisation Problems
Authors: Menghao Tang, Zimin Liang, Miqing Li
First: 2026-04-20T06:35:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T06:35:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scalability of evolutionary algorithms refers to assessing how their performance changes as problem size increases. In the area of multi-objective optimisation, research on the scalability of multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (MOEAs) has predominantly focussed on continuous problems. However, multi-objective combinatorial optimisation problems (MOCOPs) differ from continuous ones. Their discrete and rigid structure often brings rugged landscape, numerous local optimal solutions and disjoint global optimal regions. This leads to different behaviour of MOEAs. For example, SEMO, a simple MOEA without mating selection and diversity maintenance mechanisms, has been shown to be highly competitive, and in many cases to outperform more sophisticated MOEAs on MOCOPs. Yet, it remains unclear whether such findings hold for large-scale cases. In this paper, we conduct an empirical investigation into the scalability of MOEAs on combinatorial problems, with problem size from 50 to 5,000. Our results show that SEMO experiences a decline in convergence speed as dimensionality increases, compared to other MOEAs such as NSGA-II, SMS-EMOA and MOEA/D. We further demonstrate that the absence of crossover is a major contributor to SEMO's underperformance in large-scale problems, and that incorporating crossover into SEMO can substantially accelerate convergence in general, despite being detrimental in spreading solutions over the Pareto front.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多目标进化算法在组合优化问题上的可扩展性研究
进化算法的可扩展性指评估其性能随问题规模增大的变化情况。在多目标优化领域，关于多目标进化算法（MOEAs）可扩展性的研究主要集中于连续问题。然而，多目标组合优化问题（MOCOPs）与连续问题存在差异：其离散且刚性的结构常导致崎岖的搜索空间、大量局部最优解及不连通的全局最优区域，进而引发MOEAs的不同行为。例如，缺乏交配选择和多样性维护机制的简单MOEA——SEMO，已被证明在MOCOPs上具有高度竞争力，甚至常优于复杂MOEA。但此类结论是否适用于大规模问题尚不明确。本文通过问题规模从50至5,000的实证研究，探究MOEAs在组合问题上的可扩展性。结果表明，与NSGA-II、SMS-EMOA和MOEA/D等算法相比，SEMO的收敛速度随维度增加而下降。进一步分析发现，缺乏交叉操作是SEMO在大规模问题中表现不佳的主因，而引入交叉操作虽可能不利于解在帕累托前沿的分布，但总体上能显著加速收敛。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the scalability of multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (MOEAs) on combinatorial problems, motivated by the fact that prior scalability research has focused on continuous problems, while discrete combinatorial problems present unique challenges like rugged landscapes and many local optima, where simpler algorithms like SEMO have been surprisingly effective on smaller instances. The method involves an empirical study comparing the performance of SEMO against more sophisticated MOEAs (NSGA-II, SMS-EMOA, MOEA/D) across problem sizes ranging from 50 to 5,000 variables. The main experimental results show that SEMO's convergence speed declines relative to other algorithms as problem size increases, and further analysis identifies the lack of crossover as a key reason for this poor scalability, demonstrating that adding crossover to SEMO generally improves convergence speed, though it can harm the spread of solutions along the Pareto front.
本文研究了多目标进化算法在组合优化问题上的可扩展性，其动机在于现有的可扩展性研究主要针对连续问题，而离散组合问题具有独特的挑战，如崎岖的搜索空间和大量局部最优解，且先前发现简单算法SEMO在较小规模问题上表现优异。研究方法是对比SEMO与更复杂的算法（如NSGA-II、SMS-EMOA和MOEA/D）在问题规模从50到5000变量范围内的实证性能。主要实验结果表明，随着问题规模增大，SEMO的收敛速度相比其他算法下降，进一步分析发现缺乏交叉操作是导致其可扩展性差的主要原因，证明在SEMO中加入交叉操作能显著加速收敛，尽管这可能不利于解在帕累托前沿上的分布。
PaTaRM: Bridging Pairwise and Pointwise Signals via Preference-Aware Task-Adaptive Reward Modeling
Authors: Ai Jian, Jingqing Ruan, Xing Ma, Xiaoyun Zhang, Dailin Li, Weipeng Zhang, Ke Zeng, Xunliang Cai
Venue: ACL
First: 2025-10-28T09:43:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T06:29:42+00:00
Comments: ACL Main
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reward models (RMs) are central to reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), providing the critical supervision signals that align large language models (LLMs) with human preferences. Generative reward models (GRMs) provide greater interpretability than traditional scalar RMs, but they come with a critical trade-off: pairwise methods are hindered by a training-inference mismatch, while pointwise methods require expensive absolute annotations. To bridge this gap, we propose the Preference-aware Task-adaptive Reward Model (PaTaRM). Unlike prior approaches, PaTaRM enables robust pointwise training using readily available pairwise data via a novel Preference-Aware Reward (PAR) mechanism, eliminating the need for explicit rating labels. Furthermore, it incorporates a Task-Adaptive Rubric system that dynamically generates instance-specific criteria for precise evaluation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that PATRM achieves a 8.7% average improvement on RewardBench and RMBench across Qwen3-8B/14B models. Crucially, it boosts downstream RLHF performance by an average relative improvement of 13.6% across IFEval and InFoBench, validating its effectiveness for policy alignment. Our code is available at https://github.com/JaneEyre0530/PaTaRM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PaTaRM：通过偏好感知任务自适应奖励建模桥接成对与点对信号
奖励模型（RMs）是基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）的核心，为对齐大语言模型（LLMs）与人类偏好提供关键监督信号。生成式奖励模型（GRMs）比传统标量RMs具有更强的可解释性，但面临关键权衡：成对方法受限于训练-推理不匹配，而点对方法需要昂贵的绝对标注。为弥合此差距，我们提出偏好感知任务自适应奖励模型（PaTaRM）。与先前方法不同，PaTaRM通过新颖的偏好感知奖励（PAR）机制，利用现成的成对数据实现鲁棒的点对训练，无需显式评分标签。此外，它集成了任务自适应准则系统，动态生成实例特定标准以进行精确评估。大量实验表明，PaTaRM在Qwen3-8B/14B模型上，于RewardBench和RMBench平均提升8.7%。关键的是，其在IFEval和InFoBench的下游RLHF性能平均相对提升13.6%，验证了其对策略对齐的有效性。代码发布于https://github.com/JaneEyre0530/PaTaRM。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a key trade-off in generative reward models (GRMs) for aligning large language models with human preferences: pairwise methods suffer from training-inference mismatch, while pointwise methods require costly absolute annotations. To bridge this gap, the authors propose PaTaRM, a preference-aware task-adaptive reward model that enables robust pointwise training using readily available pairwise data via a novel preference-aware reward mechanism, eliminating the need for explicit rating labels, and incorporates a task-adaptive rubric system for dynamic, instance-specific evaluation criteria. Experimental results show that PaTaRM achieves an average 8.7% improvement on RewardBench and RMBench across Qwen3-8B/14B models and boosts downstream RLHF performance by an average relative improvement of 13.6% on IFEval and InFoBench, validating its effectiveness for policy alignment.
该论文针对用于对齐大语言模型与人类偏好的生成式奖励模型（GRMs）中的一个关键权衡问题：成对方法存在训练-推理不匹配，而逐点方法需要昂贵的绝对标注。为弥补这一差距，作者提出了PaTaRM，一种偏好感知的任务自适应奖励模型，它通过新颖的偏好感知奖励机制，利用现成的成对数据实现稳健的逐点训练，无需显式评分标签，并集成了一个任务自适应规则系统，用于动态生成实例特定的评估标准。实验结果表明，PaTaRM在Qwen3-8B/14B模型上于RewardBench和RMBench上平均提升了8.7%，并在IFEval和InFoBench上使下游RLHF性能平均相对提升了13.6%，验证了其在策略对齐方面的有效性。
End-to-End Optimization of LLM-Driven Multi-Agent Search Systems via Heterogeneous-Group-Based Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Guanzhong Chen, Shaoxiong Yang, Chao Li, Wei Liu, Jian Luan, Zenglin Xu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-06-03T10:17:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T04:45:22+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 Main Conference. 20 pages, 9 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are versatile, yet their deployment in complex real-world settings is limited by static knowledge cutoffs and the difficulty of producing controllable behavior within a single inference. Multi-agent search systems (MASS), which coordinate specialized LLM agents equipped with search tools, mitigate these issues via task decomposition and retrieval-augmented problem solving. However, optimizing LLMs for agent-specific roles remains labor-intensive with prompt engineering or supervised fine-tuning, motivating automated end-to-end training. Existing multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) methods such as Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (MAPPO) typically depend on large critic networks to evaluate joint actions, leading to instability and high memory costs. We introduce Multi-Agent Heterogeneous Group Policy Optimization (MHGPO), which updates policies by estimating relative advantages across heterogeneous groups of multi-agent rollouts, shifting the optimization focus from local agent performance to global system success. We further study three group rollout sampling strategies to trade off sample efficiency and optimization quality. Experiments show that MHGPO captures implicit inter-agent dependencies and consistently outperforms strong baselines in both task performance and computational efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于异构群体强化学习的LLM驱动多智能体搜索系统端到端优化
大语言模型（LLMs）功能多样，但其在复杂现实场景中的部署受限于静态知识截止点及单次推理中难以实现可控行为。多智能体搜索系统（MASS）通过协调配备搜索工具的专用LLM智能体，借助任务分解与检索增强的问题解决机制缓解了这些问题。然而，通过提示工程或有监督微调为特定智能体角色优化LLMs仍属劳动密集型工作，这推动了自动化端到端训练的需求。现有多智能体强化学习（MARL）方法（如多智能体近端策略优化MAPPO）通常依赖大型评价器网络评估联合动作，导致训练不稳定与高内存开销。本文提出多智能体异构群体策略优化（MHGPO），该方法通过估计异构多智能体轨迹群体间的相对优势来更新策略，将优化重点从局部智能体性能转向全局系统成功。我们进一步研究了三种群体轨迹采样策略以权衡样本效率与优化质量。实验表明，MHGPO能够捕捉智能体间的隐式依赖关系，在任务性能与计算效率方面均持续优于现有强基线方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of optimizing large language model (LLM)-driven multi-agent search systems, where traditional methods like prompt engineering or supervised fine-tuning are labor-intensive, and existing multi-agent reinforcement learning approaches suffer from instability and high memory costs. The authors propose Multi-Agent Heterogeneous Group Policy Optimization (MHGPO), a method that updates policies by estimating relative advantages across heterogeneous groups of multi-agent rollouts, thereby shifting the optimization focus from individual agent performance to global system success. Experimental results demonstrate that MHGPO effectively captures implicit inter-agent dependencies and consistently outperforms strong baselines in both task performance and computational efficiency, with further analysis of group rollout sampling strategies to balance sample efficiency and optimization quality.
本文针对大语言模型驱动的多智能体搜索系统优化问题展开研究，传统方法如提示工程或监督微调需要大量人工，而现有的多智能体强化学习方法存在不稳定性和高内存开销。作者提出了多智能体异构群体策略优化方法，通过估计异构多智能体轨迹组间的相对优势来更新策略，从而将优化重点从单个智能体性能转向全局系统成功。实验结果表明，该方法能有效捕捉智能体间的隐式依赖关系，在任务性能和计算效率上均优于现有基线，并进一步分析了群体轨迹采样策略以权衡样本效率与优化质量。
STRIDE-ED: A Strategy-Grounded Stepwise Reasoning Framework for Empathetic Dialogue Systems
Authors: Hongru Ji, Yuyin Fan, Meng Zhao, Xianghua Li, Lianwei Wu, Chao Gao
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-08T13:53:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T03:55:13+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Empathetic dialogue requires not only recognizing a user's emotional state but also making strategy-aware, context-sensitive decisions throughout response generation. However, the lack of a comprehensive empathy strategy framework, explicit task-aligned multi-stage reasoning, and high-quality strategy-aware data fundamentally limits existing approaches, preventing them from effectively modeling empathetic dialogue as a complex, multi-stage cognitive and decision-making process. To address these challenges, we propose STRIDE-ED, a STRategy-grounded, Interpretable, and DEep reasoning framework that models Empathetic Dialogue through structured, strategy-conditioned reasoning. To support effective learning, we develop a strategy-aware data refinement pipeline integrating LLM-based annotation, multi-model consistency-weighted evaluation, and dynamic sampling to construct high-quality training data aligned with empathetic strategies. Furthermore, we adopt a two-stage training paradigm that combines supervised fine-tuning with multi-objective reinforcement learning to better align model behaviors with target emotions, empathetic strategies, and response formats. Extensive experiments demonstrate that STRIDE-ED generalizes across diverse open-source LLMs and consistently outperforms existing methods on both automatic metrics and human evaluations. Our data and code are publicly available at https://github.com/jicoder-nwpu/STRIDE-ED.
中文标题/摘要
标题：STRIDE-ED：基于策略的渐进式推理框架用于共情对话系统
共情对话不仅需要识别用户情绪状态，更需在响应生成过程中进行策略感知、情境敏感的决策。然而，现有方法因缺乏完整的共情策略框架、明确任务对齐的多阶段推理机制及高质量策略感知数据，难以将共情对话有效建模为复杂的多阶段认知决策过程。为此，我们提出STRIDE-ED——一个基于策略、可解释的深度推理框架，通过结构化策略条件推理建模共情对话。为支持有效学习，我们开发了策略感知数据精炼流程，集成基于大语言模型的标注、多模型一致性加权评估和动态采样，构建与共情策略对齐的高质量训练数据。此外，采用监督微调与多目标强化学习相结合的两阶段训练范式，使模型行为更好地对齐目标情绪、共情策略及响应格式。大量实验表明，STRIDE-ED能泛化至多种开源大语言模型，在自动指标和人工评估中均持续优于现有方法。数据与代码已公开于https://github.com/jicoder-nwpu/STRIDE-ED。

Reverse Constitutional AI: A Framework for Controllable Toxic Data Generation via Probability-Clamped RLAIF
Authors: Yuan Fang, Yiming Luo, Aimin Zhou, Fei Tan
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-20T03:49:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T03:49:25+00:00
Comments: Accepted to Findings of ACL 2026. 10 pages, 6 figures. Code and data available at https://github.com/ZeroLoss-Lab/R-CAI
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Ensuring the safety of large language models (LLMs) requires robust red teaming, yet the systematic synthesis of high-quality toxic data remains under-explored. We propose Reverse Constitutional AI (R-CAI), a framework for automated and controllable adversarial data generation that moves beyond isolated jailbreak prompts. By inverting a harmless constitution into a constitution of toxicity and iteratively refining model outputs through a critique--revision pipeline, R-CAI enables scalable synthesis of multi-dimensional adversarial data without human annotation. Optimizing solely for toxicity-related rewards, however, can lead to reward hacking and degraded semantic coherence. To address this challenge, we introduce probability clamping within reinforcement learning from AI feedback, which stabilizes adversarial optimization while preserving adversarial intent. Experiments demonstrate that R-CAI generates diverse, high-quality toxic data and that probability clamping substantially improves semantic coherence (15%) without sacrificing adversarial strength. Overall, R-CAI provides a fully automated framework for red teaming data generation and systematic safety evaluation of aligned language models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：逆向宪法AI：基于概率钳位RLAIF的可控毒性数据生成框架
确保大语言模型（LLMs）的安全性需要强大的红队测试，但高质量毒性数据的系统性合成仍待深入探索。本文提出逆向宪法AI（R-CAI）框架，通过超越孤立越狱提示的自动化可控对抗数据生成方法，将无害宪法逆向转化为毒性宪法，并借助“批判-修订”流程迭代优化模型输出，实现无需人工标注的多维度对抗数据规模化合成。然而，仅针对毒性相关奖励进行优化可能导致奖励破解和语义连贯性下降。为此，我们在基于AI反馈的强化学习中引入概率钳位机制，在保持对抗意图的同时稳定对抗优化过程。实验表明，R-CAI能生成多样化高质量的毒性数据，且概率钳位机制在不牺牲对抗强度的前提下显著提升语义连贯性（15%）。总体而言，R-CAI为对齐语言模型的自动化红队数据生成与系统性安全评估提供了完整框架。

The paper is motivated by the need for robust red teaming to ensure large language model safety, addressing the under-exploration of systematic high-quality toxic data synthesis. It proposes Reverse Constitutional AI (R-CAI), a framework that inverts a harmless constitution into a toxicity constitution and uses a critique-revision pipeline to iteratively refine outputs, enabling scalable, multi-dimensional adversarial data generation without human annotation. To prevent reward hacking and maintain semantic coherence during toxicity optimization, the method introduces probability clamping within reinforcement learning from AI feedback. Experimental results show that R-CAI produces diverse, high-quality toxic data, with probability clamping improving semantic coherence by 15% without compromising adversarial strength, offering a fully automated framework for red teaming and safety evaluation.
本文的动机是确保大语言模型安全需要强大的红队测试，而系统性的高质量有害数据生成仍未被充分探索。作者提出了反向宪法人工智能框架，通过将无害宪法反转为有害宪法，并利用批评-修订流程迭代优化模型输出，实现了无需人工标注、可扩展的多维度对抗数据生成。为解决单纯优化毒性奖励导致的奖励破解和语义连贯性下降问题，该方法在基于AI反馈的强化学习中引入了概率钳制技术以稳定对抗优化。实验结果表明，该框架能生成多样化的高质量有害数据，且概率钳制在不削弱对抗强度的前提下将语义连贯性提升了15%，为红队数据生成和对齐模型的安全评估提供了一个全自动框架。
FaithLens: Detecting and Explaining Faithfulness Hallucination
Authors: Shuzheng Si, Qingyi Wang, Haozhe Zhao, Yuzhuo Bai, Guanqiao Chen, Kangyang Luo, Gang Chen, Fanchao Qi, Minjia Zhang, Baobao Chang, Maosong Sun
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-12-23T09:20:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T03:32:02+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 (Findings)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recognizing whether outputs from large language models (LLMs) contain faithfulness hallucination is crucial for real-world applications, e.g., retrieval-augmented generation and summarization. In this paper, we introduce FaithLens, a cost-efficient and effective faithfulness hallucination detection model that can jointly provide binary predictions and corresponding explanations to improve trustworthiness. To achieve this, we first synthesize training data with explanations via advanced LLMs and apply a well-defined data filtering strategy to ensure label correctness, explanation quality, and data diversity. Subsequently, we fine-tune the model on these well-curated training data as a cold start and further optimize it with rule-based reinforcement learning, using rewards for both prediction correctness and explanation quality. Results on 12 diverse tasks show that the 8B-parameter FaithLens outperforms advanced models such as GPT-5.2 and o3. Also, FaithLens can produce high-quality explanations, delivering a distinctive balance of trustworthiness, efficiency, and effectiveness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FaithLens：检测与解释忠实性幻觉
识别大语言模型输出是否包含忠实性幻觉对实际应用至关重要，例如检索增强生成与文本摘要。本文提出FaithLens——一种高效经济的忠实性幻觉检测模型，可同时提供二元预测及相应解释以增强可信度。我们首先通过先进大语言模型合成含解释的训练数据，并采用严格的数据过滤策略确保标签准确性、解释质量与数据多样性。随后基于这些高质量训练数据进行冷启动微调，并通过基于规则的强化学习进一步优化模型，其奖励机制同时考量预测准确性与解释质量。在12项多样化任务上的实验表明，80亿参数的FaithLens在性能上超越GPT-5.2及o3等先进模型，且能生成高质量解释，在可信度、效率与效能间实现卓越平衡。
