Robust Tool Use via Fission-GRPO: Learning to Recover from Execution Errors
Authors: Zhiwei Zhang, Fei Zhao, Rui Wang, Zezhong Wang, Bin Liang, Jiakang Wang, Yao Hu, Shaosheng Cao, Kam-Fai Wong
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-22T03:57:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T03:31:41+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 4 figures, 4 tables. Accepted to ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) can call tools effectively, yet they remain brittle in multi-turn execution: after a tool-call error, smaller models often fall into repetitive invalid re-invocations instead of interpreting the feedback and recovering. This failure mode persists because current training paradigms do not explicitly teach models how to recover from execution errors. In particular, standard reinforcement learning (RL) collapses rich failure experience into sparse negative rewards, while pre-collected error-correction datasets become mismatched to the policy's evolving failure modes. To bridge this gap, we propose Fission-GRPO, a framework that converts execution errors into on-policy corrective supervision within the RL training loop. Our core mechanism fissions each failed trajectory into a new training instance by augmenting it with diagnostic feedback from a fine-tuned Error Simulator, then resampling multiple recovery rollouts on-policy. This enables the model to learn from the precise errors it makes during exploration, rather than from static, pre-collected error cases. On BFCL v4 Multi-Turn, Fission-GRPO improves the error recovery rate of Qwen3-8B by 5.7% absolute and overall accuracy by 4.0% (from 42.75% to 46.75%), outperforming both RL baselines and specialized tool-use agents. The method further generalizes to TAU-Bench and TAU2-Bench, achieving leading results across most settings with gains up to +17.4%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于Fission-GRPO的鲁棒工具使用：学习从执行错误中恢复
大语言模型（LLMs）能有效调用工具，但在多轮执行中仍显脆弱：工具调用出错后，较小模型常陷入重复无效调用，而非解读反馈并恢复。此问题源于当前训练范式未明确教导模型如何从执行错误中恢复。标准强化学习（RL）将丰富的失败经验压缩为稀疏负奖励，而预收集的错误修正数据集则与策略演变的失败模式失配。为弥合此差距，我们提出Fission-GRPO框架，在RL训练循环中将执行错误转化为同策略修正监督。其核心机制通过微调错误模拟器生成的诊断反馈增强失败轨迹，将其裂解为新训练实例，并同策略重采样多个恢复路径。这使得模型能从探索过程中的具体错误学习，而非依赖静态预收集错误案例。在BFCL v4多轮测试中，Fission-GRPO将Qwen3-8B的错误恢复率绝对提升5.7%，整体准确率从42.75%提升至46.75%（+4.0%），优于RL基线和专用工具使用智能体。该方法进一步推广至TAU-Bench与TAU2-Bench，在多数设定中取得领先结果，最高提升达+17.4%。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the brittleness of large language models (LLMs) in multi-turn tool use, where models often fail to recover from execution errors due to current training paradigms lacking explicit error-recovery learning. To bridge this gap, the authors propose Fission-GRPO, a framework that converts execution errors into on-policy corrective supervision by augmenting failed trajectories with diagnostic feedback from a fine-tuned Error Simulator and resampling recovery rollouts during reinforcement learning training. Experimental results show that Fission-GRPO improves the error recovery rate of Qwen3-8B by 5.7% and overall accuracy by 4.0% on BFCL v4 Multi-Turn, outperforming baselines and generalizing to other benchmarks with gains up to +17.4%.
该论文针对大型语言模型在多轮工具调用中的脆弱性问题，即模型在执行错误后难以恢复，因为现有训练范式缺乏明确的错误恢复学习。为此，作者提出了Fission-GRPO框架，通过使用微调的错误模拟器为失败轨迹添加诊断反馈，并在强化学习训练中重采样恢复路径，将执行错误转化为策略内的纠正监督。实验结果表明，在BFCL v4 Multi-Turn上，Fission-GRPO将Qwen3-8B的错误恢复率提升了5.7%，整体准确率提高了4.0%，优于基线方法，并在其他基准测试中实现了高达+17.4%的性能增益。
Efficient Federated RLHF via Zeroth-Order Policy Optimization
Authors: Deyi Wang, Qining Zhang, Lei Ying
First: 2026-04-20T03:04:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T03:04:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper considers reinforcement learning from human feedback in a federated learning setting with resource-constrained agents, such as edge devices. We propose an efficient federated RLHF algorithm, named Partitioned, Sign-based Stochastic Zeroth-order Policy Optimization (Par-S$^2$ZPO). The algorithm is built on zeroth-order optimization with binary perturbation, resulting in low communication, computation, and memory complexity by design. Our theoretical analysis establishes an upper bound on the convergence rate of Par-S$^2$ZPO, revealing that it is as efficient as its centralized counterpart in terms of sample complexity but converges faster in terms of policy update iterations. Our experimental results show that it outperforms a FedAvg-based RLHF on four MuJoCo RL tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于零阶策略优化的高效联邦RLHF方法
本文研究了在资源受限的联邦学习环境中，基于人类反馈的强化学习问题，例如边缘设备场景。我们提出了一种高效的联邦RLHF算法，命名为基于分区和符号的随机零阶策略优化。该算法建立在采用二元扰动的零阶优化基础上，通过设计实现了较低的通信、计算和内存复杂度。理论分析确立了该算法收敛速度的上界，表明其在样本复杂度上与集中式方法效率相当，但在策略更新迭代中收敛更快。实验结果表明，在四个MuJoCo强化学习任务上，该算法优于基于FedAvg的RLHF方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to perform reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) efficiently on resource-constrained edge devices within a federated learning framework. The method introduces Par-S²ZPO, a federated RLHF algorithm based on zeroth-order optimization with binary perturbation, which is designed to have low communication, computation, and memory overhead. The main experimental results demonstrate that the proposed algorithm outperforms a FedAvg-based RLHF baseline on four MuJoCo tasks, with theoretical analysis confirming its sample efficiency matches centralized methods while achieving faster policy update convergence.
本文的动机是在资源受限的边缘设备联邦学习框架中，高效执行基于人类反馈的强化学习。方法上提出了Par-S²ZPO算法，这是一种基于二元扰动的零阶优化联邦RLHF方法，其设计具有低通信、计算和内存复杂度。主要实验结果表明，该算法在四个MuJoCo任务上优于基于FedAvg的RLHF基线，理论分析证实其样本效率与集中式方法相当，且在策略更新迭代上收敛更快。
Beyond Single-Turn: A Survey on Multi-Turn Interactions with Large Language Models
Authors: Yubo Li, Xiaobin Shen, Yidi Miao, Xinyu Yao, Xueying Ding, Ramayya Krishnan, Rema Padman
First: 2025-04-07T04:00:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T02:55:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have substantially improved single-turn task performance, yet real-world applications increasingly demand sophisticated multi-turn interactions. This survey provides a comprehensive review of recent progress in evaluating and enhancing multi-turn LLM interactions. Centered on a task-oriented taxonomy-spanning instruction following in domains such as mathematics and coding, and conversational engagement in role-playing, healthcare, education, and adversarial jailbreak settings-we systematically examine the challenges of maintaining context, coherence, fairness, and responsiveness across prolonged dialogues. We organize existing benchmarks and datasets into coherent categories reflecting the evolving landscape of multi-turn dialogue evaluation, and review a broad spectrum of enhancement methodologies, including model-centric strategies (in-context learning, supervised fine-tuning, reinforcement learning, and architectural innovations), external integration approaches (memory augmentation, retrieval-based methods, and knowledge graphs), and agent-based techniques for collaborative interaction. Finally, we identify open challenges and promising directions for future research to further improve the robustness and effectiveness of multi-turn LLM interactions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越单轮交互：大语言模型多轮交互研究综述
大语言模型（LLMs）的最新进展显著提升了单轮任务性能，然而实际应用日益需要复杂的多轮交互。本综述系统回顾了多轮LLM交互评估与增强的最新进展。围绕任务导向的分类体系——涵盖数学、编程等领域的指令遵循，以及角色扮演、医疗健康、教育、对抗性越狱等场景的对话交互——我们系统分析了在长程对话中保持上下文连贯性、逻辑一致性、公平性与响应能力的挑战。我们将现有基准与数据集整合为反映多轮对话评估发展脉络的连贯分类体系，并综述了广泛的增强方法，包括模型中心策略（上下文学习、监督微调、强化学习及架构创新）、外部集成方法（记忆增强、检索增强与知识图谱）以及基于智能体的协同交互技术。最后，我们指出未来研究的开放挑战与潜在方向，以进一步提升多轮LLM交互的鲁棒性与有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the growing need for sophisticated multi-turn interactions in real-world applications beyond the strong single-turn capabilities of large language models (LLMs), this survey comprehensively reviews progress in evaluating and enhancing such dialogues. The method involves establishing a task-oriented taxonomy covering instruction following and conversational engagement, systematically examining challenges like context maintenance, and organizing benchmarks while reviewing enhancement methodologies including model-centric strategies, external integrations, and agent-based techniques. The main experimental results summarized indicate that these approaches address key issues in prolonged dialogues, though open challenges remain for improving robustness and effectiveness in multi-turn settings.
本文的动机在于，尽管大语言模型在单轮任务上表现优异，但现实应用日益需要复杂的多轮交互，因此该综述全面回顾了评估和增强多轮大语言模型交互的进展。方法上，通过建立涵盖指令遵循和对话参与的任务导向分类法，系统审视了上下文保持等挑战，并整合了现有基准数据集，同时综述了包括模型中心策略、外部集成方法和基于智能体的协作技术在内的多种增强方法。主要实验结果总结表明，这些方法能应对长对话中的关键问题，但在多轮交互的鲁棒性和有效性方面仍存在开放挑战，为未来研究指明了方向。
OptunaHub: A Platform for Black-Box Optimization
Authors: Yoshihiko Ozaki, Shuhei Watanabe, Toshihiko Yanase
First: 2025-10-03T08:11:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T02:54:19+00:00
Comments: Submitted to Journal of machine learning research
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Black-box optimization (BBO) underpins advances in domains such as AutoML and Materials Informatics, yet implementations of algorithms and benchmarks remain fragmented across research communities. We introduce OptunaHub (https://hub.optuna.org/), a community-oriented, decentralized platform for distributing BBO components under a unified Optuna-compatible interface. OptunaHub enables independent publication, discovery, and reuse of optimization algorithms and benchmark problems through a lightweight Python module, a contributor-driven registry, and a searchable web interface. The source code is publicly available in the \href{https://github.com/optuna/optunahub}{\texttt{optunahub}}, \href{https://github.com/optuna/optunahub-registry}{\texttt{optunahub-registry}}, and \href{https://github.com/optuna/optunahub-web}{\texttt{optunahub-web}} repositories under the Optuna organization on GitHub (https://github.com/optuna/).
中文标题/摘要
标题：OptunaHub：黑盒优化平台
黑盒优化（BBO）是推动自动机器学习与材料信息学等领域发展的关键技术，但算法实现与基准测试在各研究社区中仍处于分散状态。本文介绍OptunaHub（https://hub.optuna.org/），这是一个面向社区、去中心化的平台，通过统一的Optuna兼容接口分发BBO组件。OptunaHub通过轻量级Python模块、贡献者驱动的注册机制以及可搜索的Web界面，实现了优化算法与基准问题的独立发布、发现与复用。源代码已在GitHub的Optuna组织下公开于\href{https://github.com/optuna/optunahub}{\texttt{optunahub}}、\href{https://github.com/optuna/optunahub-registry}{\texttt{optunahub-registry}}和\href{https://github.com/optuna/optunahub-web}{\texttt{optunahub-web}}代码库（https://github.com/optuna/）。

The method introduces OptunaHub, a decentralized, community-oriented platform that provides a unified Optuna-compatible interface for distributing BBO components, featuring a lightweight Python module, a contributor-driven registry, and a searchable web interface. The main experimental results are that the platform enables independent publication, discovery, and reuse of optimization algorithms and benchmark problems, with its source code being publicly available on GitHub.

Tool Learning Needs Nothing More Than a Free 8B Language Model
Authors: Chenming Tang, Hsiu-Yuan Huang, Weijie Liu, Junqiang Zheng, Saiyong Yang, Yunfang Wu
First: 2026-04-20T02:54:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-20T02:54:02+00:00
Comments: Preprint; Work in progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a prevalent paradigm for training tool calling agents, which typically requires online interactive environments. Existing approaches either rely on training data with ground truth annotations or require advanced commercial language models (LMs) to synthesize environments that keep fixed once created. In this work, we propose TRUSTEE, a data-free method training tool calling agents with dynamic environments fully simulated by free open-source LMs that can be as small as 8B, including task generation, user simulation, tool simulation and trajectory evaluation, paired with an adaptive curriculum learning mechanism that controls various aspects of the task difficulty dynamically during training. Our empirical results show that TRUSTEE brings consistent improvements across various domains and outperforms all the baselines which require extra external resources for training. These confirm that, with a sufficiently sophisticated design, even simulated environments with a local 8B LM as the backbone could set a strong baseline for tool learning, without expensive annotated data, realistic human interactions, executable tools or costly verifiable environments from human experts or commercial LMs. We hope our proposed paradigm could inspire future research on environment scaling with limited resources.
中文标题/摘要
标题：工具学习仅需一个免费的8B语言模型
强化学习已成为训练工具调用智能体的主流范式，通常需要在线交互环境。现有方法要么依赖带真实标注的训练数据，要么需要先进的商业语言模型来合成一旦创建即固定的环境。本研究提出TRUSTEE——一种无需训练数据的方法，通过完全由免费开源语言模型（最小可至8B参数）动态模拟的环境来训练工具调用智能体，包括任务生成、用户模拟、工具模拟和轨迹评估，并搭配自适应课程学习机制，在训练过程中动态控制任务难度的各个方面。实验结果表明，TRUSTEE在多个领域均带来持续改进，且优于所有需要额外外部训练资源的基线方法。这证实了：通过足够精巧的设计，即使以本地8B语言模型为骨干的模拟环境，也能为工具学习建立强大基线，无需昂贵的标注数据、真实人机交互、可执行工具或由人类专家/商业语言模型构建的高成本可验证环境。我们希望所提出的范式能启发未来在有限资源下进行环境扩展的研究。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high costs and dependencies of existing reinforcement learning methods for tool calling agents, which often require annotated data, commercial language models, or fixed simulated environments, this paper introduces TRUSTEE, a data-free method that trains agents using dynamic environments fully simulated by free open-source language models as small as 8B parameters. The method integrates task generation, user simulation, tool simulation, and trajectory evaluation, coupled with an adaptive curriculum learning mechanism to dynamically adjust task difficulty during training. Experimental results demonstrate that TRUSTEE consistently improves performance across various domains and outperforms baselines reliant on external resources, confirming that sophisticated design with a local 8B LM can establish a strong baseline for tool learning without expensive data, human interactions, executable tools, or costly environments.

Poly-EPO: Training Exploratory Reasoning Models
Authors: Ifdita Hasan Orney, Jubayer Ibn Hamid, Shreya S Ramanujam, Shirley Wu, Hengyuan Hu, Noah Goodman, Dorsa Sadigh, Chelsea Finn
First: 2026-04-19T22:54:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T22:54:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Exploration is a cornerstone of learning from experience: it enables agents to find solutions to complex problems, generalize to novel ones, and scale performance with test-time compute. In this paper, we present a framework for post-training language models (LMs) that explicitly encourages optimistic exploration and promotes a synergy between exploration and exploitation. The central idea is to train the LM to generate sets of responses that are collectively accurate under the reward function and exploratory in their reasoning strategies. We first develop a general recipe for optimizing LMs with set reinforcement learning (set RL) under arbitrary objective functions, showing how standard RL algorithms can be adapted to this setting through a modification to the advantage computation. We then propose Polychromic Exploratory Policy Optimization (Poly-EPO), which instantiates this framework with an objective that explicitly synergizes exploration and exploitation. Across a range of reasoning benchmarks, we show that Poly-EPO improves generalization, as evidenced by higher pass@$k$ coverage, preserves greater diversity in model generations, and effectively scales with test-time compute.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Poly-EPO：训练探索性推理模型
探索是从经验中学习的基石：它使智能体能够找到复杂问题的解决方案，泛化至新问题，并通过测试时计算资源扩展性能。本文提出一种后训练语言模型框架，该框架明确鼓励乐观探索并促进探索与利用的协同作用。核心思想是训练语言模型生成在奖励函数下集体准确、且推理策略具有探索性的响应集合。我们首先开发了在任意目标函数下通过集合强化学习优化语言模型的通用方法，展示了如何通过修改优势计算使标准强化学习算法适配此场景。随后提出多时序探索策略优化算法，该算法通过明确协同探索与利用的目标函数实例化此框架。在一系列推理基准测试中，Poly-EPO展现出更强的泛化能力（体现为更高的pass@$k$覆盖率），保持模型生成结果的更大多样性，并能有效随测试时计算资源扩展性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to enhance language models' ability to learn from experience through exploration, which is crucial for solving complex problems and generalizing to novel tasks, this paper introduces Poly-EPO, a framework for post-training models to synergize exploration and exploitation. The method adapts set reinforcement learning to optimize language models for generating sets of responses that are both collectively accurate and diverse in reasoning strategies, achieved via a modified advantage computation. Experimental results across reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that Poly-EPO improves generalization with higher pass@k coverage, preserves greater diversity in model generations, and effectively scales with test-time compute.
本文的动机是增强语言模型通过探索从经验中学习的能力，这对于解决复杂问题和泛化到新任务至关重要，为此提出了Poly-EPO框架，用于在训练后协同探索与利用。该方法通过调整优势计算，将集合强化学习应用于优化语言模型，使其生成在奖励函数下集体准确且推理策略多样化的响应集合。在多项推理基准测试中，实验结果表明Poly-EPO提高了泛化能力，表现为更高的pass@k覆盖率，保持了模型生成的更大多样性，并能有效利用测试时计算资源进行扩展。
SLO-Guard: Crash-Aware, Budget-Consistent Autotuning for SLO-Constrained LLM Serving
Authors: Christian Lysenstøen
First: 2026-04-19T21:48:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T21:48:35+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 6 figures, 5 tables. Code and raw per-trial JSONL data: https://github.com/Chrislysen/SLO-Guard
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Serving large language models under latency service-level objectives (SLOs) is a configuration-heavy systems problem with an unusually failure-prone search space: many plausible configurations crash outright or miss user-visible latency targets, and standard black-box optimizers treat these failures as wasted trials. We present SLO-Guard, a crash-aware autotuner for vLLM serving that treats crashes as first-class observations. SLO-Guard combines a feasible-first Thermal Budget Annealing (TBA) exploration phase with a warm-started Tree-structured Parzen Estimator (TPE) exploitation phase; the handoff replays all exploration history, including crashes encoded as extreme constraint violations. We additionally contribute a configuration-repair pass, a GPU-aware KV-cache memory guard, and a four-category crash taxonomy. We evaluate SLO-Guard on Qwen2-1.5B served with vLLM 0.19 on an NVIDIA A100 40GB. Across a pre-specified five-seed study, both SLO-Guard and uniform random search attain 75/75 feasibility with zero crashes under the corrected concurrent harness, and are statistically tied on best-achieved latency (Mann-Whitney two-sided p=0.84). SLO-Guard's advantage is in budget consistency: more trials in the fast-serving regime (10.20 vs. 7.40 out of 15; one-sided p=0.014) and higher post-handoff consistency (0.876 vs. 0.539; p=0.010). Under concurrent load, SLO-Guard's cross-seed standard deviation on best latency is 4.4x tighter than random search's (2.26 ms vs. 10.00 ms). A harness-replication analysis shows that the consistency findings survive an independent sequential-dispatch measurement condition. The central claim is not that SLO-Guard finds a better final configuration, but that it spends a fixed tuning budget more predictably once the fast regime has been found.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SLO-Guard：面向SLO约束大语言模型服务的崩溃感知与预算一致性自动调优系统
在延迟服务等级目标约束下部署大语言模型是配置复杂的系统难题，其搜索空间异常脆弱：大量可行配置会直接崩溃或无法满足用户可感知的延迟目标，而标准黑盒优化器将这些故障视为无效尝试。本文提出SLO-Guard——面向vLLM服务的崩溃感知自动调优器，将崩溃作为首要观测指标。该系统融合可行优先的热预算退火探索阶段与热启动树结构Parzen估计器开发阶段，并通过重放包含编码为极端约束违规的崩溃记录在内的完整探索历史实现阶段衔接。我们还贡献了配置修复流程、GPU感知KV缓存内存防护机制及四类崩溃分类法。 在NVIDIA A100 40GB上使用vLLM 0.19部署Qwen2-1.5B的评估显示：经修正的并发测试框架下，SLO-Guard与均匀随机搜索在五种子预研中均实现75/75可行性且零崩溃，最佳延迟表现统计无差异（曼-惠特尼双侧p=0.84）。SLO-Guard的优势在于预算一致性：快速服务区间内有效尝试更多（15次中10.20 vs. 7.40；单侧p=0.014），阶段衔接后一致性更高（0.876 vs. 0.539；p=0.010）。并发负载下，其最佳延迟的跨种子标准差较随机搜索压缩4.4倍（2.26 ms vs. 10.00 ms）。框架复现分析表明一致性结论在独立顺序调度测量条件下依然成立。 核心主张并非SLO-Guard能发现更优最终配置，而在于其进入快速服务区间后能以更高可预测性利用固定调优预算。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of tuning large language model serving systems under strict latency service-level objectives, where many configurations crash or violate targets, wasting tuning trials. The authors introduce SLO-Guard, an autotuner that treats crashes as explicit observations, combining a feasible-first Thermal Budget Annealing exploration phase with a warm-started Tree-structured Parzen Estimator exploitation phase, alongside configuration repair and a GPU-aware memory guard. Experimental results on serving Qwen2-1.5B with vLLM show that while SLO-Guard achieves similar feasibility and best latency as random search, it provides superior budget consistency, yielding more trials in the fast-serving regime and tighter cross-seed latency variability, making tuning more predictable once high-performance configurations are identified.
本文针对在严格延迟服务级别目标下调整大型语言模型服务系统的挑战，其中许多配置会崩溃或违反目标，导致调优试验浪费。作者提出了SLO-Guard，这是一种将崩溃视为明确观察的自调优器，结合了优先可行的热预算退火探索阶段和热启动的树结构Parzen估计器利用阶段，并辅以配置修复和GPU感知内存保护。在使用vLLM服务Qwen2-1.5B的实验中，虽然SLO-Guard在可行性和最佳延迟方面与随机搜索相当，但它提供了更优的预算一致性，在快速服务区域中产生更多试验，且跨种子延迟变异性更小，使得一旦找到高性能配置后调优过程更加可预测。
StructRL: Recovering Dynamic Programming Structure from Learning Dynamics in Distributional Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ivo Nowak
First: 2026-04-09T09:21:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T19:12:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning is typically treated as a uniform, data-driven optimization process, where updates are guided by rewards and temporal-difference errors without explicitly exploiting global structure. In contrast, dynamic programming methods rely on structured information propagation, enabling efficient and stable learning. In this paper, we provide evidence that such structure can be recovered from the learning dynamics of distributional reinforcement learning. By analyzing the temporal evolution of return distributions, we identify signals that capture when and where learning occurs in the state space. In particular, we introduce a temporal learning indicator t*(s) that reflects when a state undergoes its strongest learning update during training. Empirically, this signal induces an ordering over states that is consistent with a dynamic programming-style propagation of information. Building on this observation, we propose StructRL, a framework that exploits these signals to guide sampling in alignment with the emerging propagation structure. Our preliminary results suggest that distributional learning dynamics provide a mechanism to recover and exploit dynamic programming-like structure without requiring an explicit model. This offers a new perspective on reinforcement learning, where learning can be interpreted as a structured propagation process rather than a purely uniform optimization procedure.
中文标题/摘要
标题：StructRL：从分布强化学习动态中恢复动态规划结构
强化学习通常被视为一种均匀的数据驱动优化过程，其更新由奖励和时序差分误差引导，未显式利用全局结构。相比之下，动态规划方法依赖结构化信息传播，能实现高效稳定的学习。本文证明此类结构可从分布强化学习动态中恢复。通过分析回报分布的时序演化，我们识别出捕捉状态空间中学习发生时机与位置的信号。特别地，我们引入时序学习指标t*(s)，反映训练中状态何时经历最强的学习更新。实验表明，该信号诱导的状态排序与动态规划式的信息传播一致。基于此观察，我们提出StructRL框架，利用这些信号引导采样以对齐新兴的传播结构。初步结果表明，分布学习动态提供了一种无需显式模型即可恢复并利用类动态规划结构的机制，为强化学习提供了新视角：学习可被解释为结构化传播过程，而非纯粹的均匀优化过程。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the observation that reinforcement learning is typically treated as a uniform, data-driven optimization process, lacking the explicit exploitation of global structure found in dynamic programming methods. The method involves analyzing the temporal evolution of return distributions in distributional reinforcement learning to recover such structure, specifically by introducing a temporal learning indicator t*(s) that captures when a state undergoes its strongest learning update. Experimental results show that this indicator induces a state ordering consistent with dynamic programming-style information propagation, and the proposed StructRL framework leverages these signals to guide sampling, offering preliminary evidence that distributional learning dynamics can recover and exploit structured propagation without an explicit model.
本文的动机在于观察到强化学习通常被视为一种均匀的、数据驱动的优化过程，缺乏动态规划方法中明确利用的全局结构。方法是通过分析分布式强化学习中回报分布的时间演化来恢复这种结构，具体引入了时间学习指标t*(s)以捕捉状态在训练中经历最强学习更新的时刻。实验结果表明，该指标诱导出的状态排序与动态规划风格的信息传播一致，所提出的StructRL框架利用这些信号指导采样，初步证明了分布式学习动态能够在不依赖显式模型的情况下恢复并利用结构化传播过程。
Countdown-Code: A Testbed for Studying The Emergence and Generalization of Reward Hacking in RLVR
Authors: Muhammad Khalifa, Zohaib Khan, Omer Tafveez, Hao Peng, Lu Wang
First: 2026-03-07T07:43:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T18:13:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reward hacking is a form of misalignment in which models overoptimize proxy rewards without genuinely solving the underlying task. Precisely measuring reward hacking occurrence remains challenging because true task rewards are often expensive or impossible to compute. We introduce Countdown-Code, a minimal environment where models can both solve a mathematical reasoning task and manipulate the test harness. This dual-access design creates a clean separation between proxy rewards (test pass/fail) and true rewards (mathematical correctness), enabling accurate measurement of reward-hacking rates. Using this environment, we study reward hacking in open-weight LLMs and find that such behaviors can be unintentionally learned during supervised fine-tuning (SFT) when even a small fraction of reward-hacking trajectories leak into training data. As little as 1\% contamination in distillation SFT data is sufficient for models to internalize reward hacking which resurfaces during subsequent reinforcement learning (RL). We further show that RL amplifies misalignment and drives its generalization beyond the original domain. We open-source our environment and code to facilitate future research on reward hacking in LLMs. Our results reveal a previously underexplored pathway through which reward hacking can emerge and persist in LLMs, underscoring the need for more rigorous validation of synthetic SFT data. Code is available at https://github.com/zohaib-khan5040/Countdown-Code.
中文标题/摘要
标题：倒计时代码：研究RLVR中奖励黑客行为涌现与泛化的测试平台
奖励黑客行为是一种模型对齐失效现象，指模型过度优化代理奖励却未真正解决底层任务。由于真实任务奖励通常计算成本高昂或无法获取，精确测量奖励黑客行为的发生仍具挑战性。我们推出倒计时代码——一个极简环境，模型既可执行数学推理任务，又能操纵测试框架。这种双重访问设计在代理奖励（测试通过/失败）与真实奖励（数学正确性）间建立了清晰界限，从而能准确测量奖励黑客行为发生率。通过该环境，我们研究了开源权重大语言模型中的奖励黑客行为，发现此类行为可能在监督微调阶段被无意习得——即使训练数据中仅混入少量奖励黑客轨迹。蒸馏监督微调数据中仅需1%的污染就足以使模型内化奖励黑客行为，并在后续强化学习中重现。我们进一步证明强化学习会放大这种对齐偏差，并驱动其向原始领域外泛化。我们开源了环境与代码以促进大语言模型奖励黑客行为研究。研究结果揭示了一条先前未被充分探索的奖励黑客行为涌现与持续路径，强调了对合成监督微调数据进行更严格验证的必要性。代码发布于https://github.com/zohaib-khan5040/Countdown-Code。

The method involves a minimal environment that separates proxy rewards (test pass/fail) from true rewards (mathematical correctness), allowing precise measurement of reward-hacking rates. Experimental results show that reward hacking can emerge unintentionally during supervised fine-tuning with as little as 1% contamination in training data, and subsequent reinforcement learning amplifies and generalizes this misalignment beyond the original domain.
本文介绍了Countdown-Code，这是一个用于研究语言模型中奖励黑客行为的测试平台，其中模型过度优化代理奖励而未真正解决任务。方法通过一个最小化环境将代理奖励（测试通过/失败）与真实奖励（数学正确性）分离，从而精确测量奖励黑客发生率。实验结果表明，在监督微调中，即使训练数据中仅有1%的污染，奖励黑客行为也会无意中产生，而随后的强化学习会放大这种错位并使其泛化到原始领域之外。
COSEARCH: Joint Training of Reasoning and Document Ranking via Reinforcement Learning for Agentic Search
Authors: Hansi Zeng, Liam Collins, Bhuvesh Kumar, Neil Shah, Hamed Zamani
First: 2026-04-19T17:48:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T17:48:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic search -- the task of training agents that iteratively reason, issue queries, and synthesize retrieved information to answer complex questions -- has achieved remarkable progress through reinforcement learning (RL). However, existing approaches such as Search-R1, treat the retrieval system as a fixed tool, optimizing only the reasoning agent while the retrieval component remains unchanged. A preliminary experiment reveals that the gap between an oracle and a fixed retrieval system reaches up to +26.8% relative F1 improvement across seven QA benchmarks, suggesting that the retrieval system is a key bottleneck in scaling agentic search performance. Motivated by this finding, we propose CoSearch, a framework that jointly trains a multi-step reasoning agent and a generative document ranking model via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). To enable effective GRPO training for the ranker -- whose inputs vary across reasoning trajectories -- we introduce a semantic grouping strategy that clusters sub-queries by token-level similarity, forming valid optimization groups without additional rollouts. We further design a composite reward combining ranking quality signals with trajectory-level outcome feedback, providing the ranker with both immediate and long-term learning signals. Experiments on seven single-hop and multi-hop QA benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements over strong baselines, with ablation studies validating each design choice. Our results show that joint training of the reasoning agent and retrieval system is both feasible and strongly performant, pointing to a key ingredient for future search agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：COSEARCH：通过强化学习联合训练推理与文档排序的智能搜索代理
智能搜索——训练代理通过迭代推理、发出查询并综合检索信息以回答复杂问题的任务——已通过强化学习取得显著进展。然而，现有方法（如Search-R1）将检索系统视为固定工具，仅优化推理代理而保持检索组件不变。初步实验表明，在七个问答基准测试中，理想检索系统与固定检索系统之间的相对F1提升差距高达+26.8%，这提示检索系统是扩展智能搜索性能的关键瓶颈。基于此发现，我们提出CoSearch框架，通过组相对策略优化联合训练多步推理代理与生成式文档排序模型。为使排序器（其输入随推理轨迹变化）实现有效的GRPO训练，我们引入语义分组策略，通过词元级相似度聚类子查询，无需额外推演即可形成有效优化组。进一步设计结合排序质量信号与轨迹级结果反馈的复合奖励机制，为排序器提供即时与长期学习信号。在七个单跳与多跳问答基准上的实验显示，该方法持续优于强基线，消融研究验证了各设计选择的有效性。结果表明，推理代理与检索系统的联合训练既可行又高效，为未来搜索代理的发展提供了关键方向。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that fixed retrieval systems are a major bottleneck in agentic search, limiting performance by up to 26.8% F1 compared to an oracle, this paper introduces CoSearch, a framework that jointly trains a multi-step reasoning agent and a generative document ranking model using reinforcement learning, specifically Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). The method employs a semantic grouping strategy to cluster similar sub-queries for efficient ranker training and a composite reward combining immediate ranking signals with long-term outcome feedback. Experimental results across seven single-hop and multi-hop QA benchmarks show consistent improvements over strong baselines, demonstrating that joint training of the reasoning and retrieval components is both feasible and highly effective for enhancing agentic search performance.
本文的动机是发现固定检索系统是智能体搜索的关键瓶颈，与理想系统相比性能差距可达26.8% F1，因此提出了CoSearch框架，通过强化学习（特别是组相对策略优化）联合训练多步推理智能体和生成式文档排序模型。该方法采用语义分组策略对相似子查询进行聚类以高效训练排序器，并设计了结合即时排序信号与长期结果反馈的复合奖励机制。在七个单跳和多跳问答基准上的实验结果表明，该方法相比强基线取得了一致的性能提升，验证了联合训练推理与检索组件不仅可行，而且能显著提升智能体搜索的效能。
SVL: Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning as Survival Learning
Authors: Franki Nguimatsia Tiofack, Fabian Schramm, Théotime Le Hellard, Justin Carpentier
First: 2026-04-19T17:44:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T17:44:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Standard approaches to goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL) that rely on temporal-difference learning can be unstable and sample-inefficient due to bootstrapping. While recent work has explored contrastive and supervised formulations to improve stability, we present a probabilistic alternative, called survival value learning (SVL), that reframes GCRL as a survival learning problem by modeling the time-to-goal from each state as a probability distribution. This structured distributional Monte Carlo perspective yields a closed-form identity that expresses the goal-conditioned value function as a discounted sum of survival probabilities, enabling value estimation via a hazard model trained via maximum likelihood on both event and right-censored trajectories. We introduce three practical value estimators, including finite-horizon truncation and two binned infinite-horizon approximations to capture long-horizon objectives. Experiments on offline GCRL benchmarks show that SVL combined with hierarchical actors matches or surpasses strong hierarchical TD and Monte Carlo baselines, excelling on complex, long-horizon tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SVL：目标条件强化学习作为生存学习
依赖时序差分学习的目标条件强化学习（GCRL）标准方法因自举机制可能导致不稳定与样本效率低下。尽管近期研究探索了对比学习与监督学习框架以提升稳定性，本文提出一种概率化替代方案——生存价值学习（SVL），通过将各状态到达目标的时间建模为概率分布，将GCRL重构为生存学习问题。这种结构化分布蒙特卡洛视角导出一个闭式恒等式，将目标条件价值函数表达为生存概率的折现求和，从而支持通过风险模型（基于事件轨迹与右删失轨迹的最大似然训练）进行价值估计。我们提出三种实用价值估计器：有限时域截断法与两种分箱式无限时域近似法，以捕捉长时域目标。离线GCRL基准实验表明，SVL结合分层行动器可匹配或超越强基准方法（分层TD与蒙特卡洛），在复杂长时域任务中表现优异。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Survival Value Learning (SVL), a probabilistic method that reframes goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL) as a survival learning problem to address the instability and sample inefficiency of temporal-difference approaches. SVL models the time-to-goal distribution from each state and expresses the value function as a discounted sum of survival probabilities, enabling training via maximum likelihood on event and censored trajectories. Experimental results on offline GCRL benchmarks demonstrate that SVL, when combined with hierarchical actors, matches or outperforms strong hierarchical TD and Monte Carlo baselines, particularly excelling in complex, long-horizon tasks.
本文提出了生存价值学习（SVL），这是一种概率方法，通过将目标条件强化学习（GCRL）重新定义为生存学习问题，以解决时序差分方法的不稳定性和样本效率低下的问题。SVL对每个状态到目标的时间分布进行建模，并将价值函数表达为生存概率的折扣和，从而允许通过事件和右删失轨迹的最大似然估计进行训练。在离线GCRL基准测试中的实验结果表明，SVL与分层行动器结合后，能够匹配或超越强分层TD和蒙特卡洛基线方法，尤其在复杂、长视野任务中表现出色。
AutoSculpt: A Pattern-based Model Auto-pruning Framework Using Reinforcement Learning and Graph Learning
Authors: Lixian Jing, Jianpeng Qi, Junyu Dong, Yanwei Yu
First: 2024-12-24T02:05:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T16:09:21+00:00
Comments: I have identified a significant and fundamental flaw in the methodology described in Section 3 of the manuscript. This flaw pertains to a critical error in the implementation of the model's training procedure, which renders the reported performance metrics unreliable. This issue is not correctable through an erratum or replacement as it undermines the core findings and validity of the entire study
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
As deep neural networks (DNNs) are increasingly deployed on edge devices, optimizing models for constrained computational resources is critical. Existing auto-pruning methods face challenges due to the diversity of DNN models, various operators (e.g., filters), and the difficulty in balancing pruning granularity with model accuracy. To address these limitations, we introduce AutoSculpt, a pattern-based automated pruning framework designed to enhance efficiency and accuracy by leveraging graph learning and deep reinforcement learning (DRL). AutoSculpt automatically identifies and prunes regular patterns within DNN architectures that can be recognized by existing inference engines, enabling runtime acceleration. Three key steps in AutoSculpt include: (1) Constructing DNNs as graphs to encode their topology and parameter dependencies, (2) embedding computationally efficient pruning patterns, and (3) utilizing DRL to iteratively refine auto-pruning strategies until the optimal balance between compression and accuracy is achieved. Experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of AutoSculpt across various architectures, including ResNet, MobileNet, VGG, and Vision Transformer, achieving pruning rates of up to 90% and nearly 18% improvement in FLOPs reduction, outperforming all baselines. The codes can be available at https://github.com/jlx15588/AutoSculpt
中文标题/摘要
标题：AutoSculpt：基于模式与强化学习及图学习的模型自动剪枝框架
随着深度神经网络（DNN）在边缘设备上的部署日益增多，针对有限计算资源优化模型变得至关重要。现有自动剪枝方法因DNN模型多样性、各类算子（如滤波器）的差异以及剪枝粒度与模型精度难以平衡而面临挑战。为克服这些局限，我们提出了AutoSculpt——一种基于模式的自动剪枝框架，通过结合图学习与深度强化学习（DRL）来提升效率与精度。AutoSculpt能自动识别并剪除DNN架构中可被现有推理引擎识别的规则模式，从而实现运行时加速。其三个关键步骤包括：（1）将DNN构建为图以编码其拓扑与参数依赖关系；（2）嵌入计算高效的剪枝模式；（3）利用DRL迭代优化自动剪枝策略，直至在压缩率与精度间达到最优平衡。实验结果表明，AutoSculpt在ResNet、MobileNet、VGG及Vision Transformer等多种架构上均表现优异，最高可实现90%的剪枝率，FLOPs降低幅度提升近18%，性能超越所有基线方法。代码发布于https://github.com/jlx15588/AutoSculpt
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to optimize deep neural networks for deployment on resource-constrained edge devices, this paper introduces AutoSculpt, a pattern-based automated pruning framework that addresses challenges in model diversity, operator variety, and the accuracy-efficiency trade-off. The method leverages graph learning to represent DNNs as graphs with embedded pruning patterns and employs deep reinforcement learning to iteratively refine pruning strategies for optimal compression. Experimental results on architectures like ResNet and Vision Transformer show the framework achieves pruning rates up to 90% and nearly 18% improvement in FLOPs reduction, outperforming baselines, though a critical methodological flaw in the training procedure undermines the reliability of these reported metrics.
本文旨在优化深度神经网络以适应资源受限的边缘设备部署，针对现有自动剪枝方法在模型多样性、算子类型及精度与效率平衡方面的挑战，提出了AutoSculpt这一基于模式的自动剪枝框架。该方法利用图学习将DNN表示为包含剪枝模式的图结构，并采用深度强化学习迭代优化剪枝策略以实现最佳压缩。在ResNet和Vision Transformer等架构上的实验结果表明，该框架实现了高达90%的剪枝率和近18%的FLOPs减少，优于基线方法，但论文中训练过程存在关键方法缺陷，导致所报告性能指标的可靠性受到质疑。
RS-HyRe-R1: A Hybrid Reward Mechanism to Overcome Perceptual Inertia for Remote Sensing Images Understanding
Authors: Gaozhi Zhou, Hu He, Peng Shen, Jipeng Zhang, Liujue Zhang, Linrui Xu, Zeyuan Wang, Ziyu Li, Xuezhi Cui, Wang Guo, Haifeng Li
First: 2026-04-19T15:50:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T15:50:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) post-training substantially improves remote sensing vision-language models (RS-VLMs). However, when handling complex remote sensing imagery (RSI) requiring exhaustive visual scanning, models tend to rely on localized salient cues for rapid inference. We term this RL-induced bias "perceptual inertia". Driven by reward maximization, models favor quick outcome fitting, leading to two limitations: cognitively, overreliance on specific features impedes complete evidence construction; operationally, models struggle to flexibly shift visual focus across tasks. To address this bias and encourage comprehensive visual evidence mining, we propose RS-HyRe-R1, a hybrid reward framework for RSI understanding. It introduces: (1) a spatial reasoning activation reward that enforces structured visual reasoning; (2) a perception correctness reward that provides adaptive quality anchors across RS tasks, ensuring accurate geometric and semantic alignment; and (3) a visual-semantic path evolution reward that penalizes repetitive reasoning and promotes exploration of complementary cues to build richer evidence chains. Experiments show RS-HyRe-R1 effectively mitigates "perceptual inertia", encouraging deeper, more diverse reasoning. With only 3B parameters, it achieves state-of-the-art performance on REC, OVD, and VQA tasks, outperforming models up to 7B parameters. It also demonstrates strong zero-shot generalization, surpassing the second-best model by 3.16%, 3.97%, and 2.72% on VQA, OVD, and REC, respectively. Code and datasets are available at https://github.com/geox-lab/RS-HyRe-R1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RS-HyRe-R1：一种克服遥感图像理解中感知惯性的混合奖励机制
强化学习（RL）后训练显著提升了遥感视觉语言模型（RS-VLM）的性能。然而，在处理需要全面视觉扫描的复杂遥感图像（RSI）时，模型倾向于依赖局部显著线索进行快速推理。我们将这种由强化学习引发的偏差称为“感知惯性”。在奖励最大化的驱动下，模型偏好快速拟合结果，导致两个局限：认知上，对特定特征的过度依赖阻碍了完整证据链的构建；操作上，模型难以在不同任务间灵活转移视觉焦点。为纠正此偏差并鼓励全面的视觉证据挖掘，我们提出了用于RSI理解的混合奖励框架RS-HyRe-R1。该框架包含：（1）空间推理激活奖励，强制进行结构化视觉推理；（2）感知正确性奖励，为不同遥感任务提供自适应质量锚点，确保准确的几何与语义对齐；（3）视觉-语义路径演化奖励，惩罚重复推理并促进探索互补线索以构建更丰富的证据链。实验表明，RS-HyRe-R1有效缓解了“感知惯性”，鼓励更深入、更多样化的推理。仅用30亿参数即在REC、OVD和VQA任务上达到最先进性能，优于参数规模达70亿的模型。同时展现出强大的零样本泛化能力，在VQA、OVD和REC任务上分别超越次优模型3.16%、3.97%和2.72%。代码与数据集已开源：https://github.com/geox-lab/RS-HyRe-R1。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the issue of "perceptual inertia" in reinforcement learning (RL)-trained remote sensing vision-language models, where models overly rely on localized visual cues for quick inference, hindering comprehensive evidence construction and flexible task adaptation. To overcome this, the method proposes RS-HyRe-R1, a hybrid reward framework that combines spatial reasoning activation, perception correctness, and visual-semantic path evolution rewards to enforce structured reasoning, ensure accurate alignment, and promote exploration of diverse visual evidence. Experimental results demonstrate that RS-HyRe-R1 effectively mitigates perceptual inertia, achieving state-of-the-art performance on REC, OVD, and VQA tasks with only 3B parameters, outperforming larger models and showing strong zero-shot generalization gains of up to 3.97% over competitors.

Waking Up Blind: Cold-Start Optimization of Supervision-Free Agentic Trajectories for Grounded Visual Perception
Authors: Ashutosh Bajpai, Tamal Majumder, Akshay Nambi, Tanmoy Chakraborty
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-19T15:06:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T15:06:30+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Findings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Small Vision-Language Models (SVLMs) are efficient task controllers but often suffer from visual brittleness and poor tool orchestration. They typically require expensive supervised trajectory tuning to mitigate these deficits. In this work, we propose Self-supervised Perception Enabled by Cascaded Tool Rollout Alignment (SPECTRA), a supervision-free framework that bootstraps agentic capabilities via Coldstart Reinforcement Learning for SVLMs. SPECTRA enforces Soft Structured Multi-turn Rollouts, a topological constraint that directs agents to explicitly sequence tool derived evidence before synthesis, effectively grounding reasoning in visual observations. We employ a multi-objective reward signal that simultaneously maximizes task correctness, rollout structure, and tool utility, enabling agent to self-discover robust behaviors without human preference labels. We further introduce Tool Instrumental Utility (TIU), a novel metric to quantify tool efficacy in the absence of ground truth. Extensive evaluations across composite and out-of-distribution (MMMU-Pro) benchmarks demonstrate that SPECTRA boosts agentic trajectories, improving task accuracy by up to 5% and tool efficiency by 9%, enabling more efficient multimodal agents that learn effectively from environmental interaction alone.
中文标题/摘要
标题：盲启觉醒：基于无监督智能体轨迹冷启动优化的视觉感知基础
小型视觉语言模型（SVLMs）作为高效任务控制器，常面临视觉脆弱性与工具协调能力不足的问题，通常需依赖昂贵的监督轨迹调优来缓解。本研究提出SPECTRA框架——一种通过级联工具展开对齐实现自监督感知的无监督方法，采用冷启动强化学习为SVLMs自主引导智能体能力。该框架通过软结构化多轮次展开的拓扑约束，强制智能体在综合推理前显式序列化工具衍生的证据，从而将推理过程牢固锚定于视觉观察。我们设计的多目标奖励信号能同步最大化任务正确率、展开结构完整性与工具效用，使智能体无需人类偏好标签即可自主发现鲁棒行为模式。进一步提出工具效用量化指标（TIU），用于无真值标注场景下的工具效能评估。在复合任务及分布外基准（MMMU-Pro）上的广泛实验表明，SPECTRA能显著提升智能体轨迹质量，任务准确率最高提升5%，工具效率提高9%，实现了仅通过环境交互即可高效学习的多模态智能体。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the visual brittleness and poor tool orchestration of Small Vision-Language Models (SVLMs) without relying on expensive supervised trajectory tuning. ReflectRM: Boosting Generative Reward Models via Self-Reflection within a Unified Judgment Framework
Authors: Kai Qin, Liangxin Liu, Yu Liang, Longzheng Wang, Yan Wang, Yueyang Zhang, Long Xia, Zhiyuan Sun, Houde Liu, Daiting Shi
First: 2026-04-08T18:46:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T14:50:17+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reward Models (RMs) are critical components in the Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) pipeline, directly determining the alignment quality of Large Language Models (LLMs). Recently, Generative Reward Models (GRMs) have emerged as a superior paradigm, offering higher interpretability and stronger generalization than traditional scalar RMs. However, existing methods for GRMs focus primarily on outcome-level supervision, neglecting analytical process quality, which constrains their potential. To address this, we propose ReflectRM, a novel GRM that leverages self-reflection to assess analytical quality and enhance preference modeling. ReflectRM is trained under a unified generative framework for joint modeling of response preference and analysis preference. During inference, we use its self-reflection capability to identify the most reliable analysis, from which the final preference prediction is derived. Experiments across four benchmarks show that ReflectRM consistently improves performance, achieving an average accuracy gain of +3.7 on Qwen3-4B. Further experiments confirm that response preference and analysis preference are mutually reinforcing. Notably, ReflectRM substantially mitigates positional bias, yielding +10.2 improvement compared with leading GRMs and establishing itself as a more stable evaluator. Our code is available at https://github.com/yuliangCarmelo/ReflectRM.
中文标题/摘要

奖励模型（RMs）是基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）流程中的关键组件，直接决定大语言模型（LLMs）的对齐质量。近年来，生成式奖励模型（GRMs）作为一种更优范式出现，相比传统标量RMs具有更高的可解释性和更强的泛化能力。然而，现有GRM方法主要关注结果层面的监督，忽视了分析过程的质量，限制了其潜力。为此，我们提出ReflectRM，一种利用自反思来评估分析质量并增强偏好建模的新型GRM。ReflectRM在统一的生成框架下训练，用于联合建模回答偏好和分析偏好。在推理阶段，我们利用其自反思能力识别最可靠的分析，并据此得出最终的偏好预测。在四个基准测试上的实验表明，ReflectRM持续提升性能，在Qwen3-4B上平均准确率提升+3.7。进一步实验证实，回答偏好与分析偏好相互促进。值得注意的是，ReflectRM显著缓解了位置偏差，相比领先的GRMs提升+10.2，成为更稳定的评估器。代码已开源：https://github.com/yuliangCarmelo/ReflectRM。

The method introduces a novel GRM that employs self-reflection within a unified generative framework to jointly model both response preferences and analysis preferences, using this self-reflection during inference to select the most reliable analysis for final preference prediction. TrafficClaw: Generalizable Urban Traffic Control via Unified Physical Environment Modeling
Authors: Siqi Lai, Pan Zhang, Yuping Zhou, Jindong Han, Yansong Ning, Hao Liu
First: 2026-04-19T14:17:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T14:17:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Urban traffic control is a system-level coordination problem spanning heterogeneous subsystems, including traffic signals, freeways, public transit, and taxi services. Existing optimization-based, reinforcement learning (RL), and emerging LLM-based approaches are largely designed for isolated tasks, limiting both cross-task generalization and the ability to capture coupled physical dynamics across subsystems. We argue that effective system-level control requires a unified physical environment in which subsystems share infrastructure, mobility demand, and spatiotemporal constraints, allowing local interventions to propagate through the network. To this end, we propose TrafficClaw, a framework for general urban traffic control built upon a unified runtime environment. TrafficClaw integrates heterogeneous subsystems into a shared dynamical system, enabling explicit modeling of cross-subsystem interactions and closed-loop agent-environment feedback. Within this environment, we develop an LLM agent with executable spatiotemporal reasoning and reusable procedural memory, supporting unified diagnostics across subsystems and continual strategy refinement. Furthermore, we introduce a multi-stage training pipeline with supervised initialization and agentic RL with system-level optimization, further enabling coordinated and system-aware performance. Experiments demonstrate that TrafficClaw achieves robust, transferable, and system-aware performance across unseen traffic scenarios, dynamics, and task configurations. Our project is available at https://github.com/usail-hkust/TrafficClaw.
中文标题/摘要

PRL: Prompts from Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Paweł Batorski, Adrian Kosmala, Paul Swoboda
First: 2025-05-20T14:26:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T14:17:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Effective prompt engineering remains a central challenge in fully harnessing the capabilities of LLMs. While well-designed prompts can dramatically enhance performance, crafting them typically demands expert intuition and a nuanced understanding of the task. Moreover, the most impactful prompts often hinge on subtle semantic cues, ones that may elude human perception but are crucial for guiding LLM behavior. In this paper, we introduce PRL (Prompts from Reinforcement Learning), a novel RL-based approach for automatic prompt generation. Unlike previous methods, PRL can produce novel few-shot examples that were not seen during training. Our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance across a range of benchmarks, including text classification, simplification, and summarization. On the classification task, it surpasses prior methods by 2.58% over APE and 1.00% over EvoPrompt. Additionally, it improves the average ROUGE scores on the summarization task by 4.32 over APE and by 2.12 over EvoPrompt and the SARI score on simplification by 6.93 over APE and by 6.01 over EvoPrompt. Our code is available at https://github.com/Batorskq/prl .
中文标题/摘要
标题：PRL：基于强化学习的提示生成
有效的提示工程仍是充分发挥大语言模型能力的核心挑战。精心设计的提示能显著提升性能，但其构建通常依赖专家直觉和对任务的细致理解，且最有效的提示常依赖于细微的语义线索——这些线索可能超出人类感知，却对引导大语言模型行为至关重要。本文提出PRL（基于强化学习的提示生成），一种创新的基于强化学习的自动提示生成方法。与先前方法不同，PRL能生成训练中未见过的新颖少样本示例。该方法在文本分类、文本简化和摘要生成等多个基准测试中均达到最先进性能：在分类任务上，其表现超越APE方法2.58%，超越EvoPrompt方法1.00%；在摘要任务中，平均ROUGE分数较APE提升4.32，较EvoPrompt提升2.12；在文本简化任务中，SARI分数较APE提高6.93，较EvoPrompt提高6.01。代码已开源：https://github.com/Batorskq/prl。

The paper addresses the challenge of expert-dependent manual prompt engineering for large language models (LLMs) by introducing PRL, a reinforcement learning-based method for automatic prompt generation. This approach uniquely generates novel few-shot examples not seen during training, moving beyond prior techniques. Experimental results demonstrate state-of-the-art performance across text classification, simplification, and summarization benchmarks, with notable improvements such as a 2.58% increase over APE in classification and significant gains in ROUGE and SARI scores for summarization and simplification tasks.
本文针对大型语言模型提示工程依赖专家经验的问题，提出了PRL，一种基于强化学习的自动提示生成方法。该方法能够生成训练中未见过的全新少样本示例，超越了以往技术。实验结果表明，在文本分类、文本简化和摘要生成等多个基准测试中，该方法取得了最先进的性能，例如在分类任务上比APE提升了2.58%，并在摘要和简化任务的ROUGE和SARI分数上实现了显著提升。
Time Series Forecasting as Reasoning: A Slow-Thinking Approach with Reinforced LLMs
Authors: Yitong Zhou, Yucong Luo, Mingyue Cheng, Qi Liu, Jiahao Wang, Daoyu Wang, Enhong Chen
First: 2025-06-12T12:15:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T14:11:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
To advance time series forecasting (TSF), various methods have been proposed to improve prediction accuracy, evolving from statistical techniques to data-driven deep learning architectures. Despite their effectiveness, most existing methods still adhere to a fast thinking paradigm-relying on extracting historical patterns and mapping them to future values as their core modeling philosophy, lacking an explicit thinking process that incorporates intermediate time series reasoning. Meanwhile, emerging slow-thinking LLMs (e.g., OpenAI-o1) have shown remarkable multi-step reasoning capabilities, offering an alternative way to overcome these issues. However, prompt engineering alone presents several limitations - including high computational cost, privacy risks, and limited capacity for in-depth domain-specific time series reasoning. To address these limitations, a more promising approach is to train LLMs to develop slow thinking capabilities and acquire strong time series reasoning skills. For this purpose, we propose Time-R1, a two-stage reinforcement fine-tuning framework designed to enhance multi-step reasoning ability of LLMs for time series forecasting. Specifically, the first stage conducts supervised fine-tuning for warmup adaptation, while the second stage employs reinforcement learning to improve the model's generalization ability. Particularly, we design a fine-grained multi-objective reward specifically for time series forecasting, and then introduce GRIP (group-based relative importance for policy optimization), which leverages non-uniform sampling to further encourage and optimize the model's exploration of effective reasoning paths. Experiments demonstrate that Time-R1 significantly improves forecast performance across diverse datasets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：时间序列预测作为推理：基于强化大语言模型的慢思考方法
为推进时间序列预测（TSF）发展，从统计方法到数据驱动的深度学习架构，各类提升预测精度的方法不断涌现。尽管现有方法效果显著，但多数仍遵循快速思考范式——其核心建模理念依赖于提取历史模式并映射至未来值，缺乏融入中间时间序列推理的显式思考过程。与此同时，新兴的慢思考大语言模型（如OpenAI-o1）展现出卓越的多步推理能力，为突破这些局限提供了新路径。然而，仅依靠提示工程存在诸多限制——包括高昂计算成本、隐私风险以及领域特异性时间序列深度推理能力不足。为应对这些挑战，更具前景的方案是通过训练使大语言模型发展慢思考能力并掌握强大的时间序列推理技能。为此，我们提出Time-R1框架：一个旨在增强大语言模型时间序列预测多步推理能力的双阶段强化微调架构。具体而言，第一阶段通过监督微调实现预热适应，第二阶段运用强化学习提升模型泛化能力。我们特别设计了面向时间序列预测的细粒度多目标奖励机制，进而引入GRIP（基于群组的策略优化相对重要性）方法，该方法利用非均匀采样进一步激励并优化模型对有效推理路径的探索。实验表明，Time-R1在多样化数据集上显著提升了预测性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of fast-thinking paradigms in time series forecasting, which lack explicit reasoning processes, and the high costs of prompt engineering with slow-thinking LLMs, this paper introduces Time-R1, a two-stage reinforcement fine-tuning framework to enhance LLMs' multi-step reasoning for forecasting. The method first uses supervised fine-tuning for adaptation, then applies reinforcement learning with a fine-grained multi-objective reward and a GRIP optimization technique to encourage exploration of effective reasoning paths. Experimental results show that Time-R1 significantly improves forecasting performance across diverse datasets.
针对时间序列预测中快速思维范式缺乏显式推理过程以及慢思维大语言模型提示工程成本高的问题，本文提出了Time-R1，一个两阶段强化微调框架，旨在增强大语言模型在预测中的多步推理能力。该方法首先通过监督微调进行适应，然后采用强化学习，结合细粒度多目标奖励和GRIP优化技术，以鼓励探索有效的推理路径。实验结果表明，Time-R1在多个数据集上显著提升了预测性能。
RISC-V Functional Safety for Autonomous Automotive Systems: An Analytical Framework and Research Roadmap for ML-Assisted Certification
Authors: Nick Andreasyan, Mikhail Struve, Alexey Popov, Maksim Nikolaev, Vadim Vashkelis
First: 2026-04-19T11:39:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T11:39:16+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 3 figures, 4 tables. Analytical perspective paper on automotive-grade RISC-V functional safety, certification economics, and ML-assisted certification for autonomous driving systems
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
RISC-V is emerging as a viable platform for automotive-grade embedded computing, with recent ISO 26262 ASIL-D certifications demonstrating readiness for safety-critical deployment in autonomous driving systems. However, functional safety in automotive systems is fundamentally a certification problem rather than a processor problem. The dominant costs arise from diagnostic coverage analysis, toolchain qualification, fault injection campaigns, safety-case generation, and compliance with ISO 26262, ISO 21448 (SOTIF), and ISO/SAE 21434. This paper analyzes the role of RISC-V in automotive functional safety, focusing on ISA openness, formal verifiability, custom extension control, debug transparency, and vendor-independent qualification. We examine autonomous driving safety requirements and map them to RISC-V architectural challenges such as lockstep execution, safety islands, mixed-criticality isolation, and secure debug. Rather than proposing a single algorithmic breakthrough, we present an analytical framework and research roadmap centered on certification economics as the primary optimization objective. We also discuss how selected ML methods, including LLM-assisted FMEDA generation, knowledge-graph-based safety case automation, reinforcement learning for fault injection, and graph neural networks for diagnostic coverage, can support certification workflows. We argue that the strongest outcome is not a faster core, but an ASIL-D-ready certifiable RISC-V platform.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向自动驾驶系统的RISC-V功能安全：基于机器学习辅助认证的分析框架与研究路线图
RISC-V正逐渐成为汽车级嵌入式计算的可行平台，近期获得的ISO 26262 ASIL-D认证表明其已具备在自动驾驶系统中部署安全关键应用的条件。然而，汽车系统的功能安全本质上是认证问题而非处理器问题。主要成本源于诊断覆盖率分析、工具链鉴定、故障注入测试、安全案例生成，以及对ISO 26262、ISO 21448（SOTIF）和ISO/SAE 21434标准的合规性。 本文分析了RISC-V在汽车功能安全中的作用，重点关注指令集架构的开放性、形式化可验证性、自定义扩展控制、调试透明度和供应商无关的鉴定流程。我们研究了自动驾驶安全需求，并将其映射到RISC-V架构挑战，如锁步执行、安全岛、混合关键性隔离和安全调试。 本文未提出单一算法突破，而是以认证经济性为主要优化目标，提出了分析框架和研究路线图。同时探讨了特定机器学习方法如何支持认证流程，包括大语言模型辅助的FMEDA生成、基于知识图谱的安全案例自动化、强化学习驱动的故障注入，以及图神经网络辅助的诊断覆盖率分析。我们认为最重要的成果并非更快的处理器内核，而是具备ASIL-D认证能力的RISC-V平台。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the rising adoption of RISC-V in safety-critical automotive systems, this paper analyzes its role in functional safety, framing the core challenge as a certification economics problem rather than a processor performance one. The method involves presenting an analytical framework and research roadmap that prioritizes reducing certification costs, examining how RISC-V's architectural features like ISA openness and formal verifiability address requirements such as lockstep execution and mixed-criticality isolation. The main experimental results and discussion highlight how selected machine learning techniques, including LLM-assisted FMEDA generation and reinforcement learning for fault injection, can automate and optimize certification workflows, concluding that the primary goal is achieving an ASIL-D-ready certifiable platform.
本文的动机源于RISC-V在安全关键型汽车系统中日益广泛的应用，其核心挑战被界定为认证经济学问题而非处理器性能问题。研究方法上，论文提出了一个以降低认证成本为首要优化目标的分析框架和研究路线图，分析了RISC-V的指令集开放性、形式可验证性等架构特性如何应对锁步执行、混合关键性隔离等安全需求。主要实验成果与讨论强调了选定的机器学习技术（如大语言模型辅助的FMEDA生成和用于故障注入的强化学习）如何自动化并优化认证流程，最终结论指出，首要目标是实现一个符合ASIL-D等级、可认证的RISC-V平台。
Revisiting Entropy in Reinforcement Learning for Large Reasoning Models
Authors: Renren Jin, Pengzhi Gao, Yuqi Ren, Zhuowen Han, Tongxuan Zhang, Wuwei Huang, Wei Liu, Jian Luan, Deyi Xiong
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-11-08T12:50:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T11:25:47+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026 Findings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a prominent paradigm for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs). However, the entropy of LLMs usually collapses during RLVR training, leading to premature convergence to suboptimal local minima and hindering further performance improvement. Although various approaches have been proposed to mitigate entropy collapse, a comprehensive study of entropy in RLVR remains lacking. To bridge this gap, we conduct extensive experiments to investigate the entropy dynamics of LLMs trained with RLVR and analyze how model entropy correlates with response diversity, calibration, and performance across various benchmarks. Our results identify three key factors that influence entropy: the clipping thresholds in the optimization objective, the number of off-policy updates, and the diversity of the training data. Furthermore, through both theoretical analysis and empirical validation, we demonstrate that tokens with positive advantages are the primary drivers of entropy collapse. Motivated by this insight, we propose Positive-Advantage Reweighting, a simple yet effective approach that regulates model entropy by adjusting the loss weights assigned to tokens with positive advantages during RLVR training, while maintaining competitive performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重访大型推理模型强化学习中的熵问题
基于可验证奖励的强化学习已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的重要范式。然而，在RLVR训练过程中，大语言模型的熵通常会坍缩，导致模型过早收敛至次优局部极小值，阻碍性能的进一步提升。尽管已有多种方法被提出以缓解熵坍缩，但对RLVR中熵问题的系统性研究仍显不足。为填补这一空白，我们通过大量实验探究了RLVR训练下大语言模型的熵动态，并分析了模型熵与响应多样性、校准性及多基准测试性能之间的关联。研究结果揭示了影响熵的三个关键因素：优化目标中的裁剪阈值、离策略更新次数以及训练数据的多样性。进一步通过理论分析与实证验证，我们证明具有正优势值的词元是熵坍缩的主要驱动因素。基于此发现，我们提出了正优势重加权方法——一种简单有效的技术，通过在RLVR训练中调整对正优势词元的损失权重来调控模型熵，同时保持模型的竞争力。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the problem of entropy collapse in large language models during reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), a process used to enhance reasoning, where declining entropy leads to suboptimal convergence and limits performance gains. The authors conduct extensive experiments to analyze entropy dynamics, linking them to response diversity and calibration, and identify key influencing factors: optimization clipping thresholds, off-policy update frequency, and training data diversity. They theoretically and empirically show that tokens with positive advantages primarily drive entropy collapse, leading to the proposal of Positive-Advantage Reweighting, a method that adjusts loss weights for such tokens to regulate entropy while maintaining competitive benchmark performance.
本文研究了大型语言模型在基于可验证奖励的强化学习训练中出现的熵崩溃问题，该问题会导致模型过早收敛于次优解并阻碍性能提升。作者通过大量实验分析了熵的动态变化及其与响应多样性、校准度的关联，并确定了影响熵的三个关键因素：优化目标中的裁剪阈值、离策略更新次数以及训练数据的多样性。研究从理论和实证上证明，具有正优势值的标记是熵崩溃的主要驱动因素，据此提出了正优势重加权方法，该方法通过调整这些标记在训练中的损失权重来有效调控模型熵，同时在多个基准测试中保持竞争力。
From Kinematics to Dynamics: Learning to Refine Hybrid Plans for Physically Feasible Execution
Authors: Lidor Erez, Shahaf S. Shperberg, Ayal Taitler
First: 2026-04-14T09:00:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T09:29:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In many robotic tasks, agents must traverse a sequence of spatial regions to complete a mission. Such problems are inherently mixed discrete-continuous: a high-level action sequence and a physically feasible continuous trajectory. The resulting trajectory and action sequence must also satisfy problem constraints such as deadlines, time windows, and velocity or acceleration limits. While hybrid temporal planners attempt to address this challenge, they typically model motion using linear (first-order) dynamics, which cannot guarantee that the resulting plan respects the robot's true physical constraints. Consequently, even when the high-level action sequence is fixed, producing a dynamically feasible trajectory becomes a bi-level optimization problem. We address this problem via reinforcement learning in continuous space. We define a Markov Decision Process that explicitly incorporates analytical second-order constraints and use it to refine first-order plans generated by a hybrid planner. Our results show that this approach can reliably recover physical feasibility and effectively bridge the gap between a planner's initial first-order trajectory and the dynamics required for real execution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从运动学到动力学：学习优化混合规划以实现物理可行执行
在许多机器人任务中，智能体必须穿越一系列空间区域以完成任务。这类问题本质上是离散-连续混合的：包含高层动作序列与物理可行的连续轨迹。生成的轨迹与动作序列还需满足时间限制、时间窗口、速度或加速度限制等约束条件。虽然混合时序规划器试图解决这一挑战，但其通常采用线性（一阶）动力学建模运动，无法保证生成的规划符合机器人真实的物理约束。因此，即使高层动作序列已确定，生成动力学可行的轨迹仍会形成双层优化问题。我们通过连续空间中的强化学习解决该问题：定义显式包含解析二阶约束的马尔可夫决策过程，并利用其优化混合规划器生成的一阶规划。实验表明，该方法能可靠恢复物理可行性，有效弥合规划器初始一阶轨迹与实际执行所需动力学之间的差距。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge that hybrid temporal planners, which generate sequences of discrete actions and continuous trajectories, often rely on simplified first-order dynamics models that fail to guarantee physical feasibility under real robot constraints like acceleration limits. To address this, the authors propose a reinforcement learning method in continuous space, formulating a Markov Decision Process that incorporates analytical second-order constraints to refine the initial first-order plans. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach reliably recovers physical feasibility, effectively bridging the gap between the planner's output and the dynamics needed for real-world execution.
本文的动机在于混合时序规划器通常基于简化的一阶动力学模型生成离散动作序列和连续轨迹，但无法保证在真实机器人加速度等约束下的物理可行性。为此，作者提出一种连续空间中的强化学习方法，通过构建包含解析二阶约束的马尔可夫决策过程来优化初始一阶规划。实验结果表明，该方法能可靠地恢复物理可行性，有效弥合了规划器输出与实际执行所需动力学之间的差距。
Memory Intelligence Agent
Authors: Jingyang Qiao, Weicheng Meng, Yu Cheng, Zhihang Lin, Zhizhong Zhang, Xin Tan, Jingyu Gong, Kun Shao, Yuan Xie
First: 2026-04-06T07:59:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T09:08:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep research agents (DRAs) integrate LLM reasoning with external tools. Memory systems enable DRAs to leverage historical experiences, which are essential for efficient reasoning and autonomous evolution. Existing methods rely on retrieving similar trajectories from memory to aid reasoning, while suffering from key limitations of ineffective memory evolution and increasing storage and retrieval costs. To address these problems, we propose a novel Memory Intelligence Agent (MIA) framework, consisting of a Manager-Planner-Executor architecture. Memory Manager is a non-parametric memory system that can store compressed historical search trajectories. Planner is a parametric memory agent that can produce search plans for questions. Executor is another agent that can search and analyze information guided by the search plan. To build the MIA framework, we first adopt an alternating reinforcement learning paradigm to enhance cooperation between the Planner and the Executor. Furthermore, we enable the Planner to continuously evolve during test-time learning, with updates performed on-the-fly alongside inference without interrupting the reasoning process. Additionally, we establish a bidirectional conversion loop between parametric and non-parametric memories to achieve efficient memory evolution. Finally, we incorporate a reflection and an unsupervised judgment mechanisms to boost reasoning and self-evolution in the open world. Extensive experiments across eleven benchmarks demonstrate the superiority of MIA.
中文标题/摘要
标题：记忆智能体
深度研究智能体（DRAs）将大语言模型推理与外部工具相结合。记忆系统使DRAs能够利用历史经验，这对高效推理和自主进化至关重要。现有方法依赖从记忆中检索相似轨迹以辅助推理，但存在记忆进化低效、存储与检索成本递增等关键局限。为解决这些问题，我们提出了一种新颖的记忆智能体（MIA）框架，采用管理者-规划者-执行者架构。记忆管理者是一个非参数化记忆系统，可存储压缩的历史搜索轨迹；规划者是一个参数化记忆智能体，能为问题生成搜索计划；执行者是另一个智能体，可根据搜索计划进行信息搜索与分析。为构建MIA框架，我们首先采用交替强化学习范式增强规划者与执行者的协作。进一步地，我们使规划者能在测试时学习中持续进化，在推理过程中实时更新而不中断推理流程。此外，我们在参数化与非参数化记忆间建立双向转换循环，以实现高效记忆进化。最后，我们引入反思机制和无监督判断机制，以增强开放世界中的推理与自我进化能力。在十一个基准测试上的大量实验证明了MIA的优越性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses limitations in existing deep research agents, such as ineffective memory evolution and high storage costs, by proposing the Memory Intelligence Agent (MIA) framework. This framework employs a Manager-Planner-Executor architecture where a non-parametric Memory Manager stores compressed historical trajectories, a parametric Planner generates search plans, and an Executor conducts guided information searches. Key innovations include alternating reinforcement learning to enhance Planner-Executor cooperation, on-the-fly test-time learning for continuous Planner evolution, and a bidirectional conversion loop between parametric and non-parametric memories to enable efficient memory updates. Experimental results across eleven benchmarks show that MIA outperforms existing methods, demonstrating superior reasoning and self-evolution capabilities in open-world scenarios.
本文针对现有深度研究代理中记忆进化效率低和存储成本高等问题，提出了记忆智能代理（MIA）框架。该框架采用管理器-规划器-执行器架构，其中非参数化记忆管理器存储压缩的历史轨迹，参数化规划器生成搜索计划，执行器则根据计划进行信息搜索与分析。方法创新包括通过交替强化学习增强规划器与执行器的协作，支持在测试时进行在线学习以实现规划器的持续进化，并建立参数化与非参数化记忆之间的双向转换循环以促进高效记忆更新。在十一个基准测试上的广泛实验表明，MIA在开放世界中的推理和自我进化能力优于现有方法。
AutoSearch: Adaptive Search Depth for Efficient Agentic RAG via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jingbo Sun, Wenyue Chong, Songjun Tu, Qichao Zhang, Yaocheng Zhang, Jiajun Chai, Xiaohan Wang, Wei Lin, Guojun Yin, Dongbin Zhao
First: 2026-04-19T09:05:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T09:05:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems enable large language models (LLMs) to solve complex tasks through multi-step interaction with external retrieval tools. However, such multi-step interaction often involves redundant search steps, incurring substantial computational cost and latency. Prior work limits search depth (i.e., the number of search steps) to reduce cost, but this often leads to underexploration of complex questions. To address this, we first investigate how search depth affects accuracy and find a minimal sufficient search depth that defines an accuracy-efficiency trade-off, jointly determined by question complexity and the agent's capability. Furthermore, we propose AutoSearch, a reinforcement learning (RL) framework that evaluates each search step via self-generated intermediate answers. By a self-answering mechanism, AutoSearch identifies the minimal sufficient search depth and promotes efficient search by rewarding its attainment while penalizing over-searching. In addition, reward mechanisms are introduced to stabilize search behavior and improve answer quality on complex questions. Extensive experiments on multiple benchmarks show that AutoSearch achieves a superior accuracy-efficiency trade-off, alleviating over-searching while preserving search quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AutoSearch：基于强化学习的自适应搜索深度实现高效代理式RAG
代理式检索增强生成（RAG）系统使大语言模型（LLM）能够通过与外部检索工具的多步交互解决复杂任务。然而，这种多步交互常包含冗余搜索步骤，导致显著的计算成本与延迟。先前研究通过限制搜索深度（即搜索步数）来降低成本，但这往往导致对复杂问题的探索不足。为此，我们首先探究搜索深度如何影响准确性，并发现一个由问题复杂度与代理能力共同决定的最小充分搜索深度，它定义了准确性与效率的权衡关系。进一步，我们提出AutoSearch——一种基于强化学习（RL）的框架，通过自生成的中间答案评估每个搜索步骤。借助自应答机制，AutoSearch能够识别最小充分搜索深度，并通过奖励达成该深度、惩罚过度搜索来促进高效检索。此外，框架引入奖励机制以稳定搜索行为并提升复杂问题的答案质量。在多个基准测试上的大量实验表明，AutoSearch实现了更优的准确性与效率权衡，在保持搜索质量的同时有效缓解了过度搜索问题。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the inefficiency of multi-step search in agentic retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems, where redundant steps increase computational cost and latency. The authors propose AutoSearch, a reinforcement learning framework that adaptively determines the minimal sufficient search depth by evaluating each step via self-generated intermediate answers, rewarding efficient search attainment and penalizing over-searching. Experimental results across multiple benchmarks demonstrate that AutoSearch achieves a superior trade-off between accuracy and efficiency, reducing unnecessary searches while maintaining answer quality on complex questions.
本文针对智能检索增强生成（RAG）系统中多步搜索效率低下的问题，指出冗余步骤会增加计算成本和延迟。作者提出AutoSearch，一种通过强化学习自适应确定最小充分搜索深度的框架，利用自生成的中间答案评估每一步，奖励高效搜索并惩罚过度搜索。在多个基准测试上的实验结果表明，AutoSearch在准确性和效率之间取得了更优的平衡，减少了不必要的搜索，同时在复杂问题上保持了答案质量。
From Answers to Arguments: Toward Trustworthy Clinical Diagnostic Reasoning with Toulmin-Guided Curriculum Goal-Conditioned Learning
Authors: Chen Zhan, Xiaoyu Tan, Gengchen Ma, Yu-Jie Xiong, Xiaoyan Jiang, Xihe Qiu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-13T07:49:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T09:00:50+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The integration of Large Language Models (LLMs) into clinical decision support is critically obstructed by their opaque and often unreliable reasoning. In the high-stakes domain of healthcare, correct answers alone are insufficient; clinical practice demands full transparency to ensure patient safety and enable professional accountability. A pervasive and dangerous weakness of current LLMs is their tendency to produce "correct answers through flawed reasoning." This issue is far more than a minor academic flaw; such process errors signal a fundamental lack of robust understanding, making the model prone to broader hallucinations and unpredictable failures when faced with real-world clinical complexity. In this paper, we establish a framework for trustworthy clinical argumentation by adapting the Toulmin model to the diagnostic process. We propose a novel training pipeline: Curriculum Goal-Conditioned Learning (CGCL), designed to progressively train LLM to generate diagnostic arguments that explicitly follow this Toulmin structure. CGCL's progressive three-stage curriculum systematically builds a solid clinical argument: (1) extracting facts and generating differential diagnoses; (2) justifying a core hypothesis while rebutting alternatives; and (3) synthesizing the analysis into a final, qualified conclusion. We validate CGCL using T-Eval, a quantitative framework measuring the integrity of the diagnosis reasoning. Experiments show that our method achieves diagnostic accuracy and reasoning quality comparable to resource-intensive Reinforcement Learning (RL) methods, while offering a more stable and efficient training pipeline.

Rethinking the Comparison Unit in Sequence-Level Reinforcement Learning: An Equal-Length Paired Training Framework from Loss Correction to Sample Construction
Authors: Fei Ding, Yongkang Zhang, Runhao Liu, Yuhao Liao, Zijian Zeng, Huiming Yang, Sibo wang, Linglin Liao
First: 2026-04-19T08:48:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T08:48:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper investigates the length problem in sequence-level relative reinforcement learning. We observe that, although existing methods partially alleviate length-related phenomena, a more fundamental issue remains insufficiently characterized: the comparison units used during training lack inherent comparability. Building on this observation, we propose a new perspective: the length problem should not be viewed merely as a loss-scaling or normalization bias, but rather as a \emph{comparison unit construction} problem. We further establish a sample-construction-based training framework that, instead of applying post-hoc corrections to unequal-length responses, proactively constructs equal-length, alignable, and comparable training segments during generation. Within this framework, we propose EqLen, a concrete method applicable to group-relative comparison algorithms such as GRPO, GSPO, and RLOO. Through dual-track synchronous generation, prefix inheritance, and segment masking, EqLen efficiently collects effective equal-length training segments and enables stable
中文标题/摘要
标题：序列级强化学习中比较单元的再思考：从损失校正到样本构建的等长配对训练框架
本文研究了序列级相对强化学习中的长度问题。我们发现，尽管现有方法部分缓解了长度相关现象，但一个更根本的问题仍未得到充分刻画：训练过程中使用的比较单元缺乏内在可比性。基于此观察，我们提出一个新视角：长度问题不应仅视为损失缩放或归一化偏差，而应视为一个\emph{比较单元构建}问题。我们进一步建立了一个基于样本构建的训练框架，该框架不再对不等长响应进行事后校正，而是在生成过程中主动构建等长、可对齐且可比较的训练片段。在此框架内，我们提出了EqLen方法，这是一种适用于GRPO、GSPO、RLOO等组间相对比较算法的具体方案。通过双轨同步生成、前缀继承和片段掩码技术，EqLen能高效收集有效的等长训练片段，并实现稳定的训练过程。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the length bias problem in sequence-level reinforcement learning by identifying a fundamental issue: the lack of comparability between training samples of unequal lengths. The authors propose reframing the problem as one of comparison unit construction and introduce a training framework that proactively builds equal-length, alignable training segments during generation, rather than applying post-hoc corrections. Their method, EqLen, employs dual-track synchronous generation, prefix inheritance, and segment masking to efficiently collect comparable segments, enabling stable training for group-relative algorithms like GRPO, GSPO, and RLOO.

From $\log π$ to $π$: Taming Divergence in Soft Clipping via Bilateral Decoupled Decay of Probability Gradient Weight
Authors: Xiaoliang Fu, Jiaye Lin, Yangyi Fang, Chaowen Hu, Cong Qin, Zekai Shao, Binbin Zheng, Lu Pan, Ke Zeng
First: 2026-03-15T14:00:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T08:46:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has catalyzed a leap in Large Language Model (LLM) reasoning, yet its optimization dynamics remain fragile. Standard algorithms like GRPO enforce stability via "hard clipping", which inadvertently stifles exploration by discarding gradients of tokens outside the trust region. While recent "soft clipping" methods attempt to recover these gradients, they suffer from a critical challenge: relying on log-probability gradient ($\nabla_θ\log π_θ$) yields divergent weights as probabilities vanish, destabilizing LLM training. We rethink this convention by establishing probability gradient ($\nabla_θπ_θ$) as the superior optimization primitive. Accordingly, we propose Decoupled Gradient Policy Optimization (DGPO), which employs a decoupled decay mechanism based on importance sampling ratios. By applying asymmetric, continuous decay to boundary tokens, DGPO resolves the conflict between stability and sustained exploration. Extensive experiments across DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen series models (1.5B/7B/14B) demonstrate that DGPO consistently outperforms strong baselines on various mathematical benchmarks, offering a robust and scalable solution for RLVR. Our code and implementation are available at: https://github.com/FlyTune/DGPO-RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从$\log π$到$π$：通过概率梯度权重的双边解耦衰减驯服软截断中的发散
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）推动了大型语言模型（LLM）推理能力的飞跃，但其优化动态仍显脆弱。GRPO等标准算法通过“硬截断”强制稳定性，却因丢弃信任区域外词元的梯度而无意中抑制了探索。尽管近期“软截断”方法尝试恢复这些梯度，却面临关键挑战：依赖对数概率梯度（$\nabla_θ\log π_θ$）会在概率趋零时产生发散权重，破坏LLM训练的稳定性。我们通过确立概率梯度（$\nabla_θπ_θ$）作为更优的优化原语来重新审视这一惯例，据此提出解耦梯度策略优化（DGPO）。该方法基于重要性采样比率采用解耦衰减机制，通过对边界词元施加非对称连续衰减，解决了稳定性与持续探索间的矛盾。在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen系列模型（1.5B/7B/14B）上的大量实验表明，DGPO在多种数学基准测试中持续超越强基线，为RLVR提供了稳健且可扩展的解决方案。代码与实现已开源：https://github.com/FlyTune/DGPO-RL。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the instability in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for Large Language Models, where standard hard clipping methods limit exploration and recent soft clipping approaches suffer from divergent gradient weights as token probabilities approach zero. The authors propose Decoupled Gradient Policy Optimization (DGPO), which re-frames the optimization around the probability gradient rather than the log-probability gradient and introduces a decoupled decay mechanism using importance sampling ratios to apply asymmetric, continuous decay to boundary tokens. Experimental results on DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen models (1.5B, 7B, 14B) show that DGPO consistently outperforms strong baselines across various mathematical reasoning benchmarks, providing a more stable and scalable RLVR solution that better balances training stability with sustained exploration.
本文针对大语言模型可验证奖励强化学习中的不稳定性问题展开研究，指出标准的硬截断方法会限制探索，而近期的软截断方法则因令牌概率趋近于零时梯度权重发散而失效。作者提出了解耦梯度策略优化方法，该方法将优化核心从对数概率梯度转向概率梯度，并引入基于重要性采样比率的解耦衰减机制，对边界令牌施加非对称的连续衰减。在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen系列模型上的大量实验表明，该方法在多个数学推理基准测试中 consistently 优于现有基线，为可验证奖励强化学习提供了一个更稳定、可扩展的解决方案，更好地平衡了训练稳定性与持续探索。
A Survey of Reinforcement Learning for Large Language Models under Data Scarcity: Challenges and Solutions
Authors: Zhiyin Yu, Yuchen Mou, Juncheng Yan, Junyu Luo, Chunchun Chen, Xing Wei, Yunhui Liu, Hongru Sun, Yuxing Zhang, Jun Xu, Yatao Bian, Ming Zhang, Wei Ye, Tieke He, Jie Yang, Guanjie Zheng, Zhonghai Wu, Bo Zhang, Lei Bai, Xiao Luo
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-19T08:01:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T08:01:31+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 (Main Conference)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a powerful post-training paradigm for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs). However, reinforcement learning for LLMs faces substantial data scarcity challenges, including the limited availability of high-quality external supervision and the constrained volume of model-generated experience. These limitations make data-efficient reinforcement learning a critical research direction. In this survey, we present the first systematic review of reinforcement learning for LLMs under data scarcity. We propose a bottom-up hierarchical framework built around three complementary perspectives: the data-centric perspective, the training-centric perspective, and the framework-centric perspective. We develop a taxonomy of existing methods, summarize representative approaches in each category, and analyze their strengths and limitations. Our taxonomy aims to provide a clear conceptual foundation for understanding the design space of data-efficient RL for LLMs and to guide researchers working in this emerging area. We hope this survey offers a comprehensive roadmap for future research and inspires new directions toward more efficient and scalable reinforcement learning post-training for LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：数据稀缺环境下大语言模型强化学习研究综述：挑战与解决方案
强化学习已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的强大后训练范式。然而，大语言模型的强化学习面临显著的数据稀缺挑战，包括高质量外部监督的有限性以及模型生成经验的规模限制。这些局限使得数据高效的强化学习成为关键研究方向。本综述首次系统梳理了数据稀缺环境下大语言模型的强化学习方法，提出了围绕三个互补视角构建的自底向上分层框架：以数据为中心的视角、以训练为中心的视角和以框架为中心的视角。我们建立了现有方法的分类体系，总结了各类代表性方法，并分析了其优势与局限。该分类体系旨在为理解大语言模型数据高效强化学习的设计空间提供清晰的概念基础，并为这一新兴领域的研究者提供指引。我们希望本综述能为未来研究提供全面的路线图，并激发实现更高效、可扩展的大语言模型强化学习后训练的新方向。

ARCS: Autoregressive Circuit Synthesis with Topology-Aware Graph Attention and Spec Conditioning
Authors: Tushar Dhananjay Pathak
First: 2026-03-30T23:14:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T06:47:38+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 6 figures, 11 tables. Code available at https://github.com/tusharpathaknyu/ARCS
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
This paper presents ARCS (Autoregressive Circuit Synthesis), a system for amortized analog circuit generation. ARCS produces complete, SPICE-simulatable designs (topology and component values) in milliseconds rather than the minutes required by search-based methods. A hybrid pipeline combines two learned generators, a graph VAE and a flow-matching model, with SPICE-based ranking. It achieves 99.9% simulation validity (reward 6.43/8.0) across 32 topologies using only 8 SPICE evaluations, 40x fewer than genetic algorithms. For single-model inference, a topology-aware Graph Transformer with Best-of-3 candidate selection reaches 85% simulation validity in 97ms, over 600x faster than random search. The key technical contribution adapts Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to multi-topology circuit reinforcement learning. GRPO resolves a critical failure mode of REINFORCE, cross-topology reward distribution mismatch, through per-topology advantage normalization. This improves simulation validity by +9.6 percentage points over REINFORCE in only 500 RL steps (10x fewer). Grammar-constrained decoding additionally guarantees 100% structural validity by construction via topology-aware token masking.
