标题：ARCS：基于拓扑感知图注意力与规格条件化的自回归电路综合方法
本文提出ARCS（自回归电路综合），一种用于摊销式模拟电路生成的系统。ARCS能在毫秒级生成完整、可进行SPICE仿真的设计（拓扑结构与元件参数），而基于搜索的方法通常需要数分钟。该系统采用混合流程，结合了图变分自编码器与流匹配模型两种学习生成器，并基于SPICE仿真进行排序。在仅使用8次SPICE评估（比遗传算法减少40倍）的情况下，对32种拓扑结构实现了99.9%的仿真有效性（奖励分数6.43/8.0）。在单模型推理中，采用拓扑感知图变换器配合三选一候选方案，可在97毫秒内达到85%的仿真有效性，比随机搜索快600倍以上。核心技术创新在于将组相对策略优化（GRPO）适配于多拓扑电路强化学习。GRPO通过按拓扑结构进行优势归一化，解决了REINFORCE算法中跨拓扑奖励分布失配的关键失效问题，仅用500步强化学习（减少10倍）就将仿真有效性较REINFORCE提升9.6个百分点。此外，通过拓扑感知的令牌掩码进行语法约束解码，从结构上保证了100%的拓扑有效性。

SafeVLA: Towards Safety Alignment of Vision-Language-Action Model via Constrained Learning
Authors: Borong Zhang, Yuhao Zhang, Jiaming Ji, Yingshan Lei, Yishuai Cai, Josef Dai, Yuanpei Chen, Yaodong Yang
Venue: NeurIPS 2025 Spotlight
First: 2025-03-05T13:16:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T06:23:17+00:00
Comments: Accepted by NeurIPS 2025 Spotlight Presentation
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Vision-language-action models (VLAs) show potential as generalist robot policies. However, these models pose extreme safety challenges during real-world deployment, including the risk of harm to the environment, the robot itself, and humans. How can safety constraints be explicitly integrated into VLAs? We address this by exploring an integrated safety approach (ISA), systematically modeling safety requirements, then actively eliciting diverse unsafe behaviors, effectively constraining VLA policies via safe reinforcement learning, and rigorously assuring their safety through targeted evaluations. Leveraging the constrained Markov decision process (CMDP) paradigm, ISA optimizes VLAs from a min-max perspective against elicited safety risks. Thus, policies aligned through this comprehensive approach achieve the following key features: (I) effective safety-performance trade-offs, reducing the cumulative cost of safety violations by 83.58% compared to the state-of-the-art method, while also maintaining task success rate (+3.85%). (II) strong safety assurance, with the ability to mitigate long-tail risks and handle extreme failure scenarios. (III) robust generalization of learned safety behaviors to various out-of-distribution perturbations. The effectiveness is evaluated on long-horizon mobile manipulation tasks. Our data, models and newly proposed benchmark environment are available at https://pku-safevla.github.io.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SafeVLA：通过约束学习实现视觉-语言-动作模型的安全对齐
视觉-语言-动作模型（VLA）展现出作为通用机器人策略的潜力，但其在现实部署中面临严峻的安全挑战，包括对环境、机器人自身及人类造成伤害的风险。如何将安全约束显式整合到VLA中？本研究提出集成安全方法（ISA），通过系统建模安全需求、主动激发多样化不安全行为、利用安全强化学习有效约束VLA策略，并针对性评估严格保障其安全性。基于约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP）框架，ISA从最小化最大安全风险的角度优化VLA。经此综合方法对齐的策略具备以下关键特性：（I）实现安全与性能的有效权衡，相比前沿方法将安全违规累计成本降低83.58%，同时保持任务成功率（+3.85%）；（II）具备强安全保证能力，可缓解长尾风险并处理极端故障场景；（III）学习到的安全行为能稳健泛化至多种分布外扰动。该方法在长时程移动操作任务中验证有效性。数据、模型及新提出的基准环境发布于https://pku-safevla.github.io。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for SafeVLA is to address the critical safety risks posed by vision-language-action models (VLAs) when deployed as robot policies, which could harm the environment, robots, or humans. The method introduces an integrated safety approach (ISA) that systematically models safety requirements, actively elicits unsafe behaviors, and constrains VLA policies via safe reinforcement learning within a constrained Markov decision process (CMDP) framework, optimizing from a min-max perspective against safety risks. The main experimental results demonstrate an 83.58% reduction in cumulative safety violation costs compared to state-of-the-art methods while increasing task success rate by 3.85%, along with strong safety assurance against long-tail risks and robust generalization to out-of-distribution perturbations in long-horizon mobile manipulation tasks.
SafeVLA的研究动机源于视觉-语言-动作模型（VLA）作为机器人策略部署时可能对环境、机器人或人类造成伤害的严重安全风险。该方法提出了一种集成安全方法（ISA），通过系统建模安全需求、主动激发不安全行为，并利用安全强化学习在约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP）框架内约束VLA策略，以最小化安全风险的视角进行优化。主要实验结果表明，与现有最优方法相比，该方法将累计安全违规成本降低了83.58%，同时任务成功率提高了3.85%，并在长时程移动操作任务中展现出对长尾风险的强安全保证以及对外部分布扰动的鲁棒泛化能力。
OpenVLThinkerV2: A Generalist Multimodal Reasoning Model for Multi-domain Visual Tasks
Authors: Wenbo Hu, Xin Chen, Yan Gao-Tian, Yihe Deng, Nanyun Peng, Kai-Wei Chang
First: 2026-04-09T17:59:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T05:24:16+00:00
Comments: code at: https://github.com/uclanlp/openvlthinker
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) has emerged as the de facto Reinforcement Learning (RL) objective driving recent advancements in Multimodal Large Language Models. However, extending this success to open-source multimodal generalist models remains heavily constrained by two primary challenges: the extreme variance in reward topologies across diverse visual tasks, and the inherent difficulty of balancing fine-grained perception with multi-step reasoning capabilities. To address these issues, we introduce Gaussian GRPO (G$^2$RPO), a novel RL training objective that replaces standard linear scaling with non-linear distributional matching. By mathematically forcing the advantage distribution of any given task to strictly converge to a standard normal distribution, $\mathcal{N}(0,1)$, G$^2$RPO theoretically ensures inter-task gradient equity, mitigates vulnerabilities to heavy-tail outliers, and offers symmetric update for positive and negative rewards. Leveraging the enhanced training stability provided by G$^2$RPO, we introduce two task-level shaping mechanisms to seamlessly balance perception and reasoning. First, response length shaping dynamically elicits extended reasoning chains for complex queries while enforce direct outputs to bolster visual grounding. Second, entropy shaping tightly bounds the model's exploration zone, effectively preventing both entropy collapse and entropy explosion. Integrating these methodologies, we present OpenVLThinkerV2, a highly robust, general-purpose multimodal model. Extensive evaluations across 18 diverse benchmarks demonstrate its superior performance over strong open-source and leading proprietary frontier models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OpenVLThinkerV2：面向多领域视觉任务的通用多模态推理模型
群体相对策略优化（GRPO）已成为推动多模态大语言模型近期发展的实际强化学习目标。然而，将这一成功扩展到开源多模态通用模型仍面临两大主要挑战：不同视觉任务间奖励拓扑的极端差异，以及平衡细粒度感知与多步推理能力的内在困难。为解决这些问题，我们提出了高斯GRPO（G²RPO），这是一种用非线性分布匹配替代标准线性缩放的新型强化学习训练目标。通过数学上强制任何给定任务的优势分布严格收敛至标准正态分布𝒩(0,1)，G²RPO从理论上确保了任务间梯度均衡性，减轻了对重尾异常值的脆弱性，并为正负奖励提供对称更新。借助G²RPO增强的训练稳定性，我们引入了两种任务级塑形机制以无缝平衡感知与推理：首先，响应长度塑形动态激发复杂查询的扩展推理链，同时强制直接输出以增强视觉基础；其次，熵塑形紧密约束模型的探索区域，有效防止熵崩溃与熵爆炸。综合这些方法，我们提出了OpenVLThinkerV2——一个高度鲁棒的通用多模态模型。在18个多样化基准测试中的广泛评估表明，其性能优于强大的开源模型及领先的专有前沿模型。

The motivation for this work is to overcome two key challenges in training open-source multimodal generalist models: the high variance in reward structures across different visual tasks and the difficulty of balancing detailed perception with multi-step reasoning. The method introduces Gaussian GRPO (G²RPO), a novel reinforcement learning objective that uses non-linear distributional matching to enforce a standard normal advantage distribution, ensuring gradient equity and stability, alongside two task-level shaping mechanisms for balancing perception and reasoning. The main experimental results show that the resulting model, OpenVLThinkerV2, demonstrates superior performance across 18 diverse benchmarks, outperforming both strong open-source and leading proprietary models.

From Passive Metric to Active Signal: The Evolving Role of Uncertainty Quantification in Large Language Models
Authors: Jiaxin Zhang, Wendi Cui, Zhuohang Li, Lifu Huang, Bradley Malin, Caiming Xiong, Chien-Sheng Wu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-22T06:21:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T04:51:57+00:00
Comments: This paper has been accepted by ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While Large Language Models (LLMs) show remarkable capabilities, their unreliability remains a critical barrier to deployment in high-stakes domains. This survey charts a functional evolution in addressing this challenge: the evolution of uncertainty from a passive diagnostic metric to an active control signal guiding real-time model behavior. We demonstrate how uncertainty is leveraged as an active control signal across three frontiers: in \textbf{advanced reasoning} to optimize computation and trigger self-correction; in \textbf{autonomous agents} to govern metacognitive decisions about tool use and information seeking; and in \textbf{reinforcement learning} to mitigate reward hacking and enable self-improvement via intrinsic rewards. By grounding these advancements in emerging theoretical frameworks like Bayesian methods and Conformal Prediction, we provide a unified perspective on this transformative trend. This survey provides a comprehensive overview, critical analysis, and practical design patterns, arguing that mastering the new trend of uncertainty is essential for building the next generation of scalable, reliable, and trustworthy AI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从被动度量到主动信号：不确定性量化在大型语言模型中的角色演变
尽管大型语言模型展现出卓越能力，但其不可靠性仍是高风险领域部署的关键障碍。本综述描绘了应对这一挑战的功能演进路径：不确定性从被动的诊断度量演变为指导实时模型行为的主动控制信号。我们展示了不确定性如何作为主动控制信号在三大前沿领域发挥作用：在**高级推理**中优化计算并触发自我修正；在**自主智能体**中管理关于工具使用和信息寻求的元认知决策；在**强化学习**中缓解奖励攻击并通过内在奖励实现自我改进。通过将这些进展锚定于贝叶斯方法和共形预测等新兴理论框架，我们为这一变革性趋势提供了统一视角。本综述提供了全面概述、批判性分析和实用设计模式，论证掌握不确定性的新趋势对于构建下一代可扩展、可靠且可信的人工智能至关重要。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the critical need to enhance the reliability of Large Language Models (LLMs) for high-stakes applications, this survey paper examines the functional evolution of uncertainty quantification from a passive diagnostic metric into an active control signal that guides real-time model behavior. The method involves synthesizing and analyzing how uncertainty is leveraged across three key frontiers: advanced reasoning to optimize computation and trigger self-correction, autonomous agents to govern metacognitive decisions about tool use and information seeking, and reinforcement learning to mitigate reward hacking and enable self-improvement via intrinsic rewards, all grounded in emerging theoretical frameworks like Bayesian methods and Conformal Prediction. The main experimental results and analysis presented demonstrate that this active use of uncertainty provides a unified, transformative approach for building more scalable, reliable, and trustworthy AI systems.

GanitLLM: Difficulty-Aware Bengali Mathematical Reasoning through Curriculum-GRPO
Authors: Shubhashis Roy Dipta, Khairul Mahbub, Nadia Najjar
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-11T03:49:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T03:51:00+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ACL 2026 (Findings)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
We present a Bengali mathematical reasoning model called GanitLLM (named after the Bangla word for mathematics, Ganit), together with a new difficulty-aware Bengali math corpus and a curriculum-based GRPO pipeline. Bengali is one of the world's most widely spoken languages, yet existing LLMs either reason in English and then translate, or simply fail on multi-step Bengali math, in part because reinforcement learning recipes are tuned for high-resource languages and collapse under reward sparsity in low-resource settings. To address this, we construct Ganit, a rigorously filtered and decontaminated Bengali math dataset with automatic difficulty tags derived from the pass@k of a strong evaluator model. Building on this dataset, we propose Curriculum-GRPO, which combines multi-stage training (SFT + GRPO) with difficulty-aware sampling and verifiable rewards for format, numerical correctness, and Bengali reasoning. On Bn-MGSM and Bn-MSVAMP, GanitLLM-4B improves over its Qwen3-4B base by +8 and +6 accuracy points, respectively, while increasing the percentage of Bengali reasoning tokens from 14% to over 88% and reducing average solution length from 943 to 193 words. Project page is available at https://dipta007.github.io/GanitLLM

Temporal Representations for Exploration: Learning Complex Exploratory Behavior without Extrinsic Rewards
Authors: Faisal Mohamed, Catherine Ji, Benjamin Eysenbach, Glen Berseth
First: 2026-03-02T15:55:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T02:45:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Effective exploration in reinforcement learning requires not only tracking where an agent has been, but also understanding how the agent perceives and represents the world. To learn powerful representations, an agent should actively explore states that contribute to its knowledge of the environment. Temporal representations can capture the information necessary to solve a wide range of potential tasks while avoiding the computational cost associated with full state reconstruction. In this paper, we propose an exploration method that leverages temporal contrastive representations to guide exploration, prioritizing states with unpredictable future outcomes. We demonstrate that such representations can enable the learning of complex exploratory x in locomotion, manipulation, and embodied-AI tasks, revealing capabilities and behaviors that traditionally require extrinsic rewards. Unlike approaches that rely on explicit distance learning or episodic memory mechanisms (e.g., quasimetric-based methods), our method builds directly on temporal similarities, yielding a simpler yet effective strategy for exploration.

Guardrails in Logit Space: Safety Token Regularization for LLM Alignment
Authors: Thong Bach, Truyen Tran
First: 2026-04-19T02:41:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T02:41:04+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Fine-tuning well-aligned large language models (LLMs) on new domains often degrades their safety alignment, even when using benign datasets. Existing safety alignment techniques primarily focus on pretraining, leaving fine-tuned models vulnerable to behavioral shifts. In this work, we introduce safety token regularization (STR), a lightweight method designed to preserve safety properties during fine-tuning. Our approach identifies salient tokens from rejection templates of well-aligned models and constrains their associated logits during training, preventing the loss of critical safety behaviors. Unlike reinforcement learning or preference optimization methods, STR requires minimal additional computation and seamlessly integrates with parameter-efficient fine-tuning techniques such as LoRA. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate that our approach achieves safety performance on par with state-of-the-art methods, while preserving task-specific utility and requiring minimal implementation overhead. Furthermore, we show that safety token regularization enhances training stability and overall performance beyond safety considerations alone. This work offers a practical and readily deployable strategy for continual safety alignment in fine-tuned LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Logit空间护栏：面向大语言模型对齐的安全令牌正则化
即使在良性数据集上对新领域进行微调，也常导致已对齐大语言模型的安全对齐性能下降。现有安全对齐技术主要集中于预训练阶段，使微调模型易受行为偏移影响。本研究提出安全令牌正则化（STR），一种轻量级方法，旨在微调过程中保持安全属性。该方法从已对齐模型的拒绝模板中识别显著令牌，并在训练期间约束其关联logit值，从而防止关键安全行为丢失。与强化学习或偏好优化方法不同，STR仅需极少额外计算量，并可无缝集成LoRA等参数高效微调技术。综合实验表明，本方法在安全性能上达到与前沿方法相当的水平，同时保持任务特定效用且实现开销极低。此外，安全令牌正则化还能提升训练稳定性及超越安全考量的整体性能。本研究为微调大语言模型的持续安全对齐提供了实用且易部署的策略。

What If Consensus Lies? Selective-Complementary Reinforcement Learning at Test Time
Authors: Dong Yan, Jian Liang, Yanbo Wang, Shuo Lu, Ran He, Tieniu Tan
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-03-20T11:47:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T02:15:51+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Test-Time Reinforcement Learning (TTRL) enables Large Language Models (LLMs) to enhance reasoning capabilities on unlabeled test streams by deriving pseudo-rewards from majority voting consensus. However, existing TTRL methods rely exclusively on positive pseudo-labeling strategies. Such reliance becomes vulnerable under challenging scenarios where answer distributions are highly dispersed, resulting in weak consensus that inadvertently reinforces incorrect trajectories as supervision signals. In this paper, we propose SCRL (Selective-Complementary Reinforcement Learning), a robust test-time reinforcement learning framework that effectively mitigates label noise amplification. SCRL develops Selective Positive Pseudo-Labeling, which enforces strict consensus criteria to filter unreliable majorities. Complementarily, SCRL introduces Entropy-Gated Negative Pseudo-Labeling, the first negative supervision mechanism in TTRL, to reliably prune incorrect trajectories based on generation uncertainty. Extensive experiments on multiple reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that SCRL achieves substantial improvements over baselines, while maintaining robust generalization and training stability under constrained rollout budgets. Our code is available at https://github.com/Jasper-Yan/SCRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：若共识存疑？测试时选择性互补强化学习
测试时强化学习（TTRL）使大语言模型（LLM）能够通过多数投票共识推导伪奖励，从而增强对未标注测试流的推理能力。然而，现有TTRL方法仅依赖正向伪标注策略。当答案分布高度分散、共识薄弱时，这种依赖在挑战性场景下变得脆弱，可能无意中将错误轨迹作为监督信号进行强化。本文提出SCRL（选择性互补强化学习），一种鲁棒的测试时强化学习框架，能有效缓解标签噪声放大问题。SCRL开发了选择性正向伪标注，通过严格共识标准过滤不可靠的多数结果；互补性地引入熵门控负向伪标注——这是TTRL领域首个负向监督机制，能基于生成不确定性可靠地剪除错误轨迹。在多个推理基准上的大量实验表明，SCRL较基线方法取得显著提升，同时在受限推演预算下保持鲁棒的泛化能力和训练稳定性。代码已开源：https://github.com/Jasper-Yan/SCRL。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the vulnerability of existing Test-Time Reinforcement Learning (TTRL) methods, which rely on positive pseudo-labeling from majority voting and can amplify errors when answer distributions are dispersed and consensus is weak. The proposed solution, Selective-Complementary Reinforcement Learning (SCRL), introduces a dual strategy: Selective Positive Pseudo-Labeling applies strict consensus criteria to filter unreliable majorities, while Entropy-Gated Negative Pseudo-Labeling, a novel negative supervision mechanism, prunes incorrect trajectories based on generation uncertainty. Experimental results on multiple reasoning benchmarks show that SCRL achieves substantial performance improvements over baselines, demonstrating robust generalization and training stability even with limited rollout budgets.
本文针对现有测试时强化学习方法依赖多数投票进行正伪标注的脆弱性提出改进，该方法在答案分布分散、共识较弱时容易放大错误标签。提出的选择性互补强化学习框架采用双重策略：选择性正伪标注通过严格共识标准过滤不可靠的多数答案，而熵门控负伪标注作为首个负监督机制，基于生成不确定性修剪错误轨迹。在多个推理基准上的实验表明，该方法相比基线取得了显著性能提升，并在有限计算预算下保持了鲁棒的泛化能力和训练稳定性。
Do LLM-derived graph priors improve multi-agent coordination?
Authors: Nikunj Gupta, Rajgopal Kannan, Viktor Prasanna
First: 2026-04-19T01:40:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-19T01:40:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) is crucial for AI systems that operate collaboratively in distributed and adversarial settings, particularly in multi-domain operations (MDO). A central challenge in cooperative MARL is determining how agents should coordinate: existing approaches must either hand-specify graph topology, rely on proximity-based heuristics, or learn structure entirely from environment interaction; all of which are brittle, semantically uninformed, or data-intensive. We investigate whether large language models (LLMs) can generate useful coordination graph priors for MARL by using minimal natural language descriptions of agent observations to infer latent coordination patterns. These priors are integrated into MARL algorithms via graph convolutional layers within a graph neural network (GNN)-based pipeline, and evaluated on four cooperative scenarios from the Multi-Agent Particle Environment (MPE) benchmark against baselines spanning the full spectrum of coordination modeling, from independent learners to state-of-the-art graph-based methods. We further ablate across five compact open-source LLMs to assess the sensitivity of prior quality to model choice. Our results provide the first quantitative evidence that LLM-derived graph priors can enhance coordination and adaptability in dynamic multi-agent environments, and demonstrate that models as small as 1.5B parameters are sufficient for effective prior generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LLM衍生的图先验能否提升多智能体协同能力？
多智能体强化学习（MARL）对分布式对抗环境下协同运作的AI系统至关重要，尤其适用于多域作战（MDO）。合作型MARL的核心挑战在于确定智能体间的协同机制：现有方法需手动指定图拓扑、依赖基于邻近度的启发式规则，或完全从环境交互中学习结构；这些方法均存在脆弱性、语义信息缺失或数据依赖性强的问题。本研究通过智能体观测的极简自然语言描述推断潜在协同模式，探索大型语言模型（LLM）能否为MARL生成有效的协同图先验。这些先验通过图神经网络（GNN）流程中的图卷积层集成至MARL算法，并在多智能体粒子环境（MPE）基准的四个合作场景中，与涵盖从独立学习到前沿图基方法的全谱系协同建模基线进行对比评估。我们进一步对五种紧凑型开源LLM进行消融实验，以评估先验质量对模型选择的敏感性。研究结果首次提供量化证据：LLM衍生的图先验能增强动态多智能体环境中的协同性与适应性，并证明仅需15亿参数规模的模型即可实现有效的先验生成。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether large language models (LLMs) can generate useful coordination graph priors to address the challenge of brittle, uninformed, or data-intensive coordination in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL). The method involves using minimal natural language descriptions of agent observations to prompt LLMs to infer latent coordination patterns, which are then integrated into MARL algorithms via graph convolutional layers within a graph neural network (GNN)-based pipeline. Experimental results on four cooperative scenarios from the Multi-Agent Particle Environment benchmark show that LLM-derived priors enhance coordination and adaptability compared to a range of baselines, and further ablation studies demonstrate that even compact LLMs with as few as 1.5B parameters are sufficient for effective prior generation.
本文研究大型语言模型（LLM）能否生成有用的协调图先验，以解决多智能体强化学习（MARL）中协调机制脆弱、缺乏语义信息或数据需求大的核心挑战。其方法是通过智能体观测的最小化自然语言描述来提示LLM推断潜在的协调模式，并将这些先验通过图神经网络（GNN）流程中的图卷积层集成到MARL算法中。在Multi-Agent Particle Environment基准的四个合作场景上的实验结果表明，与一系列基线方法相比，LLM衍生的先验能提升协调能力和动态环境适应性，进一步的消融实验证明，即使是参数量小至15亿的紧凑型LLM也足以生成有效的先验。
DR-SAC: Distributionally Robust Soft Actor-Critic for Reinforcement Learning under Uncertainty
Authors: Mingxuan Cui, Duo Zhou, Yuxuan Han, Grani A. Hanasusanto, Qiong Wang, Huan Zhang, Zhengyuan Zhou
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-14T20:36:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-18T21:54:34+00:00
Comments: 31 Pages. Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Deep reinforcement learning (RL) has achieved remarkable success, yet its deployment in real-world scenarios is often limited by vulnerability to environmental uncertainties. Distributionally robust RL (DR-RL) algorithms have been proposed to resolve this challenge, but existing approaches are largely restricted to value-based methods in tabular settings. In this work, we introduce Distributionally Robust Soft Actor-Critic (DR-SAC), the first actor-critic based DR-RL algorithm for offline learning in continuous action spaces. DR-SAC maximizes the entropy-regularized rewards against the worst possible transition models within an KL-divergence constrained uncertainty set. We derive the distributionally robust version of the soft policy iteration with a convergence guarantee and incorporate a generative modeling approach to estimate the unknown nominal transition models. Experiment results on five continuous RL tasks demonstrate our algorithm achieves up to 9.8 times higher average reward than the SAC baseline under common perturbations. Additionally, DR-SAC significantly improves computing efficiency and applicability to large-scale problems compared with existing DR-RL algorithms. Code is publicly available at github.com/Lemutisme/DR-SAC.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DR-SAC：不确定性下强化学习的分布鲁棒软演员-评论家算法
深度强化学习（RL）已取得显著成功，但其在实际场景中的应用常因对环境不确定性的脆弱性而受限。分布鲁棒强化学习（DR-RL）算法被提出以应对这一挑战，但现有方法主要局限于表格设定下的基于价值的方法。本研究提出分布鲁棒软演员-评论家（DR-SAC），这是首个基于演员-评论家框架的DR-RL算法，适用于连续动作空间的离线学习。DR-SAC在KL散度约束的不确定性集合内，针对最坏可能的转移模型最大化熵正则化奖励。我们推导出具有收敛保证的软策略迭代的分布鲁棒版本，并采用生成建模方法估计未知的名义转移模型。在五个连续RL任务上的实验结果表明，该算法在常见扰动下的平均奖励比SAC基线最高提升9.8倍。此外，与现有DR-RL算法相比，DR-SAC显著提升了计算效率及对大规模问题的适用性。代码公开于github.com/Lemutisme/DR-SAC。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the vulnerability of deep reinforcement learning to environmental uncertainties in real-world deployment, this paper introduces DR-SAC, a distributionally robust actor-critic algorithm for offline learning in continuous action spaces. The method maximizes entropy-regularized rewards against the worst-case transition models within a KL-divergence constrained uncertainty set, deriving a robust soft policy iteration with convergence guarantees and using generative modeling to estimate nominal transitions. Experimental results on five continuous control tasks show DR-SAC achieves up to 9.8 times higher average reward than the SAC baseline under perturbations while improving computational efficiency and scalability over prior distributionally robust RL methods.
本文针对深度强化学习在现实部署中易受环境不确定性影响的局限性，提出了DR-SAC，一种用于连续动作空间离线学习的分布鲁棒演员-评论家算法。该方法在KL散度约束的不确定性集合内最大化熵正则化奖励以对抗最坏情况转移模型，推导出具有收敛保证的鲁棒软策略迭代，并利用生成建模估计名义转移。在五个连续控制任务上的实验结果表明，在常见扰动下，DR-SAC相比SAC基线实现了高达9.8倍的平均奖励提升，同时较现有分布鲁棒强化学习方法显著提高了计算效率与可扩展性。
Multimodal Reinforcement Learning with Adaptive Verifier for AI Agents
Authors: Reuben Tan, Baolin Peng, Zhengyuan Yang, Hao Cheng, Oier Mees, Theodore Zhao, Andrea Tupini, Isar Meijier, Qianhui Wu, Yuncong Yang, Lars Liden, Yu Gu, Sheng Zhang, Xiaodong Liu, Lijuan Wang, Marc Pollefeys, Yong Jae Lee, Jianfeng Gao
First: 2025-12-03T04:42:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-18T20:34:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic reasoning models trained with multimodal reinforcement learning (MMRL) have become increasingly capable, yet they are almost universally optimized using sparse, outcome-based rewards computed based on the final answers. Richer rewards computed from the reasoning tokens can improve learning significantly by providing more fine-grained guidance. However, it is challenging to compute more informative rewards in MMRL beyond those based on outcomes since different samples may require different scoring functions and teacher models may provide noisy reward signals too. In this paper, we introduce the Argos (Agentic Reward for Grounded & Objective Scoring), a principled reward agent to train multimodal reasoning models for agentic tasks. For each sample, Argos selects from a pool of teacher-model derived and rule-based scoring functions to simultaneously evaluate: (i) final response accuracy, (ii) spatiotemporal localization of referred entities and actions, and (iii) the quality of the reasoning process. We find that by leveraging our agentic verifier across both SFT data curation and RL training, our model achieves state-of-the-art results across multiple agentic tasks such as spatial reasoning, visual hallucination as well as robotics and embodied AI benchmarks. Critically, we demonstrate that just relying on SFT post-training on highly curated reasoning data is insufficient, as agents invariably collapse to ungrounded solutions during RL without our online verification. We also show that our agentic verifier can help to reduce reward-hacking in MMRL. Finally, we also provide a theoretical justification for the effectiveness of Argos through the concept of pareto-optimality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于自适应验证器的多模态强化学习AI智能体
通过多模态强化学习（MMRL）训练的智能体推理模型能力日益增强，但当前普遍采用基于最终答案的稀疏结果奖励进行优化。若从推理过程标记中计算更丰富的奖励，可通过细粒度指导显著提升学习效果。然而，在MMRL中超越结果奖励计算更具信息量的奖励面临挑战：不同样本可能需要不同的评分函数，且教师模型可能提供带噪声的奖励信号。本文提出Argos（面向具身与客观评分的智能体奖励），这是一种用于训练多模态智能体任务推理模型的原则性奖励智能体。针对每个样本，Argos从教师模型衍生和基于规则的评分函数池中动态选择，同步评估：（i）最终响应准确性；（ii）所指实体与动作的时空定位；（iii）推理过程质量。实验表明，通过在监督微调数据筛选和强化学习训练中部署该智能体验证器，我们的模型在空间推理、视觉幻觉以及机器人学与具身AI基准测试等多项智能体任务中取得最优结果。关键发现是，仅依赖对高质推理数据进行监督微调后训练是不够的——若无在线验证，智能体在强化学习中必然退化为无实体依据的解决方案。研究还证明该验证器有助于减少MMRL中的奖励破解行为。最后，我们通过帕累托最优性理论为Argos的有效性提供了理论依据。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of providing fine-grained, informative rewards in multimodal reinforcement learning (MMRL) for agentic reasoning, where traditional sparse, outcome-based rewards are insufficient. The authors propose Argos, an adaptive verifier that dynamically selects from a pool of teacher-model and rule-based scoring functions to evaluate final answer accuracy, spatiotemporal localization, and reasoning process quality per sample. Experimental results show that integrating Argos into both supervised fine-tuning data curation and RL training yields state-of-the-art performance on spatial reasoning, visual hallucination, robotics, and embodied AI benchmarks, prevents agents from collapsing to ungrounded solutions during RL, and mitigates reward hacking, with theoretical support via pareto-optimality.
本文针对多模态强化学习中智能体推理任务面临的挑战，即传统稀疏的、基于最终结果的奖励信号不足，提出了一种自适应验证器Argos，用于提供更细粒度的指导。该方法为每个样本从一组教师模型和基于规则的评分函数中动态选择，以同时评估最终答案准确性、所指实体和动作的时空定位以及推理过程质量。实验结果表明，将Argos集成到监督微调数据整理和强化学习训练中，在空间推理、视觉幻觉、机器人学和具身人工智能等多个基准上取得了最先进的性能，防止了智能体在强化学习中崩溃为无根据的解决方案，并减少了奖励黑客行为，其有效性通过帕累托最优性得到了理论支持。
